asgi.py
"""
ASGI config for nlmk_sim project.

It exposes the ASGI callable as a module-level variable named ``application``.

For more information on this file, see
https://docs.djangoproject.com/en/5.2/howto/deployment/asgi/
"""

import os

from django.core.asgi import get_asgi_application

os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'nlmk_sim.settings')

application = get_asgi_application()




celery.py
import os
from celery import Celery

os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'nlmk_sim.settings')

app = Celery('nlmk_sim')

app.config_from_object('django.conf:settings', namespace='CELERY')

app.autodiscover_tasks()

@app.task(bind=True)
def debug_task(self):
    print(f'Request: {self.request!r}')

                    <td>{{ order.required_weight|default:0 }}</td>
                    <td>{{ order.get_progress|default:"—" }}%</td>
                    <td>—</td>
                    <td>—</td>
                    <td>—</td>
                    <td>
                        {% if order.is_completed %}
                            <span class="badge badge-success">Выполнен</span>
                        {% else %}
                            <span class="badge badge-warning">В работе</span>
                        {% endif %}
                    </td>
                </tr>
                {% empty %}
                <tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center; padding:80px; color: var(--gray);">
                    Нет активных заказов
                </td></tr>
                {% endfor %}
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

</div>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

    // Динамика выпуска
    const outputCtx = document.getElementById('outputChart');
    if (outputCtx && outputCtx.dataset.labels) {
        new Chart(outputCtx, {
            type: 'bar',
            data: {
                labels: JSON.parse(outputCtx.dataset.labels),
                datasets: [{ 
                    label: 'Выпуск', 
                    data: JSON.parse(outputCtx.dataset.values), 
                    backgroundColor: '#3b6796', 
                    borderRadius: 4 
                }]
            },
            options: { 
                responsive: true, 
                scales: { y: { beginAtZero: true } }, 
                plugins: { legend: { display: false }} 
            }
        });
    }

    // Структура брака
    const scrapCtx = document.getElementById('scrapChart');
    if (scrapCtx) {
        const success = parseFloat(scrapCtx.dataset.success) || 75;
        const defect = parseFloat(scrapCtx.dataset.defect) || 25;
        new Chart(scrapCtx, {
            type: 'doughnut',
            data: { 
                labels: ['Годная продукция', 'Брак'], 
                datasets: [{ data: [success, defect], backgroundColor: ['#2e7d32', '#c62828'] }] 
            },
            options: { 
                cutout: '68%', 
                responsive: true, 
                plugins: { legend: { position: 'bottom' } }
            }
        });
    }

    // MAPE — исправленная версия
    const mapeCtx = document.getElementById('mapeChart');
    if (mapeCtx && mapeCtx.dataset.labels) {
        let values = JSON.parse(mapeCtx.dataset.values || '[]');
        // Ограничиваем значения для нормального отображения
        values = values.map(v => Math.min(Math.max(v, 0), 30));

        new Chart(mapeCtx, {
            type: 'line',
            data: {
                labels: JSON.parse(mapeCtx.dataset.labels),
                datasets: [{ 
                    label: 'MAPE (%)', 
                    data: values, 
                    borderColor: '#c62828', 
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(198, 40, 40, 0.08)',
                    tension: 0.35,
                    fill: true,
                    borderWidth: 3,
                    pointRadius: 4
                }]
            },
            options: { 
                responsive: true, 
                scales: { 
                    y: { 
                        beginAtZero: true, 
                        max: 35,
                        ticks: { stepSize: 5 }
                    } 
                }
            }
        });
    }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<!-- GOST TOOLTIP ELEMENT -->
<div id="gostTooltip" class="gost-tooltip"></div>

<script>
// === GOST TOOLTIP FUNCTIONS ===
function showGostTooltip(event, paramType, data) {
    const tooltip = document.getElementById('gostTooltip');
    let content = '';
    
    // GOST requirements database
    const gostStandards = {
        '2412': {
            name: '2412 (NGO)',
            thickness: { min: 0.23, max: 0.50 },
            si: { min: 2.7, max: 3.4 },
            c: { max: 0.006 },
            p15_50: { max: 2.40 },
            b2500: { min: 1.70 },
            p10_400: { max: 13.5 },
            b5000: { min: 1.66 },
            b10000: { min: 1.56 },
            anisotropy: { max: 5.5 }
        },
        '2413': {
            name: '2413 (NGO)',
            thickness: { min: 0.27, max: 0.50 },
            si: { min: 2.5, max: 3.3 },
            c: { max: 0.008 },
            p15_50: { max: 2.80 },
            b2500: { min: 1.66 },
            p10_400: { max: 15.0 },
            b5000: { min: 1.62 },
            b10000: { min: 1.52 },
            anisotropy: { max: 6.5 }
        },
        '3408': {
            name: '3408 (GO)',
            thickness: { min: 0.23, max: 0.30 },
            si: { min: 3.0, max: 3.6 },
            c: { max: 0.004 },
            p15_50: { max: 1.20 },
            b2500: { min: 1.90 },
            p10_400: { max: 8.0 },
            b5000: { min: 1.95 },
            b10000: { min: 1.88 },
            anisotropy: { max: 2.0 }
        }
    };
    
    // Determine grade from data
    const grade = data.grade || '2412';
    const standard = gostStandards[grade] || gostStandards['2412'];
    
    if (paramType === 'thickness') {
        const value = parseFloat(data);
        const min = standard.thickness.min;
        const max = standard.thickness.max;
        const ok = value >= min && value <= max;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Толщина:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(2)} мм</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Допустимый диапазон:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${min} – ${max} мм</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, таблица 1</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'si') {
        const value = parseFloat(data);
        const min = standard.si.min;
        const max = standard.si.max;
        const ok = value >= min && value <= max;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Содержание Si:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(2)} %</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Допустимый диапазон:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${min} – ${max} %</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, химический состав</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'c') {
        const value = parseFloat(data);
        const max = standard.c.max;
        const ok = value <= max;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Содержание C:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(4)} %</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Максимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≤ ${max} %</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, углерод</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'p15_50') {
        const value = parseFloat(data.value);
        const max = standard.p15_50.max;
        const ok = value <= max;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">P1.5/50:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(3)} Вт/кг</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Максимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≤ ${max} Вт/кг</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, магнитные потери</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'b2500') {
        const value = parseFloat(data.value);
        const min = standard.b2500.min;
        const ok = value >= min;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">B2500:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(3)} Тл</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Минимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≥ ${min} Тл</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, магнитная индукция</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'p10_400') {
        const value = parseFloat(data.value);
        const max = standard.p10_400.max;
        const ok = value <= max;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования IEC 60404</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">P1.0/400:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(2)} Вт/кг</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Максимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≤ ${max} Вт/кг</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">IEC 60404-8-4, высокочастотные потери</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'b5000') {
        const value = parseFloat(data.value);
        const min = standard.b5000.min;
        const ok = value >= min;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования IEC 60404</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">B5000:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(3)} Тл</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Минимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≥ ${min} Тл</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">IEC 60404-8-4, индукция при 5000 А/м</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'b10000') {
        const value = parseFloat(data.value);
        const min = standard.b10000.min;
        const ok = value >= min;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования IEC 60404</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">B10000:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(3)} Тл</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Минимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≥ ${min} Тл</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">IEC 60404-8-4, индукция при 10000 А/м</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'anisotropy') {
        const value = parseFloat(data.value);
        const max = standard.anisotropy.max;
        const ok = value <= max;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Анизотропия:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${value.toFixed(1)} %</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${ok ? '✓ В норме' : '✗ Отклонение'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">Максимум:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">≤ ${max} %</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, анизотропия свойств</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'gost_full') {
        const p15 = parseFloat(data.p15);
        const b2500 = parseFloat(data.b2500);
        const p15ok = p15 <= standard.p15_50.max;
        const b2500ok = b2500 >= standard.b2500.min;
        const overall = p15ok && b2500ok;
        
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Полная проверка по ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">Марка: ${standard.name}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">P1.5/50:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${p15.toFixed(3)} Вт/кг</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${p15ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${p15ok ? '✓ ≤' + standard.p15_50.max : '✗ >' + standard.p15_50.max}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">B2500:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${b2500.toFixed(3)} Тл</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${b2500ok ? 'ok' : 'fail'}">${b2500ok ? '✓ ≥' + standard.b2500.min : '✗ <' + standard.b2500.min}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row" style="margin-top: 10px; padding-top: 10px; border-top: 2px solid #eee; font-weight: 700;">
                <span class="gost-param-name">ОБЩИЙ ВЕРДИКТ:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ${overall ? 'ok' : 'fail'}" style="font-size: 12px; padding: 5px 15px;">${overall ? 'СООТВЕТСТВУЕТ' : 'НЕ СООТВЕТСТВУЕТ'}</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, основные требования</div>
        `;
    }
    else if (paramType === 'h2' || paramType === 'n2') {
        content = `
            <div class="gost-tooltip-header">Требования к защитной атмосфере</div>
            <div class="gost-tooltip-grade">
                <div class="gost-tooltip-grade-title">ГОСТ 21427.2-83</div>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-param-row">
                <span class="gost-param-name">${paramType === 'h2' ? 'H₂' : 'N₂'}:</span>
                <span class="gost-param-value">${parseFloat(data).toFixed(4)} %</span>
                <span class="gost-param-status ok">✓ Норма</span>
            </div>
            <div class="gost-standard-ref">Защитная атмосфера отжига</div>
        `;
    }
    
    tooltip.innerHTML = content;
    tooltip.style.display = 'block';
    
    // Position tooltip
    const rect = event.target.getBoundingClientRect();
    let top = rect.bottom + window.scrollY + 10;
    let left = rect.left + window.scrollX;
    
    // Adjust if tooltip goes off screen
    const tooltipRect = tooltip.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (left + tooltipRect.width > window.innerWidth) {
        left = window.innerWidth - tooltipRect.width - 20;
    }
    if (top + tooltipRect.height > window.innerHeight + window.scrollY) {
        top = rect.top + window.scrollY - tooltipRect.height - 10;
    }
    
    tooltip.style.top = top + 'px';
    tooltip.style.left = left + 'px';
}

function hideGostTooltip() {
    const tooltip = document.getElementById('gostTooltip');
    tooltip.style.display = 'none';
}

// === TAB SWITCHING ===
function switchTab(tabName) {
    // Скрываем все вкладки
    const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');
    contents.forEach(el => el.style.display = 'none');
    
    // Сбрасываем кнопки
    const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('[id^="tab-btn-"]');
    buttons.forEach(btn => {
        btn.style.background = '#eee';
        btn.style.color = '#333';
    });
    
    // Показываем выбранную вкладку
    document.getElementById('tab-' + tabName).style.display = 'block';
    
    // Подсвечиваем активную кнопку
    const activeBtn = document.getElementById('tab-btn-' + tabName);
    activeBtn.style.background = 'var(--primary)';
    activeBtn.style.color = 'white';
}

// === INPUT SOURCE TOGGLE ===
function toggleInputSource() {
    const source = document.getElementById('roll_source').value;
    document.getElementById('db_select_group').style.display = (source === 'db') ? 'block' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('manual_input_group').style.display = (source === 'manual') ? 'block' : 'none';
}

// === GRADE FILTERS ===
function setupGradeFilters() {
    const filterBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.grade-filter-btn');
    const gradeCards = document.querySelectorAll('.grade-card');
    
    filterBtns.forEach(btn => {
        btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            // Update active button
            filterBtns.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
            this.classList.add('active');
            
            const filter = this.dataset.filter;
            
            // Filter cards
            gradeCards.forEach(card => {
                const type = card.dataset.type;
                const standard = card.dataset.standard;
                
                if (filter === 'all') {
                    card.style.display = 'block';
                } else if (filter === 'NGO' || filter === 'GO') {
                    card.style.display = (type === filter) ? 'block' : 'none';
                } else if (filter === 'gost' || filter === 'iec') {
                    card.style.display = (standard === filter) ? 'block' : 'none';
                }
            });
        });
    });
}

// === BATCH SELECTION LOGIC ===
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    switchTab('setup');
    toggleInputSource();
    setupGradeFilters(); // Initialize grade filters
    
    if (document.getElementById('monte_carlo')?.checked) {
        document.getElementById('monte_carlo_options').style.display = 'block';
    }
    document.getElementById('monte_carlo').addEventListener('change', function() {
        document.getElementById('monte_carlo_options').style.display = this.checked ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
    
    const selectAll = document.getElementById('select-all');
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.roll-checkbox');
    const countSpan = document.getElementById('selected-count');
    const batchCountSpan = document.getElementById('batch-count');
    const batchBtn = document.getElementById('batch-run-btn');
    const singleBtn = document.getElementById('single-run-btn');
    const form = document.getElementById('simulation-form');
    const rollSourceSelect = document.getElementById('roll_source');
    
    function updateUI() {
        const isDbMode = rollSourceSelect.value === 'db';
        checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.disabled = !isDbMode);
        selectAll.disabled = !isDbMode || checkboxes.length === 0;
        if (!isDbMode) {
            checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
            countSpan.textContent = "(Ручной ввод активен)";
            batchCountSpan.textContent = "0";
            batchBtn.disabled = true;
            singleBtn.disabled = true;
            return;
        }
        const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.roll-checkbox:checked');
        const count = checked.length;
        countSpan.textContent = `(${count} выбрано)`;
        batchCountSpan.textContent = count;
        batchBtn.disabled = count < 2;
        singleBtn.disabled = count !== 1;
        selectAll.checked = checkboxes.length > 0 && count === checkboxes.length;
    }
    
    selectAll.addEventListener('change', function() {
        checkboxes.forEach(cb => { if (!cb.disabled) cb.checked = this.checked; });
        updateUI();
    });
    checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.addEventListener('change', updateUI));
    rollSourceSelect.addEventListener('change', updateUI);
    updateUI();
    
    // Batch simulation
    batchBtn.addEventListener('click', async function() {
        const formData = new FormData(form);
        formData.delete('roll_ids');
        formData.delete('roll_id');
        const selectedIds = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.roll-checkbox:checked')).map(cb => cb.value);
        selectedIds.forEach(id => formData.append('roll_ids', id));
        formData.append('batch_mode', 'true');
        batchBtn.textContent = '⏳ Отправка...';
        batchBtn.disabled = true;
        try {
            const csrfToken = form.querySelector('[name=csrfmiddlewaretoken]').value;
            const response = await fetch('', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'X-CSRFToken': csrfToken },
                body: formData
            });
            if (response.ok) {
                document.getElementById('batch-progress-section').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('session-id').textContent = 'запущена...';
                switchTab('batch');
                startSessionPolling();
                alert('Парная симуляция запущена. Прогресс отображается выше.');
            } else {
                const errText = await response.text();
                alert(' Ошибка: ' + errText.substring(0, 200));
                batchBtn.textContent = `Парная симуляция (${selectedIds.length})`;
                batchBtn.disabled = false;
            }
        } catch (e) {
            alert('Ошибка сети: ' + e.message);
            batchBtn.textContent = `Парная симуляция (${selectedIds.length})`;
            batchBtn.disabled = false;
        }
    });
    
    // Form submit
    form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
        const isDbMode = rollSourceSelect.value === 'db';
        if (isDbMode) {
            const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.roll-checkbox:checked');
            if (checked.length !== 1) {
                e.preventDefault();
                alert('Для одиночного расчёта выберите ровно 1 рулон.');
                return false;
            }
            document.getElementById('single-roll-id').value = checked[0].value;
        }
    });
    
    // === INTERACTIVE SIMULATION POLLING ===
    let simulationInterval = null;
    
    async function startInteractiveSimulation(rollId, modeId) {
        document.getElementById('tab-results').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('simulation-progress-section').style.display = 'block';
        
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/start-simulation/', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'X-CSRFToken': getCsrfToken()
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({ roll_id: rollId, mode_id: modeId })
            });
            
            const data = await response.json();
            const sessionId = data.session_id;
            
            simulationInterval = setInterval(() => {
                checkSimulationProgress(sessionId);
            }, 1000);
            
        } catch (error) {
            alert('Ошибка запуска симуляции: ' + error);
            document.getElementById('simulation-progress-section').style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
    
    async function checkSimulationProgress(sessionId) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`/api/simulation-progress/${sessionId}/`);
            const data = await response.json();
            
            const progressBar = document.getElementById('progress-bar');
            progressBar.style.width = data.progress + '%';
            progressBar.textContent = data.progress + '%';
            
            if (data.current_step) {
                document.getElementById('step-stage').textContent = data.current_step.stage || '-';
                document.getElementById('step-hour').textContent = data.current_step.hour || '-';
                document.getElementById('step-temp').textContent = (data.current_step.temp || '-') + '°C';
                document.getElementById('live-p15').textContent = (data.current_step.p15_50 || '-') + ' Вт/кг';
                document.getElementById('live-b2500').textContent = (data.current_step.b2500 || '-') + ' Тл';
                
                const statusEl = document.getElementById('live-status');
                statusEl.textContent = data.current_step.status || '-';
                statusEl.style.color = data.current_step.status === 'БРАК' ? '#e74c3c' : '#27ae60';
            }
            
            if (data.status === 'completed') {
                clearInterval(simulationInterval);
                setTimeout(() => {
                    loadSimulationResults(data.result.simulation_result_id);
                }, 1000);
            } else if (data.status === 'failed') {
                clearInterval(simulationInterval);
                alert('Ошибка симуляции: ' + data.error);
                document.getElementById('simulation-progress-section').style.display = 'none';
            }
            
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Ошибка получения прогресса:', error);
        }
    }
    
    function loadSimulationResults(resultId) {
        window.location.href = `/simulation-result/${resultId}/`;
    }
    
    function getCsrfToken() {
        return document.querySelector('[name=csrfmiddlewaretoken]').value;
    }
    
    // === BATCH POLLING ===
    let pollingInterval = null;
    function startSessionPolling() {
        if (pollingInterval) clearInterval(pollingInterval);
        pollingInterval = setInterval(async () => {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/sessions/active/', {
                    method: 'GET',
                    headers: { 'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest' }
                });
                if (!response.ok) { updateProgressPlaceholder(); return; }
                const data = await response.json();
                if (data.session && data.session.status !== 'idle') {
                    updateProgressUI(data.session);
                    if (data.session.status === 'completed' || data.session.status === 'failed') {
                        stopPolling();
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            alert('Симуляция завершена! Обновляю...');
                            window.location.reload();
                        }, 1500);
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) { updateProgressPlaceholder(); }
        }, 3000);
    }
    function stopPolling() { if (pollingInterval) { clearInterval(pollingInterval); pollingInterval = null; } }
    function updateProgressUI(session) {
        document.getElementById('session-id').textContent = session.id;
        document.getElementById('processed-count').textContent = session.processed_rolls || 0;
        document.getElementById('total-count').textContent = session.total_rolls || 0;
        const percent = session.total_rolls > 0 ? Math.round((session.processed_rolls / session.total_rolls) * 100) : 0;
        const fill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
        fill.style.width = percent + '%';
        fill.textContent = percent + '%';
        fill.className = 'progress-bar-fill';
        if (session.status === 'completed') fill.classList.add('completed');
        else if (session.status === 'failed') fill.classList.add('failed');
        else fill.classList.add('processing');
        updateRollsList(session.rolls || []);
    }
    function updateRollsList(rolls) {
        const list = document.getElementById('rolls-progress-list');
        if (!rolls || rolls.length === 0) {
            list.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:14px; color:#666; text-align:center;">Ожидание...</div>';
            return;
        }
        list.innerHTML = rolls.map(roll => {
            let statusClass = 'status-pending', statusText = 'Ожидание';
            if (['На проверке','В обработке (пакет)'].includes(roll.status)) { statusClass = 'status-processing'; statusText = 'В работе'; }
            else if (roll.status === 'Обработан') { statusClass = 'status-done'; statusText = 'Годен'; }
            else if (roll.status === 'Брак') { statusClass = 'status-defect'; statusText = 'Брак'; }
            else if (roll.status === 'Ошибка') { statusClass = 'status-error'; statusText = 'Ошибка'; }
            return `<div class="roll-item"><span class="roll-number">#${roll.number}</span><span class="roll-status ${statusClass}">${statusText}</span></div>`;
        }).join('');
    }
    function updateProgressPlaceholder() {
        const fill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
        if (fill.classList.contains('processing')) {
            const current = parseInt(fill.textContent) || 0;
            const next = Math.min(current + Math.random() * 15, 95);
            fill.style.width = next.toFixed(0) + '%';
            fill.textContent = next.toFixed(0) + '%';
        }
    }
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', stopPolling);
});

// === ACCORDION ===
function toggleAccordion(id) {
    const header = event.currentTarget;
    const content = document.getElementById(id);
    header.classList.toggle('active');
    content.classList.toggle('active');
}

// === ROLL DETAILS ===
function showRollDetails(rollId) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.roll-details').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
    if (rollId) {
        const details = document.getElementById('roll-details-' + rollId);
        if (details) {
            details.classList.add('active');
            details.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
        }
    }
}
function showAllRolls() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.roll-details').forEach(el => el.classList.add('active'));
    document.getElementById('batch-roll-select').value = '';
}
function closeBatchResults() {
    document.getElementById('batch-results-section').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('batch-accordion').classList.remove('active');
    document.querySelector('.accordion-header').classList.remove('active');
}

// === ACTIONS ===
function downloadPassport(btn) {
    const rollId = btn.getAttribute('data-roll-id');
    if (!rollId) { alert('ID рулона не указан'); return; }
    window.open('/passport/' + rollId + '/', '_blank');
}
function copyRollData(btn) {
    const rollId = btn.getAttribute('data-roll-id');
    if (!rollId) { alert('ID рулона не указан'); return; }
    const details = document.getElementById('roll-details-' + rollId);
    if (!details) return;
    const text = `Рулон #${rollId}\n` +
    Array.from(details.querySelectorAll('.param-row')).map(r =>
        `${r.querySelector('.label').textContent}: ${r.querySelector('.value').textContent}`
    ).join('\n');
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => alert('Данные скопированы!'));
}
function exportBatchResults() {
    const rows = [['Рулон','Марка','Статус','P1.5/50','B2500','Вес','Дефект']];
    document.querySelectorAll('.roll-details').forEach(details => {
        const rollId = details.id.replace('roll-details-','');
        const gradeEl = details.querySelector('.alert-success strong');
        const grade = gradeEl ? gradeEl.textContent.replace('Марка присвоена:','').trim() : '—';
        const verdictBox = details.querySelector('.verdict-box');
        const status = verdictBox ? verdictBox.textContent.split('СТАТУС:')[1]?.trim() || '—' : '—';
        const p = details.querySelector('.param-row:nth-child(1) .value')?.textContent || '—';
        const b = details.querySelector('.param-row:nth-child(2) .value')?.textContent || '—';
        const weight = details.querySelector('.param-row:nth-child(4) .value')?.textContent || '—';
        const defect = details.querySelector('.alert-danger') ? 'Да' : 'Нет';
        rows.push([rollId, grade, status, p, b, weight, defect]);
    });
    const csv = rows.map(r => r.join(',')).join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url; a.download = `batch_results_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`;
    a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

<div id="gostTooltip" class="gost-tooltip"></div>

<script>
    const GOST_STANDARDS = {
        '2412': { p15_max: 2.40, b2500_min: 1.70, name: '2412 (NGO)' },
        '2413': { p15_max: 2.80, b2500_min: 1.66, name: '2413 (NGO)' },
        '2414': { p15_max: 3.40, b2500_min: 1.60, name: '2414 (NGO)' },
        '3408': { p15_max: 1.20, b2500_min: 1.90, name: '3408 (GO)' },
        '3411': { p15_max: 1.45, b2500_min: 1.87, name: '3411 (GO)' },
        '3412': { p15_max: 1.65, b2500_min: 1.84, name: '3412 (GO)' },
        'M250-35A': { p15_max: 2.50, b2500_min: 1.63, name: 'M250-35A (IEC)' },
        'M400-50A': { p15_max: 4.00, b2500_min: 1.55, name: 'M400-50A (IEC)' },
    };

    function switchTab(tabName) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.style.display = 'none');
        document.querySelectorAll('.tabs-nav button').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
        document.getElementById('tab-' + tabName).style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('tab-btn-' + tabName).classList.add('active');
    }

    function applyFilters() {
        const grade = document.getElementById('filter-grade').value;
        const thickness = document.getElementById('filter-thickness').value;
        const risk = document.getElementById('filter-risk').value;
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.queue-row').forEach(row => {
            const rowGrade = row.dataset.grade;
            const rowThickness = row.dataset.thickness;
            const rowRisk = row.dataset.risk;
            
            let show = true;
            if (grade && rowGrade !== grade) show = false;
            if (thickness && rowThickness !== thickness) show = false;
            if (risk === 'high' && parseFloat(rowRisk) <= 2.5) show = false;
            if (risk === 'medium' && (parseFloat(rowRisk) <= 2.5 || parseFloat(rowRisk) > 4.5)) show = false;
            if (risk === 'low' && parseFloat(rowRisk) > 2.5) show = false;
            
            row.style.display = show ? '' : 'none';
        });
    }

    function resetFilters() {
        document.getElementById('filter-grade').value = '';
        document.getElementById('filter-thickness').value = '';
        document.getElementById('filter-risk').value = '';
        document.querySelectorAll('.queue-row').forEach(row => row.style.display = '');
    }

    let selectedRows = [];

    function toggleSelectAll() {
        const selectAll = document.getElementById('select-all');
        const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.row-checkbox');
        checkboxes.forEach(cb => cb.checked = selectAll.checked);
        updateBulkActions();
    }

    function updateBulkActions() {
        const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.row-checkbox:checked');
        selectedRows = Array.from(checkboxes).map(cb => cb.value);
        const bulkActions = document.getElementById('bulk-actions');
        const selectedCount = document.getElementById('selected-count');
        if (selectedRows.length > 0) {
            bulkActions.classList.add('active');
            selectedCount.textContent = selectedRows.length;
        } else {
            bulkActions.classList.remove('active');
        }
    }

    function clearSelection() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.row-checkbox').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
        document.getElementById('select-all').checked = false;
        updateBulkActions();
    }

    function bulkApprove() {
        if (selectedRows.length === 0) return;
        if (!confirm('Утвердить ' + selectedRows.length + ' рулонов?')) return;
        alert('Функция массовой обработки в разработке. Для демо: выберите рулоны по одному.');
        clearSelection();
    }

    function bulkReject() {
        if (selectedRows.length === 0) return;
        if (!confirm('Забраковать ' + selectedRows.length + ' рулонов?')) return;
        alert('Функция массовой обработки в разработке. Для демо: выберите рулоны по одному.');
        clearSelection();
    }

    function loadDetails(row, event) {
        if (event && event.target.type === 'checkbox') {
            updateBulkActions();
            return;
        }
        
        const id = row.dataset.id;
        const rollNumber = row.dataset.roll;
        const actualP = row.dataset.p;
        const actualB = row.dataset.b;
        const grade = row.dataset.grade;
        const riskScore = parseFloat(row.dataset.risk || 0);
        const gostOk = row.dataset.gostOk === 'true';

        document.getElementById('details-section').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('current-roll-num').innerText = rollNumber;
        document.getElementById('form-id').value = id;

        document.getElementById('det-p').innerText = actualP ? actualP + " Вт/кг" : "—";
        document.getElementById('det-b').innerText = actualB ? actualB + " Тл" : "—";

        const gost = GOST_STANDARDS[grade] || GOST_STANDARDS['2412'];
        document.getElementById('gost-grade').innerText = gost.name;
        document.getElementById('gost-p-max').innerText = gost.p15_max;
        document.getElementById('gost-b-min').innerText = gost.b2500_min;

        const recommendationEl = document.getElementById('expert-recommendation');
        const recommendationText = document.getElementById('recommendation-text');
        
        if (!gostOk && actualP && parseFloat(actualP) > gost.p15_max) {
            recommendationEl.style.display = 'block';
            recommendationText.innerHTML = 'Повышенные потери при ' + grade + '. Возможная причина: недостаточное обезуглероживание или перегрев при отжиге.';
        } else if (!gostOk && actualB && parseFloat(actualB) < gost.b2500_min) {
            recommendationEl.style.display = 'block';
            recommendationText.innerHTML = 'Низкая индукция при ' + grade + '. Возможная причина: недостаток Si или нарушение режима рекристаллизации.';
        } else {
            recommendationEl.style.display = 'none';
        }

        const alertBox = document.getElementById('auto-block-alert');
        const statusSelect = document.getElementById('status-select');
        
        if (riskScore > 4.5) {
            alertBox.style.display = 'block';
            statusSelect.value = 'reject';
            statusSelect.disabled = true;
        } else {
            alertBox.style.display = 'none';
            statusSelect.disabled = false;
            statusSelect.value = gostOk ? 'approve' : 'reject';
        }

        toggleDefectField();
        updateDefectHint();

        document.querySelectorAll('.queue-row').forEach(r => r.classList.remove('selected'));
        row.classList.add('selected');
        document.getElementById('details-section').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
    }

    function toggleDefectField() {
        const status = document.getElementById('status-select').value;
        const defectBlock = document.getElementById('defect-reason-block');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
        const defectSelect = document.getElementById('defect_type_select');

        if (status === 'reject') {
            defectBlock.style.display = 'block';
            defectSelect.required = true;
            submitBtn.style.backgroundColor = 'var(--danger)';
            submitBtn.innerText = 'ПОДТВЕРДИТЬ БРАК';
        } else {
            defectBlock.style.display = 'none';
            defectSelect.required = false;
            submitBtn.style.backgroundColor = 'var(--success)';
            submitBtn.innerText = 'ЗАФИКСИРОВАТЬ РЕШЕНИЕ';
        }
    }

    function updateDefectHint() {
        const select = document.getElementById('defect_type_select');
        const hint = select.options[select.selectedIndex]?.dataset?.hint || '';
        document.getElementById('defect-hint').textContent = hint || 'Выберите тип дефекта для отображения подсказки';
    }

    function showGostTooltip(event, gradeName, data) {
        const tooltip = document.getElementById('gostTooltip');
        const gost = GOST_STANDARDS[gradeName] || GOST_STANDARDS['2412'];
        
        const p15 = parseFloat(data.p15) || 0;
        const b2500 = parseFloat(data.b2500) || 0;
        const p15ok = p15 <= gost.p15_max;
        const b2500ok = b2500 >= gost.b2500_min;
        const overall = p15ok && b2500ok;

        tooltip.innerHTML = 
            '<div class="gost-tooltip-header">ГОСТ 21427.2-83 — ' + gost.name + '</div>' +
            '<div class="gost-param-row">' +
                '<span class="gost-param-name">P1.5/50:</span>' +
                '<span class="gost-param-value">' + p15.toFixed(3) + ' Вт/кг</span>' +
                '<span class="gost-param-status ' + (p15ok ? 'ok' : 'fail') + '">' + (p15ok ? '✓' : '✗') + ' ≤' + gost.p15_max + '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="gost-param-row">' +
                '<span class="gost-param-name">B2500:</span>' +
                '<span class="gost-param-value">' + b2500.toFixed(3) + ' Тл</span>' +
                '<span class="gost-param-status ' + (b2500ok ? 'ok' : 'fail') + '">' + (b2500ok ? '✓' : '✗') + ' ≥' + gost.b2500_min + '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="gost-param-row" style="margin-top:10px; padding-top:10px; border-top:2px solid #eee; font-weight:700;">' +
                '<span class="gost-param-name">ВЕРДИКТ:</span>' +
                '<span class="gost-param-status ' + (overall ? 'ok' : 'fail') + '" style="font-size:12px; padding:5px 15px;">' +
                    (overall ? 'СООТВЕТСТВУЕТ' : 'НЕ СООТВЕТСТВУЕТ') +
                '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="gost-standard-ref">ГОСТ 21427.2-83, таблица 1</div>';
        
        tooltip.style.display = 'block';
        
        const rect = event.target.getBoundingClientRect();
        let top = rect.bottom + window.scrollY + 10;
        let left = rect.left + window.scrollX;
        
        if (left + 450 > window.innerWidth) left = window.innerWidth - 470;
        if (top + 200 > window.innerHeight + window.scrollY) top = rect.top + window.scrollY - 220;
        
        tooltip.style.top = top + 'px';
        tooltip.style.left = left + 'px';
    }

    function hideGostTooltip() {
        document.getElementById('gostTooltip').style.display = 'none';
    }

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        switchTab('queue');
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.row-checkbox').forEach(cb => {
            cb.addEventListener('change', updateBulkActions);
        });
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.gost-badge').forEach(badge => {
            badge.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
                const grade = this.dataset.grade;
                const p15 = this.dataset.p15;
                const b2500 = this.dataset.b2500;
                showGostTooltip({ target: this }, grade, { p15, b2500 });
            });
            badge.addEventListener('mouseleave', hideGostTooltip);
        });
        
        window.addEventListener('scroll', hideGostTooltip);
    });
</script>

</body>
</html>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const dataScript = document.getElementById('results-data');
    if (!dataScript) return;

    let results;
    try {
        results = JSON.parse(dataScript.textContent);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error("Ошибка парсинга JSON результатов:", e);
        return;
    }

    if (!results || !Array.isArray(results) || results.length === 0) return;

    const labels = results.map((_, i) => `Точка ${i+1}`);
    const pValues = results.map(r => parseFloat(r.p15_50) || 0);
    const bValues = results.map(r => parseFloat(r.b2500) || 0);

    // График P1.5/50
    new Chart(document.getElementById('pChart'), {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels: labels,
            datasets: [{
                label: 'P1.5/50',
                data: pValues,
                borderColor: '#e74c3c',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(231, 76, 60, 0.1)',
                tension: 0.3,
                fill: true
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            plugins: { 
                legend: { display: true, position: 'top' }
            },
            scales: { 
                y: { beginAtZero: false }
            }
        }
    });

    // График B2500
    new Chart(document.getElementById('bChart'), {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels: labels,
            datasets: [{
                label: 'B2500',
                data: bValues,
                borderColor: '#3498db',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.1)',
                tension: 0.3,
                fill: true
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            plugins: { 
                legend: { display: true, position: 'top' }
            },
            scales: { 
                y: { beginAtZero: false }
            }
        }
    });
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<div class="auth-container">
    <div class="card">
        {% if request.resolver_match.url_name == 'register' %}
            <h2>Регистрация сотрудника</h2>
        {% else %}
            <h2>Вход в систему</h2>
        {% endif %}

            <div class="alert-error">
                {{ form.non_field_errors.0 }}
            </div>
        {% endif %}

        <form method="post">
            {% csrf_token %}
            
            {% for field in form %}
                {# Скрываем поле role, если это страница входа #}
                {% if field.name == 'role' and request.resolver_match.url_name != 'register' %}
                    {# Пропускаем отрисовку поля роли #}
                {% else %}
                    <div class="form-group">
                        <label for="{{ field.id_for_label }}">{{ field.label }}</label>
                        {{ field }}
                        {% if field.errors %}
                            <p class="error-text">{{ field.errors.0 }}</p>
                        {% endif %}
                    </div>
                {% endif %}
            {% endfor %}

            <button type="submit">
                {% if request.resolver_match.url_name == 'register' %}Зарегистрироваться{% else %}Войти{% endif %}
            </button>
        </form>

        <div class="auth-footer">
            {% if request.resolver_match.url_name == 'register' %}
                Уже есть учетная запись? <a href="{% url 'login' %}">Войти</a>
            {% else %}
                Новый сотрудник? <a href="{% url 'register' %}">Создать аккаунт</a>
            {% endif %}
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

</body>

admin.py
from django.contrib import admin
from .models import (
    Grade, Standart, Roll, ProcessMode, 
    SimulationResult, Route, Order, SteelGradeReference, GlobalSettings
)


class RollAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ('number', 'grade', 'si_content', 'weight', 'status', 'created_at')
    list_filter = ('status', 'grade')
    search_fields = ('number',)


class StandartAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ('name', 'grade', 'thickness', 'p15_50_max', 'b2500_min')
    list_filter = ('grade',)

class GlobalSettingsAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    
    def has_add_permission(self, request):
        return not GlobalSettings.objects.exists()
    
@admin.register(SimulationResult)
class SimulationResultAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = [
        'roll', 'route', 'inspection_status', 'is_ok', 'gost_ok',
        'predicted_p15_50', 'actual_p15_50', 'final_weight', 'simulation_time'
    ]
    
    list_filter = [
        'inspection_status',
        'is_ok',
        'gost_ok',
        'is_defect',           # ← исправлено
        'route',
        'annealing_type',
        'simulation_time',
    ]
    
    search_fields = ['roll__number', 'notes', 'analog_roll_number', 'defect_reason']
    readonly_fields = ['simulation_time', 'p15_50_delta', 'b2500_delta']
    ordering = ['-simulation_time']

    fieldsets = [
        ("Основная информация", {
            'fields': ('roll', 'order', 'route', 'analog_roll_number')
        }),
        ("Результаты симуляции", {
            'fields': (
                'predicted_p15_50', 'actual_p15_50',
                'predicted_b2500', 'actual_b2500',
                'predicted_p10_400', 'actual_p10_400',
                'predicted_anisotropy', 'actual_anisotropy',
                'final_temperature', 'final_weight', 'yield_percent'
            )
        }),
        ("Статусы", {
            'fields': (
                'is_ok', 'gost_ok', 'inspection_status',
                'is_defect', 'defect_reason', 'notes'
            )
        }),
    ]

    def p15_50_delta(self, obj):
        return obj.p15_50_delta
    p15_50_delta.short_description = 'Δ P1.5/50'

    def b2500_delta(self, obj):
        return obj.b2500_delta
    b2500_delta.short_description = 'Δ B2500'


admin.site.register(Grade)
admin.site.register(Standart, StandartAdmin)
admin.site.register(Roll, RollAdmin)
admin.site.register(ProcessMode)
admin.site.register(Route)
admin.site.register(Order)
admin.site.register(SteelGradeReference)


api.py
from rest_framework.decorators import api_view
from rest_framework.response import Response
from rest_framework import status

from django.db import transaction
from django.conf import settings
from django.core.cache import cache

import uuid
import logging

from .models import (
    Roll,
    ProcessMode,
    SimulationSession
)

from .models_math import predictor
from .math_formulas import (
    assign_route,
    optimize_annealing_parameters
)

from .tasks import run_production_simulation

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


@api_view(['POST'])
def simulate_roll(request):
    """
    API эндпоинт симуляции.

    Поддерживает:
    - Ручной ввод параметров
    - Один рулон из БД
    - Пакетную обработку рулонов
    """

    try:
        data = request.data

        # =========================================================
        # 1. ОБЩИЕ ПАРАМЕТРЫ
        # =========================================================

        use_manual = str(data.get('use_manual', 'false')).lower() == 'true'
        monte_carlo_runs = int(data.get('monte_carlo_runs', 1))
        tick_interval = float(data.get('tick_interval', 0.4))

        # =========================================================
        # 2. ПОЛУЧЕНИЕ roll_ids
        # =========================================================

        roll_ids = []

        if hasattr(data, 'getlist'):
            roll_ids = data.getlist('roll_ids')

        if not roll_ids:
            raw_roll_ids = data.get('roll_ids', [])

            if isinstance(raw_roll_ids, list):
                roll_ids = raw_roll_ids
            elif isinstance(raw_roll_ids, str) and raw_roll_ids.strip():
                roll_ids = [raw_roll_ids]

        # Поддержка старого одиночного режима
        single_roll_id = data.get('roll_id')
        if single_roll_id and not roll_ids:
            roll_ids = [single_roll_id]

        # =========================================================
        # 3. РУЧНОЙ ВВОД
        # =========================================================

        if use_manual:
            try:
                si = float(data.get('si', 3.15))
                c = float(data.get('c', 0.005))
                thickness = float(data.get('thickness', 0.35))
                weight = float(data.get('weight', 17.8))
                h2 = float(data.get('h2', 0.0005))
                n2 = float(data.get('n2', 0.006))
                incoming_state = data.get('incoming_state', 'hot_rolled')
            except (ValueError, TypeError) as e:
                return Response(
                    {"success": False, "error": f"Ошибка параметров: {str(e)}"},
                    status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST
                )
            roll_obj = None
            roll_label = "Ручной ввод"

        # =========================================================
        # 4. РАБОТА С РУЛОНАМИ ИЗ БД
        # =========================================================
        else:
            if not roll_ids:
                return Response(
                    {"success": False, "error": "Не указан roll_id или roll_ids"},
                    status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST
                )

            # =====================================================
            # 4.1 ПАКЕТНАЯ ОБРАБОТКА
            # =====================================================
            if len(roll_ids) >= 2:
                max_limit = getattr(settings, 'MAX_ROLLS_PER_SESSION', 500)
                if len(roll_ids) > max_limit:
                    return Response(
                        {"success": False, "error": f"Превышен лимит рулонов: {len(roll_ids)} > {max_limit}"},
                        status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST
                    )

                with transaction.atomic():
                    session = SimulationSession.objects.create(
                        tick_interval=tick_interval,
                        status='running',
                        total_rolls=len(roll_ids),
                        processed_rolls=0,
                        notes=f"Пакетная симуляция ({len(roll_ids)} рулонов)"
                    )
                    updated = Roll.objects.filter(
                        id__in=roll_ids,
                        status='В очереди'
                    ).update(
                        session=session,
                        status='В обработке (пакет)'
                    )
                    if updated != len(roll_ids):
                        raise Exception(f"Не удалось заблокировать рулоны ({updated}/{len(roll_ids)})")

                # Запуск Celery
                task = run_production_simulation.delay(session.id)

                return Response(
                    {
                        "success": True,
                        "session_id": session.id,
                        "task_id": str(task.id),
                        "status": "queued",
                        "mode": "batch",
                        "rolls_count": len(roll_ids),
                        "message": f"Пакетная симуляция запущена ({len(roll_ids)} рулонов)"
                    },
                    status=status.HTTP_202_ACCEPTED
                )

            # =====================================================
            # 4.2 ОДИНОЧНЫЙ РУЛОН
            # =====================================================
            roll_id = roll_ids[0]
            try:
                roll_obj = Roll.objects.select_related('order', 'target_grade').get(id=roll_id)
            except Roll.DoesNotExist:
                return Response(
                    {"success": False, "error": f"Рулон id={roll_id} не найден"},
                    status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND
                )

            si = float(roll_obj.si_content)
            c = float(getattr(roll_obj, 'c_content', 0.005))
            thickness = float(roll_obj.thickness)
            weight = float(roll_obj.weight)
            h2 = float(getattr(roll_obj, 'h2_content', 0.0005))
            n2 = float(getattr(roll_obj, 'n2_content', 0.006))
            incoming_state = getattr(roll_obj, 'incoming_state', 'hot_rolled')
            roll_label = f"Рулон №{roll_obj.number}"

        # =========================================================
        # 5. ПРОВЕРКИ
        # =========================================================
        if thickness > 2.0:
            return Response(
                {"success": False, "error": f"Толщина {thickness} мм превышает лимит"},
                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST
            )

        mode_id = data.get('mode_id')
        if not mode_id:
            return Response(
                {"success": False, "error": "Не указан mode_id"},
                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST
            )

        try:
            selected_mode = ProcessMode.objects.get(id=mode_id)
        except ProcessMode.DoesNotExist:
            return Response(
                {"success": False, "error": f"Режим id={mode_id} не найден"},
                status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND
            )

        base_temp = float(selected_mode.temperature)

        # =========================================================
        # 6. ПРОГНОЗ
        # =========================================================
        prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
            thickness=thickness,
            si=si,
            c=c,
            temp=base_temp,
            h2=h2,
            n2=n2,
            weight=weight,
            annealing_type='recrystallization_annealing'
        )

        p_predicted = prediction.get('p15_50')
        b_predicted = prediction.get('b2500')

        optimization = optimize_annealing_parameters(
            thickness=thickness,
            si=si,
            c=c,
            base_temp=base_temp,
            base_h2=h2
        )

        route_id, route_description = assign_route(
            thickness=thickness,
            si=si,
            incoming_state=incoming_state
        )

        # =========================================================
        # 7. СОЗДАНИЕ СЕССИИ ДЛЯ ОДИНОЧНОЙ СИМУЛЯЦИИ
        # =========================================================
        with transaction.atomic():
            session = SimulationSession.objects.create(
                tick_interval=tick_interval,
                status='running',
                total_rolls=1,
                processed_rolls=0,
                notes=f"Одиночная симуляция: {roll_label}"
            )

            if roll_obj:
                updated = Roll.objects.filter(
                    id=roll_obj.id,
                    status='В очереди'
                ).update(
                    session=session,
                    status='На проверке'
                )
                if updated == 0:
                    return Response(
                        {"success": False, "error": "Рулон уже обрабатывается или недоступен"},
                        status=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT
                    )

        # =========================================================
        # 8. ЗАПУСК CELERY
        # =========================================================
        task = run_production_simulation.delay(session.id)

        # =========================================================
        # 9. ОТВЕТ
        # =========================================================
        return Response(
            {
                "success": True,
                "session_id": session.id,
                "task_id": str(task.id),
                "status": "queued",
                "mode": "single",
                "message": "Симуляция запущена",
                "roll": roll_label,
                "route": {
                    "id": route_id,
                    "description": route_description
                },
                "parameters": {
                    "thickness": round(thickness, 3),
                    "si": round(si, 3),
                    "c": round(c, 5),
                    "temperature": base_temp,
                    "h2": round(h2, 6),
                    "n2": round(n2, 6),
                    "incoming_state": incoming_state
                },
                "predicted": {
                    "p15_50": round(p_predicted, 3) if p_predicted else None,
                    "b2500": round(b_predicted, 3) if b_predicted else None,
                    "p10_400": prediction.get('p10_400'),
                    "b5000": prediction.get('b5000'),
                    "b10000": prediction.get('b10000'),
                    "anisotropy": prediction.get('anisotropy')
                },
                "optimization": optimization,
                "monte_carlo_runs": monte_carlo_runs
            },
            status=status.HTTP_202_ACCEPTED
        )

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[simulate_roll] ERROR: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
        return Response(
            {"success": False, "error": str(e)},
            status=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR
        )


# =====================================================================
# НОВЫЕ ФУНКЦИИ ДЛЯ ИНТЕРАКТИВНОЙ СИМУЛЯЦИИ
# =====================================================================

@api_view(['POST'])
def start_interactive_simulation(request):
    """
    Запуск интерактивной симуляции одного рулона с отслеживанием прогресса в реальном времени.
    Возвращает session_id для polling.
    """
    try:
        data = request.data
        roll_id = data.get('roll_id')
        mode_id = data.get('mode_id')

        if not roll_id or not mode_id:
            return Response(
                {"success": False, "error": "roll_id и mode_id обязательны"},
                status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST
            )

        session_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        
        # Инициализация состояния в кэше
        cache.set(f'sim_interactive_{session_id}', {
            'status': 'queued',
            'progress': 0,
            'current_step': None,
            'roll_id': roll_id,
            'mode_id': mode_id,
            'steps_total': 0,
            'steps_done': 0,
            'result': None
        }, timeout=3600)

        # Запуск задачи Celery
        # Примечание: в tasks.py необходимо создать задачу run_interactive_simulation
        from .tasks import run_interactive_simulation
        run_interactive_simulation.delay(session_id, roll_id, mode_id)

        return Response({
            "success": True,
            "session_id": session_id,
            "status": "started",
            "message": "Интерактивная симуляция запущена. Используйте session_id для получения прогресса."
        }, status=status.HTTP_202_ACCEPTED)

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[start_interactive_simulation] ERROR: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
        return Response(
            {"success": False, "error": str(e)},
            status=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR
        )


@api_view(['GET'])
def get_simulation_progress(request, session_id):
    """
    Получение текущего прогресса интерактивной симуляции.
    """
    try:
        data = cache.get(f'sim_interactive_{session_id}')
        
        if not data:
            return Response(
                {"success": False, "error": "Сессия не найдена или истек срок действия"},
                status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND
            )

        return Response({
            "success": True,
            "session_id": session_id,
            "status": data.get('status'),
            "progress": data.get('progress', 0),
            "current_step": data.get('current_step'),
            "steps_total": data.get('steps_total', 0),
            "steps_done": data.get('steps_done', 0),
            "result": data.get('result')
        })

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[get_simulation_progress] ERROR: {str(e)}", exc_info=True)
        return Response(
            {"success": False, "error": str(e)},
            status=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR
        )

grade_assignment.py
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from django.db.models import Q

from .models import (
    Grade,
    SteelStandard,
)


# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================

def normalize_steel_type(steel_type: Optional[str]) -> str:
    """
    Нормализует тип стали. Возвращает 'GO' или 'NGO'.
    По умолчанию — 'NGO'.
    """
    if not steel_type:
        return "NGO"
    
    steel_type = str(steel_type).strip().upper()
    return steel_type if steel_type in ("GO", "NGO") else "NGO"


# =========================================================
# ОСНОВНОЕ НАЗНАЧЕНИЕ МАРКИ
# =========================================================

def assign_grade_from_properties(
    p15_50: float,
    b2500: float,
    thickness: float = 0.35,
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
    p_tolerance: float = 0.05,
    b_tolerance: float = 0.02,
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Подбор марки стали по магнитным свойствам.
    
    Алгоритм:
    1. Ищет марки, строго соответствующие ГОСТ/IEC (P <= limit, B >= limit).
    2. Если подходящих несколько, выбирает высший класс (наименьший P1.5/50_max).
    3. Если строгих соответствий нет, вычисляет ближайшую марку для диагностики,
       но помечает matched=False (сигнал для ОТК/симуляции).
    """
    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)
    
    # Безопасное приведение типов
    p_val = float(p15_50 or 0.0)
    b_val = float(b2500 or 0.0)
    h_val = float(thickness or 0.35)

    # =====================================================
    # 1. ПОИСК СТРОГО СООТВЕТСТВУЮЩИХ СТАНДАРТОВ
    # =====================================================
    # Учитываем небольшой допуск на погрешность симуляции/измерений
    compliant_standards = SteelStandard.objects.filter(
        steel_type=steel_type,
        is_active=True,
        p15_50_max__gte=p_val - p_tolerance,
        b2500_min__lte=b_val + b_tolerance,
    ).order_by("p15_50_max")  # Сортируем от лучшего класса (меньшие потери) к худшему

    best_standard = compliant_standards.first()
    matched = best_standard is not None

    # =====================================================
    # 2. FALLBACK: ЕСЛИ НИ ОДНА МАРКА НЕ ПРОШЛА СТРОГО
    # =====================================================
    if not matched:
        # Ищем марку с минимальным "штрафом" за несоответствие
        all_standards = SteelStandard.objects.filter(
            steel_type=steel_type,
            is_active=True
        )
        
        best_penalty = float("inf")
        for std in all_standards:
            p_limit = float(std.p15_50_max or 999.0)
            b_limit = float(std.b2500_min or 0.0)
            
            # Штраф: превышение потерь + недобор индукции
            penalty = (
                max(0.0, p_val - p_limit) * 2.0 +
                max(0.0, b_limit - b_val)
            )
            
            if penalty < best_penalty:
                best_penalty = penalty
                best_standard = std

    # =====================================================
    # 3. ФОРМИРОВАНИЕ РЕЗУЛЬТАТА
    # =====================================================
    grade_name = best_standard.name if best_standard else None
    grade_obj = None
    
    if grade_name:
        grade_obj = Grade.objects.filter(name=grade_name).first()

    return {
        "grade": grade_obj,
        "grade_name": grade_name,
        "steel_type": steel_type,
        "matched": matched,  # True если прошла ГОСТ/IEC, False если fallback
        "standard_id": best_standard.id if best_standard else None,
    }


# =========================================================
# ПРОВЕРКА ГОСТ / IEC
# =========================================================

def check_grade_compliance(
    p15_50: float,
    b2500: float,
    standard: SteelStandard,
) -> bool:
    """
    Строгая проверка соответствия параметров конкретному стандарту.
    Возвращает True только если оба параметра в пределах норм.
    """
    if not standard:
        return False

    p_val = float(p15_50 or 0.0)
    b_val = float(b2500 or 0.0)
    
    p_limit = float(standard.p15_50_max or float("inf"))
    b_limit = float(standard.b2500_min or 0.0)

    p_ok = p_val <= p_limit
    b_ok = b_val >= b_limit

    return p_ok and b_ok



iec_classifier.py
# production/iec_classifier.py

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional


@dataclass
class IECGradeResult:
    grade: str
    standard: str
    steel_type: str

    p15_50_max: Optional[float] = None
    b2500_min: Optional[float] = None

    confidence: float = 0.0
    matched: bool = False


class IECClassifier:
    """
    Классификатор марок по IEC / EN.

    Поддержка:
    - NGO
    - GO
    - IEC 60404
    - EN 10106
    - EN 10107
    """

    # =====================================================
    # NGO
    # =====================================================

    NGO_GRADES = [

        {
            "grade": "M250-35A",
            "p15_50_max": 2.50,
            "b2500_min": 1.63,
            "thickness": 0.35,
        },

        {
            "grade": "M270-35A",
            "p15_50_max": 2.70,
            "b2500_min": 1.62,
            "thickness": 0.35,
        },

        {
            "grade": "M310-35A",
            "p15_50_max": 3.10,
            "b2500_min": 1.60,
            "thickness": 0.35,
        },

        {
            "grade": "M400-50A",
            "p15_50_max": 4.00,
            "b2500_min": 1.55,
            "thickness": 0.50,
        },
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    GO_GRADES = [

        {
            "grade": "27Q120",
            "p17_50_max": 1.20,
            "b800_min": 1.89,
            "thickness": 0.27,
        },

        {
            "grade": "30Q140",
            "p17_50_max": 1.40,
            "b800_min": 1.88,
            "thickness": 0.30,
        },

        {
            "grade": "35Q155",
            "p17_50_max": 1.55,
            "b800_min": 1.87,
            "thickness": 0.35,
        },
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # NGO CLASSIFICATION
    # =====================================================

    def classify_ngo(
        self,
        p15_50,
        b2500,
        thickness,
    ):

        best_match = None
        best_score = -999

        for grade in self.NGO_GRADES:

            score = 0

            p_limit = grade["p15_50_max"]
            b_limit = grade["b2500_min"]

            if p15_50 <= p_limit:
                score += 50

            score -= abs(p15_50 - p_limit) * 25

            if b2500 >= b_limit:
                score += 40

            score -= abs(b2500 - b_limit) * 30

            score -= abs(
                thickness - grade["thickness"]
            ) * 100

            if score > best_score:
                best_score = score
                best_match = grade

        if not best_match:
            return IECGradeResult(
                grade="UNDEFINED",
                standard="IEC 60404",
                steel_type="NGO",
                matched=False,
            )

        confidence = max(
            0.0,
            min(100.0, 70 + best_score / 10)
        )

        return IECGradeResult(
            grade=best_match["grade"],
            standard="IEC 60404-8-4",
            steel_type="NGO",

            p15_50_max=best_match["p15_50_max"],
            b2500_min=best_match["b2500_min"],

            confidence=round(confidence, 1),
            matched=True,
        )

    # =====================================================
    # GO CLASSIFICATION
    # =====================================================

    def classify_go(
        self,
        p15_50,
        b2500,
        thickness,
    ):

        best_match = None
        best_score = -999

        for grade in self.GO_GRADES:

            score = 0

            target_p = grade["p17_50_max"]
            target_b = grade["b800_min"]

            score -= abs(p15_50 - target_p) * 40
            score -= abs(b2500 - target_b) * 45

            score -= abs(
                thickness - grade["thickness"]
            ) * 120

            if score > best_score:
                best_score = score
                best_match = grade

        if not best_match:
            return IECGradeResult(
                grade="UNDEFINED",
                standard="IEC 60404",
                steel_type="GO",
                matched=False,
            )

        confidence = max(
            0.0,
            min(100.0, 75 + best_score / 10)
        )

        return IECGradeResult(
            grade=best_match["grade"],
            standard="IEC 60404-8-7",
            steel_type="GO",

            confidence=round(confidence, 1),
            matched=True,
        )

    # =====================================================
    # UNIVERSAL
    # =====================================================

    def classify(
        self,
        steel_type,
        p15_50,
        b2500,
        thickness,
    ):

        steel_type = (
            steel_type or "NGO"
        ).upper()

        if steel_type == "GO":

            return self.classify_go(
                p15_50=p15_50,
                b2500=b2500,
                thickness=thickness,
            )

        return self.classify_ngo(
            p15_50=p15_50,
            b2500=b2500,
            thickness=thickness,
        )


# =====================================================
# GLOBAL
# =====================================================

iec_classifier = IECClassifier()

kpi_engine.py
# production/kpi_engine.py

from statistics import mean
from typing import Dict, Any


def calculate_kpis(simulation_result) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Расчёт KPI для SimulationResult.

    KPI:
    - yield
    - quality
    - defect rate
    - energy index
    - process stability
    """

    steps = simulation_result.steps.all()

    if not steps.exists():

        return {
            "yield_percent": 0.0,
            "average_quality": 0.0,
            "defect_rate": 0.0,
            "energy_efficiency": 0.0,
            "process_stability": 0.0,
        }

    # =====================================================
    # QUALITY
    # =====================================================

    qualities = [
        float(step.annealing_quality or 0)
        for step in steps
    ]

    average_quality = round(
        mean(qualities),
        2
    )

    # =====================================================
    # DEFECT RATE
    # =====================================================

    defect_steps = steps.filter(
        is_defect=True
    ).count()

    total_steps = steps.count()

    defect_rate = round(
        (defect_steps / total_steps) * 100,
        2
    ) if total_steps else 0.0

    # =====================================================
    # WEIGHT / YIELD
    # =====================================================

    initial_weight = float(
        getattr(
            simulation_result.roll,
            "weight",
            0
        ) or 0
    )

    final_weight = float(
        getattr(
            simulation_result,
            "final_weight",
            0
        ) or 0
    )

    if initial_weight > 0:

        yield_percent = round(
            (final_weight / initial_weight) * 100,
            2
        )

    else:
        yield_percent = 0.0

    # =====================================================
    # ENERGY
    # =====================================================

    temperatures = [
        float(step.temperature or 0)
        for step in steps
    ]

    avg_temp = mean(temperatures)

    energy_efficiency = round(
        max(
            0.0,
            100 - (avg_temp - 750) * 0.05
        ),
        2
    )

    # =====================================================
    # STABILITY
    # =====================================================

    temp_spread = (
        max(temperatures) - min(temperatures)
        if temperatures else 0
    )

    process_stability = round(
        max(
            0.0,
            100 - temp_spread * 0.08
        ),
        2
    )

    # =====================================================
    # SAVE
    # =====================================================

    simulation_result.yield_percent = yield_percent
    simulation_result.average_quality = average_quality

    simulation_result.save(
        update_fields=[
            "yield_percent",
            "average_quality",
        ]
    )

    # =====================================================
    # RETURN
    # =====================================================

    return {

        "yield_percent": yield_percent,

        "average_quality": average_quality,

        "defect_rate": defect_rate,

        "energy_efficiency": energy_efficiency,

        "process_stability": process_stability,

        "total_steps": total_steps,

        "defect_steps": defect_steps,
    }

math_formulas.py
# production/math_formulas.py

import math
import random

from typing import Tuple, Dict, Any


# =========================================================
# CONSTANTS
# =========================================================

MIN_P_GO = 0.70
MAX_P_GO = 2.20

MIN_P_NGO = 1.00
MAX_P_NGO = 4.80

MIN_B_GO = 1.78
MAX_B_GO = 2.15

MIN_B_NGO = 1.45
MAX_B_NGO = 1.95
