# =========================================================
# HELPERS
# =========================================================

def clamp(value, minimum, maximum):

    return max(minimum, min(value, maximum))


def normalize_steel_type(steel_type: str) -> str:

    if not steel_type:
        return "NGO"

    steel_type = str(steel_type).upper()

    if steel_type not in ["GO", "NGO"]:
        return "NGO"

    return steel_type


def safe_float(value, default=0.0):

    try:
        return float(value)
    except Exception:
        return float(default)


# =========================================================
# P1.5/50
# =========================================================

def calculate_p15_50(
    thickness: float,
    si: float,
    c: float = 0.005,
    temp: float = 840.0,
    h2: float = 0.0005,
    annealing_type: str = "recrystallization",
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
    cooling_rate: float = 18.0,
    grain_size: float = 1.0,
    texture_factor: float = 1.0,
    nitriding_factor: float = 1.0,
    stress_factor: float = 1.0,
) -> float:
    """
    Расчёт магнитных потерь P1.5/50.
    """

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    thickness = clamp(
        safe_float(thickness, 0.35),
        0.18,
        1.20
    )

    si = clamp(
        safe_float(si, 3.0),
        0.8,
        4.8
    )

    c = clamp(
        safe_float(c, 0.005),
        0.0001,
        0.05
    )

    temp = clamp(
        safe_float(temp, 840.0),
        650.0,
        1250.0
    )

    h2 = clamp(
        safe_float(h2, 0.0005),
        0.00001,
        0.05
    )

    cooling_rate = clamp(
        safe_float(cooling_rate, 18.0),
        1.0,
        120.0
    )

    grain_size = clamp(
        safe_float(grain_size, 1.0),
        0.3,
        5.0
    )

    texture_factor = clamp(
        safe_float(texture_factor, 1.0),
        0.6,
        2.0
    )

    nitriding_factor = clamp(
        safe_float(nitriding_factor, 1.0),
        0.7,
        1.4
    )

    stress_factor = clamp(
        safe_float(stress_factor, 1.0),
        0.8,
        1.5
    )

    # =====================================================
    # BASE MODEL
    # =====================================================

    p = (
        4.55
        + thickness * 2.18
        - si * 0.88
        + c * 11.5
    )

    # =====================================================
    # TEMPERATURE
    # =====================================================

    optimum_temp = (
        1120.0
        if steel_type == "GO"
        else 860.0
    )

    temp_delta = abs(temp - optimum_temp)

    p += temp_delta * 0.0048

    # =====================================================
    # H2
    # =====================================================

    h2_effect = max(
        0.0,
        h2 * 10000 - 3
    )

    p -= h2_effect * 0.075

    # =====================================================
    # COOLING RATE
    # =====================================================

    if cooling_rate > 40:
        p += 0.24

    elif cooling_rate < 8:
        p += 0.10

    # =====================================================
    # GRAIN SIZE
    # =====================================================

    grain_factor = (
        1.10
        - min(grain_size, 4.0) * 0.05
    )

    p *= grain_factor

    # =====================================================
    # TEXTURE
    # =====================================================

    texture_multiplier = (
        1.06
        - min(texture_factor, 1.6) * 0.065
    )

    p *= texture_multiplier

    # =====================================================
    # NITRIDING
    # =====================================================

    p *= nitriding_factor

    # =====================================================
    # STRESS
    # =====================================================

    p *= stress_factor

    # =====================================================
    # GO / NGO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":

        p *= 0.70

        if annealing_type in [
            "high_temp",
            "secondary_recrystallization",
        ]:
            p *= 0.80

        if texture_factor > 1.15:
            p *= 0.88

        if grain_size >= 2.5:
            p *= 0.92

    else:

        if annealing_type == "high_temp":
            p *= 0.93
        else:
            p *= 0.985

    # =====================================================
    # SILICON
    # =====================================================

    if si < 2.7:
        p += 0.42

    elif si > 3.4:
        p -= 0.16

    # =====================================================
    # CARBON
    # =====================================================

    if c > 0.008:
        p *= 1.10

    elif c < 0.002:
        p *= 0.97

    # =====================================================
    # RANDOM PROCESS NOISE
    # =====================================================

    noise = (
        random.uniform(-0.05, 0.05)
        if steel_type == "NGO"
        else random.uniform(-0.03, 0.03)
    )

    p += noise

    # =====================================================
    # LIMITS
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":
        p = clamp(p, MIN_P_GO, MAX_P_GO)
    else:
        p = clamp(p, MIN_P_NGO, MAX_P_NGO)

    return round(float(p), 3)


# =========================================================
# B2500
# =========================================================

def calculate_b2500(
    thickness: float,
    si: float,
    temp: float = 840.0,
    h2: float = 0.0005,
    annealing_type: str = "recrystallization",
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
    grain_size: float = 1.0,
    texture_factor: float = 1.0,
    stress_factor: float = 1.0,
) -> float:
    """
    Расчёт магнитной индукции B2500.
    """

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    thickness = clamp(
        safe_float(thickness, 0.35),
        0.18,
        1.20
    )

    si = clamp(
        safe_float(si, 3.0),
        0.8,
        4.8
    )

    temp = clamp(
        safe_float(temp, 840.0),
        650.0,
        1250.0
    )

    h2 = clamp(
        safe_float(h2, 0.0005),
        0.00001,
        0.05
    )

    grain_size = clamp(
        safe_float(grain_size, 1.0),
        0.3,
        5.0
    )

    texture_factor = clamp(
        safe_float(texture_factor, 1.0),
        0.6,
        2.0
    )

    stress_factor = clamp(
        safe_float(stress_factor, 1.0),
        0.8,
        1.5
    )

    # =====================================================
    # BASE
    # =====================================================

    b = (
        1.50
        + si * 0.058
        - thickness * 0.085
        + temp * 0.00017
    )

    # =====================================================
    # H2
    # =====================================================

    b += h2 * 10000 * 0.0032

    # =====================================================
    # GRAIN
    # =====================================================

    b += grain_size * 0.011

    # =====================================================
    # TEXTURE
    # =====================================================

    b += texture_factor * 0.030

    # =====================================================
    # STRESS
    # =====================================================

    b /= stress_factor

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":

        b += 0.13

        if annealing_type in [
            "high_temp",
            "secondary_recrystallization",
        ]:
            b += 0.045

        if texture_factor >= 1.20:
            b += 0.025

    # =====================================================
    # SI
    # =====================================================

    if si < 2.7:
        b -= 0.05

    elif si > 3.5:
        b += 0.020

    # =====================================================
    # CARBON
    # =====================================================

    if annealing_type == "secondary_recrystallization":
        b += 0.02

    # =====================================================
    # NOISE
    # =====================================================

    noise = (
        random.uniform(-0.010, 0.010)
        if steel_type == "NGO"
        else random.uniform(-0.006, 0.006)
    )

    b += noise

    # =====================================================
    # LIMITS
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":
        b = clamp(b, MIN_B_GO, MAX_B_GO)
    else:
        b = clamp(b, MIN_B_NGO, MAX_B_NGO)

    return round(float(b), 3)


# =========================================================
# ANNEALING QUALITY
# =========================================================

def calculate_annealing_quality(
    temp: float,
    h2: float,
    annealing_type: str = "recrystallization",
    dew_point: float = -25,
    cooling_rate: float = 18,
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
) -> float:
    """
    Качество отжига.
    """

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    optimum_temp = (
        1120.0
        if steel_type == "GO"
        else 860.0
    )

    quality = 96.0

    # =====================================================
    # TEMP
    # =====================================================

    quality -= abs(
        temp - optimum_temp
    ) * 0.06

    # =====================================================
    # H2
    # =====================================================

    quality += min(
        12.0,
        h2 * 10000 * 0.8
    )

    # =====================================================
    # DEW POINT
    # =====================================================

    if dew_point > -10:
        quality -= 6.0

    elif dew_point < -40:
        quality += 1.5

    # =====================================================
    # COOLING
    # =====================================================

    if cooling_rate > 40:
        quality -= 4.5

    elif cooling_rate < 6:
        quality -= 2.0

    # =====================================================
    # ANNEALING TYPE
    # =====================================================

    if annealing_type == "high_temp":
        quality += 6.5

    elif annealing_type == "secondary_recrystallization":
        quality += 11.0

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":
        quality += 3.0

    # =====================================================
    # NOISE
    # =====================================================

    quality += random.uniform(-2.0, 2.0)

    quality = clamp(
        quality,
        55.0,
        100.0
    )

    return round(float(quality), 1)


# =========================================================
# MAGNETIC PROPERTIES
# =========================================================

def calculate_magnetic_properties(
    base_p: float,
    base_b: float,
    quality: float,
    h2_percent: float,
    temp: float,
    annealing_type: str = "recrystallization",
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
) -> Tuple[float, float]:

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    temp_bonus = max(
        0.0,
        (temp - 820) / 220
    )

    h2_bonus = min(
        1.2,
        h2_percent * 80
    )

    effective_quality = (
        quality * 0.72
        + temp_bonus * 12
        + h2_bonus * 8
    )

    p_loss = base_p * (
        1.27
        - 0.29 * (effective_quality / 100)
    )

    b_induction = base_b * (
        0.91
        + 0.10 * (effective_quality / 100)
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ANNEALING
    # =====================================================

    if annealing_type == "high_temp":

        p_loss *= 0.92
        b_induction *= 1.03

    elif annealing_type == "secondary_recrystallization":

        p_loss *= 0.86
        b_induction *= 1.06

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":

        p_loss *= 0.96
        b_induction *= 1.015

    return (
        round(float(p_loss), 3),
        round(float(b_induction), 3),
    )


# =========================================================
# ROUTE ASSIGNMENT
# =========================================================

def assign_route(
    thickness: float,
    si: float,
    incoming_state: str = "hot_rolled",
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
) -> Tuple[str, str]:

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    thickness = safe_float(thickness, 0.35)
    si = safe_float(si, 3.0)

    # =====================================================
    # INVALID
    # =====================================================

    if thickness > 0.65:

        return (
            "BR",
            "Брак: слишком большая толщина"
        )

    if si < 2.0 or si > 4.5:

        return (
            "BR",
            "Брак: недопустимое содержание Si"
        )

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":

        if thickness <= 0.27:

            return (
                "GO_PREMIUM",
                (
                    "GO premium: "
                    "secondary recrystallization + laser"
                )
            )

        if thickness <= 0.35:

            return (
                "GO_THIN",
                "GO тонкий маршрут"
            )

        return (
            "GO_STANDARD",
            "GO стандартный маршрут"
        )

    # =====================================================
    # NGO
    # =====================================================

    if thickness <= 0.30 and si >= 3.10:

        return (
            "NGO_THIN",
            "Тонкий NGO маршрут"
        )

    if si >= 3.25:

        return (
            "NGO_HIGH_SI",
            "Высококремнистый NGO"
        )

    return (
        "NGO_STANDARD",
        "Стандартный NGO маршрут"
    )


# =========================================================
# DOWNTIME
# =========================================================

def calculate_downtime_probability(
    temp: float,
    h2: float,
    cumulative_risk: float,
) -> float:

    probability = 0.018

    if temp > 900:
        probability += 0.06

    elif temp > 870:
        probability += 0.03

    if h2 < 0.0003:
        probability += 0.025

    probability += cumulative_risk * 0.08

    probability = clamp(
        probability,
        0.003,
        0.22
    )

    return round(float(probability), 4)


# =========================================================
# DEFECT PROBABILITY
# =========================================================

def calculate_defect_probability(
    si: float,
    c: float,
    temp: float,
    h2: float,
    n2: float,
    cumulative_risk: float,
    annealing_quality: float,
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
) -> float:

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    probability = 0.0012

    # =====================================================
    # SI
    # =====================================================

    if si < 2.8:
        probability += 0.006

    if si > 3.55:
        probability += 0.003

    # =====================================================
    # C
    # =====================================================

    if c > 0.006:
        probability += 0.005

    # =====================================================
    # TEMP
    # =====================================================

    if temp > 930:
        probability += 0.010

    elif temp < 800:
        probability += 0.008

    # =====================================================
    # H2
    # =====================================================

    if h2 < 0.00025:
        probability += 0.006

    # =====================================================
    # N2
    # =====================================================

    if n2 > 0.03:
        probability += 0.004

    # =====================================================
    # QUALITY
    # =====================================================

    probability *= (
        1.0
        + (100 - annealing_quality) / 120
    )

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == "GO":
        probability *= 1.25

    # =====================================================
    # CUMULATIVE RISK
    # =====================================================

    probability += cumulative_risk * 0.06

    probability = clamp(
        probability,
        0.0005,
        0.055
    )

    return round(float(probability), 4)


# =========================================================
# PROCESS RISK
# =========================================================

def calculate_risk(
    cumulative_defect_risk: float,
    annealing_quality: float,
) -> float:

    risk = (
        cumulative_defect_risk * 7.8
        + (100 - annealing_quality) * 0.045
    )

    risk = clamp(risk, 0.5, 5.9)

    return round(float(risk), 1)


# =========================================================
# DECARBURIZATION
# =========================================================

def calculate_decarburization(
    temp: float,
    h2: float,
    time_hours: float,
    initial_c: float,
) -> float:
    """
    Расчёт остаточного углерода.
    """

    temp = clamp(
        safe_float(temp, 840),
        700,
        1250
    )

    h2 = clamp(
        safe_float(h2, 0.001),
        0.00001,
        0.05
    )

    time_hours = clamp(
        safe_float(time_hours, 6),
        0.5,
        72
    )

    initial_c = clamp(
        safe_float(initial_c, 0.005),
        0.0001,
        0.05
    )

    efficiency = (
        (temp - 780) * 0.0008
        + h2 * 100
        + time_hours * 0.015
    )

    efficiency = clamp(
        efficiency,
        0.05,
        0.95
    )

    final_c = initial_c * (
        1.0 - efficiency
    )

    final_c = max(final_c, 0.0003)

    return round(float(final_c), 5)


# =========================================================
# ANNEALING OPTIMIZATION
# =========================================================

def optimize_annealing_parameters(
    thickness: float,
    si: float,
    c: float = 0.005,
    base_temp: float = 840.0,
    base_h2: float = 0.0005,
    steel_type: str = "NGO",
) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    steel_type = normalize_steel_type(steel_type)

    best_p = float("inf")

    best_temp = base_temp
    best_h2 = base_h2
    best_quality = 0.0
    best_b = 0.0

    temp_range = range(
        int(base_temp - 40),
        int(base_temp + 41),
        10
    )

    h2_range = [
        0.0005,
        0.001,
        0.002,
        0.003,
        0.005,
    ]

    for temp in temp_range:

        for h2_val in h2_range:

            p = calculate_p15_50(
                thickness=thickness,
                si=si,
                c=c,
                temp=temp,
                h2=h2_val,
                annealing_type="high_temp",
                steel_type=steel_type,
            )

            b = calculate_b2500(
                thickness=thickness,
                si=si,
                temp=temp,
                h2=h2_val,
                annealing_type="high_temp",
                steel_type=steel_type,
            )

            quality = calculate_annealing_quality(
                temp=temp,
                h2=h2_val,
                annealing_type="high_temp",
                steel_type=steel_type,
            )

            if (
                p < best_p
                and quality > 75
            ):

                best_p = p
                best_temp = temp
                best_h2 = h2_val
                best_quality = quality
                best_b = b

    return {

        "optimal_temp": round(
            float(best_temp),
            1
        ),

        "optimal_h2": round(
            float(best_h2),
            5
        ),

        "predicted_p15_50": round(
            float(best_p),
            3
        ),

        "predicted_b2500": round(
            float(best_b),
            3
        ),

        "annealing_quality": round(
            float(best_quality),
            1
        ),

        "steel_type": steel_type,
    }


ml_data_collector.py
import os
import csv
from pathlib import Path

class MLDataCollector:
    """
    Собирает данные из симуляции для последующего обучения ML-моделей.
    Сохраняет в CSV формат, удобный для pandas/sklearn.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, filename="ml_dataset.csv"):
        self.filepath = Path(filename)
        # Заголовки CSV
        self.headers = [
            # Features (Входные параметры процесса)
            "thickness", "si", "c", "h2", "n2", 
            "annealing_temp", "cooling_rate", "dew_point", "grain_size",
            # Targets (Выходные параметры, которые предсказываем)
            "p15_50", "b2500", "p10_400", "b5000", "b10000", "anisotropy",
            # Classification targets
            "grade", "is_scrap"
        ]
        
        # Если файл не существует, создаем с заголовком
        if not self.filepath.exists():
            with open(self.filepath, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                writer = csv.writer(f)
                writer.writerow(self.headers)

    def save_row(self, data_dict: dict):
        """
        Принимает словарь с данными и дописывает строку в CSV.
        """
        try:
            with open(self.filepath, 'a', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=self.headers)
                writer.writerow(data_dict)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ML Collector Error] Не удалось сохранить строку: {e}")

# Глобальный экземпляр для удобства импорта
collector = MLDataCollector()


ml_models.py
import pandas as pd
import joblib
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestRegressor, RandomForestClassifier
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.metrics import mean_absolute_error, accuracy_score
from pathlib import Path
import sys

# === ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ ПУТЕЙ ===
# SCRIPT_DIR = production/
# PROJECT_DIR = web/ (корень проекта)
SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
PROJECT_DIR = SCRIPT_DIR.parent

MODEL_DIR = SCRIPT_DIR / "ml_models_saved"
MODEL_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

# По умолчанию ищем датасет в корне проекта (web/ml_dataset.csv)
DEFAULT_DATASET_PATH = PROJECT_DIR / "ml_dataset.csv"

def train_and_save_models(dataset_path=None):
    if dataset_path is None:
        dataset_path = DEFAULT_DATASET_PATH

    dataset_path = Path(dataset_path)

    if not dataset_path.exists():
        print(f"❌ Файл датасета не найден: {dataset_path}")
        print("💡 Сначала запустите генерацию: python generate_ml_data.py")
        sys.exit(1)

    print(f"📂 Загрузка датасета: {dataset_path}")
    df = pd.read_csv(dataset_path)
    
    # === ОСТАЛЬНОЙ ВАШ КОД ОСТАЁТСЯ БЕЗ ИЗМЕНЕНИЙ ===
    if df.empty:
        print("Датасет пуст. Нечему учиться.")
        return

    # === 1. Регрессия: Предсказание P1.5/50 ===
    features_reg = ["thickness", "si", "c", "h2", "n2", "annealing_temp", "cooling_rate", "dew_point", "grain_size"]
    
    # Проверка наличия колонок (если каких-то нет, нужно исключить или заполнить)
    available_features = [f for f in features_reg if f in df.columns]
    
    X = df[available_features].fillna(0) # Заполняем NaN нулями для безопасности
    y_p15 = df["p15_50"]
    
    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y_p15, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)
    
    model_p15 = RandomForestRegressor(n_estimators=100, max_depth=10, random_state=42)
    model_p15.fit(X_train, y_train)
    
    preds = model_p15.predict(X_test)
    mae = mean_absolute_error(y_test, preds)
    print(f"Model P1.5/50 trained. MAE: {mae:.4f}")
    
    joblib.dump(model_p15, MODEL_DIR / "model_p15.pkl")
    
    # === 2. Классификация: Вероятность брака (Scrap) ===
    if "is_scrap" in df.columns:
        y_scrap = df["is_scrap"]
        X_train_s, X_test_s, y_train_s, y_test_s = train_test_split(X, y_scrap, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)
        
        # Используем Classifier, так как target бинарный (0 или 1)
        model_scrap = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, max_depth=5, random_state=42)
        model_scrap.fit(X_train_s, y_train_s)
        
        acc = accuracy_score(y_test_s, model_scrap.predict(X_test_s))
        print(f"Model Scrap trained. Accuracy: {acc:.4f}")
        
        joblib.dump(model_scrap, MODEL_DIR / "model_scrap.pkl")

    print(f"✅ Модели сохранены в папке: {MODEL_DIR}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    train_and_save_models()


ml_predictor.py
# production/ml_predictor.py
import joblib
import numpy as np
import warnings
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Optional

# Подавляем назойливое предупреждение sklearn о feature names (безопасно для наших задач)
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore", message="X does not have valid feature names")

# Абсолютный путь к папке с моделями относительно этого файла
# Это гарантирует работу и из manage.py, и из celery worker
MODEL_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "ml_models_saved"

class MLPredictor:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model_p15: Optional[object] = None
        self.model_scrap: Optional[object] = None
        self._load_models()

    def _load_models(self):
        """Безопасная загрузка моделей при старте"""
        try:
            p15_path = MODEL_DIR / "model_p15.pkl"
            if p15_path.exists():
                self.model_p15 = joblib.load(p15_path)
            else:
                print("[ML] Model P1.5 not found. Using physics fallback.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ML Error] Failed to load P1.5 model: {e}")

        try:
            scrap_path = MODEL_DIR / "model_scrap.pkl"
            if scrap_path.exists():
                self.model_scrap = joblib.load(scrap_path)
            else:
                print("[ML] Model Scrap not found. Using default risk.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ML Error] Failed to load Scrap model: {e}")

    def _get_feature_vector(self, features_dict: dict) -> np.ndarray:
        """
        Подготовка вектора признаков в точном порядке, как при обучении.
        Порядок должен строго соответствовать ml_models.py
        """
        return np.array([[
            float(features_dict.get('thickness', 0.35)),
            float(features_dict.get('si', 3.0)),
            float(features_dict.get('c', 0.005)),
            float(features_dict.get('h2', 0.0005)),
            float(features_dict.get('n2', 0.006)),
            float(features_dict.get('annealing_temp', 840)),
            float(features_dict.get('cooling_rate', 15)),
            float(features_dict.get('dew_point', -30)),
            float(features_dict.get('grain_size', 7)),
        ]])

    def predict_p15_hybrid(self, features_dict: dict, physics_p15: float) -> float:
        """
        Гибридное предсказание: 70% физика + 30% ML.
        Если ML не загружен или упал → возвращается чистое значение физики.
        """
        if self.model_p15 is None:
            return round(physics_p15, 3)

        try:
            X = self._get_feature_vector(features_dict)
            ml_pred = float(self.model_p15.predict(X)[0])
            
            # Гибридная формула
            hybrid_result = (0.7 * physics_p15) + (0.3 * ml_pred)
            return round(hybrid_result, 3)
        except Exception:
            # Fallback на физику при любой ошибке ML
            return round(physics_p15, 3)

    def predict_scrap_risk(self, features_dict: dict) -> float:
        """
        Возвращает вероятность брака от 0.0 до 1.0.
        Безопасно обрабатывает ситуацию, когда в датасете был только один класс.
        """
        if self.model_scrap is None:
            return 0.05

        try:
            X = self._get_feature_vector(features_dict)
            probabilities = self.model_scrap.predict_proba(X)[0]

            # КРИТИЧЕСКАЯ ЗАЩИТА от IndexError при одноклассовых моделях
            if len(probabilities) == 2:
                risk = float(probabilities[1])  # Вероятность класса 1 (Scrap)
            else:
                # Модель знала только один класс (скорее всего все 0)
                known_class = self.model_scrap.classes_[0]
                risk = 0.0 if known_class == 0 else 1.0

            return round(max(0.0, min(1.0, risk)), 4)
        except Exception:
            # Fallback на низкий базовый риск
            return 0.05

# Глобальный инстанс для импорта в simulation_engine.py и tasks.py
predictor = MLPredictor()


models_math.py
# production/models_math.py

import random
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional

import numpy as np

from sklearn.linear_model import Ridge
from sklearn.metrics import mean_absolute_percentage_error
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler

from .math_formulas import (
    calculate_p15_50,
    calculate_b2500,
    calculate_magnetic_properties,
    calculate_annealing_quality,
)


class Predictor:
    """
    Финальная математическая модель прогнозирования
    электротехнической стали.

    Поддерживает:
    - NGO
    - GO
    - IEC / ГОСТ / EN / ASTM
    - high-temp annealing
    - recrystallization annealing
    - деградацию при нарушении технологии
    """

    # =====================================================
    # БАЗОВЫЕ КОЭФФИЦИЕНТЫ
    # =====================================================

    P_COEFFS = {
        "a0": 3.15,
        "a1": 1.92,
        "a2": -0.88,
        "a3": 8.10,
        "a4": -0.0021,
    }

    B_COEFFS = {
        "b0": 1.64,
        "b1": 0.064,
        "b2": -0.00011,
    }

    # =====================================================
    # НОРМАЛИЗАЦИЯ ТИПА ОТЖИГА
    # =====================================================

    def normalize_annealing_type(
        self,
        annealing_type: Optional[str]
    ) -> str:

        annealing_type = (
            annealing_type or ""
        ).lower()

        if annealing_type in [
            "high_temp",
            "high_temp_annealing",
            "secondary_recrystallization",
        ]:
            return "high_temp"

        return "recrystallization"

    # =====================================================
    # НОРМАЛИЗАЦИЯ ТИПА СТАЛИ
    # =====================================================

    def normalize_steel_type(
        self,
        steel_type: Optional[str],
        si: float,
    ) -> str:

        if steel_type:

            steel_type = (
                steel_type.upper().strip()
            )

            if steel_type in ["GO", "NGO"]:
                return steel_type

        # Автоопределение

        if si >= 3.0:
            return "GO"

        return "NGO"

    # =====================================================
    # ГЛАВНЫЙ ПРОГНОЗ
    # =====================================================

    def predict_properties(
        self,
        thickness: float,
        si: float,
        c: float = 0.005,
        temp: float = 840.0,
        h2: float = 0.0005,
        n2: float = 0.006,
        weight: float = 18.5,
        wi: float = 1200.0,
        annealing_type: str = "recrystallization",
        steel_type: str = "NGO",
        grain_size: float = 1.0,
        texture_factor: float = 1.0,
        cooling_rate: float = 18.0,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        # =================================================
        # НОРМАЛИЗАЦИЯ
        # =================================================

        thickness = max(
            0.18,
            min(float(thickness), 1.20)
        )

        si = max(
            0.8,
            min(float(si), 4.5)
        )

        c = max(
            0.0001,
            min(float(c), 0.03)
        )

        temp = max(
            650.0,
            min(float(temp), 1250.0)
        )

        h2 = max(
            0.00001,
            min(float(h2), 0.05)
        )

        n2 = max(
            0.0001,
            min(float(n2), 0.99)
        )

        weight = max(
            1.0,
            min(float(weight), 45.0)
        )

        wi = max(
            100.0,
            min(float(wi), 5000.0)
        )

        grain_size = max(
            0.2,
            min(float(grain_size), 6.0)
        )

        texture_factor = max(
            0.5,
            min(float(texture_factor), 2.0)
        )

        cooling_rate = max(
            1.0,
            min(float(cooling_rate), 120.0)
        )

        steel_type = self.normalize_steel_type(
            steel_type,
            si,
        )

        annealing_type = (
            self.normalize_annealing_type(
                annealing_type
            )
        )

        # =================================================
        # БАЗОВЫЕ РАСЧЕТЫ
        # =================================================

        p_clean = calculate_p15_50(
            thickness=thickness,
            si=si,
            c=c,
            temp=temp,
            h2=h2,
            annealing_type=annealing_type,
            steel_type=steel_type,
            cooling_rate=cooling_rate,
            grain_size=grain_size,
            texture_factor=texture_factor,
        )

        b_clean = calculate_b2500(
            thickness=thickness,
            si=si,
            temp=temp,
            h2=h2,
            annealing_type=annealing_type,
            steel_type=steel_type,
            grain_size=grain_size,
            texture_factor=texture_factor,
        )

        # =================================================
        # КАЧЕСТВО ОТЖИГА
        # =================================================

        annealing_quality = (
            calculate_annealing_quality(
                temp=temp,
                h2=h2,
                annealing_type=annealing_type,
                cooling_rate=cooling_rate,
            )
        )

        # =================================================
        # ФИНАЛЬНАЯ КОРРЕКЦИЯ
        # =================================================

        p_final, b_final = (
            calculate_magnetic_properties(
                base_p=p_clean,
                base_b=b_clean,
                quality=annealing_quality,
                h2_percent=h2,
                temp=temp,
                annealing_type=annealing_type,
            )
        )

        # =================================================
        # ТОЛЩИНА
        # =================================================

        if thickness <= 0.30:

            p_final *= 0.93
            b_final *= 1.015

        elif thickness >= 0.50:

            p_final *= 1.07
            b_final *= 0.985

        # =================================================
        # SI
        # =================================================

        if si >= 3.35:

            p_final *= 0.92
            b_final *= 1.025

        elif si <= 2.70:

            p_final *= 1.10
            b_final *= 0.97

        # =================================================
        # УГЛЕРОД
        # =================================================

        if c > 0.008:

            p_final *= 1.12

        elif c < 0.002:

            p_final *= 0.97

        # =================================================
        # H2
        # =================================================

        if h2 >= 0.003:

            p_final *= 0.96
            b_final *= 1.01

        elif h2 <= 0.0002:

            p_final *= 1.05

        # =================================================
        # N2
        # =================================================

        if n2 >= 0.03:

            p_final *= 1.04
            b_final *= 0.99

        # =================================================
        # GO
        # =================================================

        if steel_type == "GO":

            p_final *= 0.84
            b_final *= 1.08

        # =================================================
        # ДОПОЛНИТЕЛЬНЫЕ СВОЙСТВА
        # =================================================

        if steel_type == "GO":

            p10_400 = round(
                p_final * random.uniform(4.9, 5.5),
                2
            )

            b5000 = round(
                b_final * random.uniform(1.08, 1.12),
                3
            )

            b10000 = round(
                b5000 * random.uniform(1.05, 1.08),
                3
            )

            anisotropy = round(
                random.uniform(0.7, 3.2),
                1
            )

        else:

            p10_400 = round(
                p_final * random.uniform(5.6, 6.3),
                2
            )

            b5000 = round(
                b_final * random.uniform(1.04, 1.08),
                3
            )

            b10000 = round(
                b5000 * random.uniform(1.05, 1.09),
                3
            )

            anisotropy = round(
                random.uniform(2.5, 7.0),
                1
            )

        # =================================================
        # ФИЗИЧЕСКИЕ ГРАНИЦЫ
        # =================================================

        if steel_type == "GO":

            p_final = max(
                0.68,
                min(float(p_final), 2.8)
            )

            b_final = max(
                1.72,
                min(float(b_final), 2.15)
            )

        else:

            p_final = max(
                1.05,
                min(float(p_final), 5.2)
            )

            b_final = max(
                1.45,
                min(float(b_final), 1.98)
            )

        # =================================================
        # РЕКОМЕНДУЕМАЯ ТЕМПЕРАТУРА
        # =================================================

        if steel_type == "GO":

            recommended_temp = max(
                1080,
                temp + 60
            )

        else:

            recommended_temp = max(
                820,
                temp + 25
            )

        # =================================================
        # ПРОГНОЗ МАРКИ
        # =================================================

        probable_grade = "UNKNOWN"

        if steel_type == "GO":

            if p_final <= 1.20:
                probable_grade = "3408"

            elif p_final <= 1.40:
                probable_grade = "3411"

            else:
                probable_grade = "3413"

        else:

            if (
                p_final <= 2.10
                and b_final >= 1.72
            ):
                probable_grade = "2412"

            elif (
                p_final <= 2.80
                and b_final >= 1.66
            ):
                probable_grade = "2413"

            else:
                probable_grade = "2414"

        # =================================================
        # ВЕРОЯТНОСТЬ БРАКА
        # =================================================

        defect_probability = 0.0

        if p_final > 4.0:
            defect_probability += 0.25

        if b_final < 1.55:
            defect_probability += 0.25

        if annealing_quality < 70:
            defect_probability += 0.20

        if c > 0.01:
            defect_probability += 0.12

        defect_probability = round(
            min(defect_probability, 0.95),
            3
        )

        # =================================================
        # RETURN
        # =================================================

        return {

            # --------------------------------------------
            # ОСНОВНОЕ
            # --------------------------------------------

            "p15_50": round(p_final, 3),

            "b2500": round(b_final, 3),

            "p10_400": round(p10_400, 2),

            "b5000": round(b5000, 3),

            "b10000": round(b10000, 3),

            "anisotropy": round(anisotropy, 1),

            # --------------------------------------------
            # CLEAN
            # --------------------------------------------

            "p15_50_clean": round(p_clean, 3),

            "b2500_clean": round(b_clean, 3),

            # --------------------------------------------
            # ТЕХНОЛОГИЯ
            # --------------------------------------------

            "steel_type": steel_type,

            "annealing_type": annealing_type,

            "estimated_annealing_quality": round(
                annealing_quality,
                1
            ),

            "recommended_temp": round(
                recommended_temp,
                1
            ),

            "predicted_grade": probable_grade,

            "defect_probability": defect_probability,

            # --------------------------------------------
            # ВХОДНЫЕ
            # --------------------------------------------

            "input_vector": {

                "thickness": round(thickness, 3),

                "si": round(si, 3),

                "c": round(c, 5),

                "temp": round(temp, 1),

                "h2": round(h2, 5),

                "n2": round(n2, 5),

                "weight": round(weight, 3),

                "wi": round(wi, 1),

                "grain_size": round(
                    grain_size,
                    2
                ),

                "texture_factor": round(
                    texture_factor,
                    2
                ),

                "cooling_rate": round(
                    cooling_rate,
                    1
                ),
            }
        }

    # =====================================================
    # ПРОВЕРКА СТАНДАРТА
    # =====================================================

    def check_gost_compliance(
        self,
        results,
        standard,
    ):

        if not standard:

            return {
                "ok": False,
                "reason": "Стандарт не найден",
            }

        checks = {}

        if (
            standard.p15_50_max is not None
        ):
            checks["p15_50"] = (
                results["p15_50"]
                <= standard.p15_50_max
            )

        if (
            standard.b2500_min is not None
        ):
            checks["b2500"] = (
                results["b2500"]
                >= standard.b2500_min
            )

        if (
            standard.p10_400_max is not None
        ):
            checks["p10_400"] = (
                results["p10_400"]
                <= standard.p10_400_max
            )

        if (
            standard.b5000_min is not None
        ):
            checks["b5000"] = (
                results["b5000"]
                >= standard.b5000_min
            )

        if (
            standard.b10000_min is not None
        ):
            checks["b10000"] = (
                results["b10000"]
                >= standard.b10000_min
            )

        if (
            standard.anisotropy_max is not None
        ):
            checks["anisotropy"] = (
                results["anisotropy"]
                <= standard.anisotropy_max
            )

        final_ok = (
            all(checks.values())
            if checks
            else False
        )

        return {
            "ok": final_ok,
            "checks": checks,
        }

    # =====================================================
    # АВТОКАЛИБРОВКА
    # =====================================================

    def tune_coefficients(
        self,
        accuracy_logs
    ):

        if not accuracy_logs:
            return False

        if accuracy_logs.count() < 30:
            return False

        recent_logs = list(
            accuracy_logs[:1000]
        )

        X = []
        y = []

        for log in recent_logs:

            try:

                if not log.roll:
                    continue

                X.append([

                    float(
                        getattr(
                            log.roll,
                            "thickness",
                            0.35
                        )
                    ),

                    float(
                        getattr(
                            log.roll,
                            "si_content",
                            3.0
                        )
                    ),

                    float(
                        getattr(
                            log.roll,
                            "c_content",
                            0.005
                        )
                    ),

                    float(
                        getattr(
                            log,
                            "actual_temp",
                            850
                        )
                    ),
                ])

                y.append(
                    float(
                        log.actual_p15_50
                        or log.predicted_p15_50
                    )
                )

            except Exception:
                continue

        if len(X) < 25:
            return False

        try:

            X = np.array(X)
            y = np.array(y)

            mask = (
                np.abs(
                    y - np.median(y)
                )
                < 3 * np.std(y)
            )

            X = X[mask]
            y = y[mask]

            scaler = StandardScaler()

            X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)

            model = Ridge(
                alpha=5.0,
                fit_intercept=True
            )

            model.fit(X_scaled, y)

            predictions = model.predict(
                X_scaled
            )

            mape = (
                mean_absolute_percentage_error(
                    y,
                    predictions
                ) * 100
            )

            if mape < 12.0:

                self.P_COEFFS["a0"] = round(
                    float(model.intercept_),
                    4
                )

                for i, key in enumerate([
                    "a1",
                    "a2",
                    "a3",
                    "a4",
                ]):

                    self.P_COEFFS[key] = round(
                        float(model.coef_[i]),
                        4
                    )

                print(
                    f"[Predictor] "
                    f"Калибровка успешна "
                    f"(MAPE={mape:.2f}%)"
                )

                return True

        except Exception as e:

            print(
                f"[Predictor] "
                f"Ошибка калибровки: {e}"
            )

        return False


# =====================================================
# ГЛОБАЛЬНЫЙ PREDICTOR
# =====================================================

predictor = Predictor()


models.py
from django.db import models
from django.utils import timezone
from django.core.validators import MinValueValidator, MaxValueValidator
from django.core.exceptions import ValidationError

class Grade(models.Model):
    """
    Справочник марок стали с эталонными значениями по ГОСТ/НЛМК.
    Сюда входят добавленные поля: B5000, B10000, P1.0/400, анизотропия и плотность.
    """
    name = models.CharField("Марка стали", max_length=50, unique=True)
    description = models.TextField("Описание", blank=True, null=True)
    
    # --- БАЗОВЫЕ ПАРАМЕТРЫ (уже были) ---
    max_p150 = models.FloatField("Макс. потери P1.5/50, Вт/кг")
    min_b2500 = models.FloatField("Мин. индукция B2500, Тл")
    
    STEEL_TYPES = [
    ('NGO', 'Non Grain Oriented'),
    ('GO', 'Grain Oriented'),
    ]
    
    steel_type = models.CharField(
    "Тип электротехнической стали",
    max_length=10,
    choices=STEEL_TYPES,
    default='NGO'
    )

    # --- НОВЫЕ ПОЛЯ (соответствуют твоим ALTER TABLE) ---
    min_b5000 = models.FloatField("Мин. индукция B5000, Тл", null=True, blank=True)
    min_b10000 = models.FloatField("Мин. индукция B10000, Тл", null=True, blank=True)
    max_p10_400 = models.FloatField("Макс. потери P1.0/400, Вт/кг", null=True, blank=True)
    max_anisotropy = models.FloatField("Макс. анизотропия, %", default=10.0)
    density = models.FloatField("Плотность, кг/дм³", null=True, blank=True)
    
    # --- ТЕХНОЛОГИЧЕСКИЕ ТАРГЕТЫ ---
    target_si = models.FloatField("Целевой Кремний (Si), %", null=True, blank=True)
    target_c = models.FloatField("Целевой Углерод (C), %", null=True, blank=True)

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Марка стали"
        verbose_name_plural = "Марки стали"

    def __str__(self):
        return self.name

class Standart(models.Model):
    grade = models.ForeignKey(Grade, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name="Марка стали")
    name = models.CharField("Название ГОСТ/EN", max_length=100)
    thickness = models.FloatField("Толщина, мм")
    p15_50_max = models.FloatField("P1.5/50 макс, Вт/кг")
    b2500_min = models.FloatField("B2500 мин, Тл")

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Стандарт (ГОСТ)"
        verbose_name_plural = "Стандарты (ГОСТы)"

    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.name} ({self.grade.name}, {self.thickness}мм)"

class Order(models.Model):
    order_number = models.CharField(max_length=50, unique=True, verbose_name="Номер заказа")
    target_grade_name = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name="Целевая марка стали") 
    required_thickness = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Требуемая толщина (мм)")
    required_weight = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Требуемая масса (т)")
    
    is_active = models.BooleanField(default=True, verbose_name="Активен")
    is_completed = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name="Завершен")
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

    def __str__(self):
        return f"Заказ {self.order_number} ({self.target_grade_name})"

    def get_ready_weight(self):

        ready_weight = self.rolls.filter(status='Обработан').aggregate(models.Sum('weight'))['weight__sum']
        return round(ready_weight, 1) if ready_weight else 0.0

    def get_progress(self):

        if self.required_weight > 0:
            progress = (self.get_ready_weight() / self.required_weight) * 100
            return round(min(progress, 100), 1)
        return 0.0

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Заказ"
        verbose_name_plural = "Заказы"



from django.db import models

from django.db import models
from django.core.validators import MinValueValidator, MaxValueValidator

# =========================================================
# ROLL
# =========================================================

class Roll(models.Model):

    STATUS_CHOICES = [
        ('queue', 'В очереди'),
        ('processing', 'В обработке'),
        ('inspection', 'На проверке'),
        ('completed', 'Обработан'),
        ('defect', 'Брак'),
        ('error', 'Ошибка'),
    ]

    INCOMING_STATE_CHOICES = [
        ('hot_rolled', 'Горячекатаный'),
        ('pickled', 'После травления'),
        ('cold_rolled', 'После ХП'),
        ('ready_for_annealing', 'Готов к отжигу'),
    ]

    STEEL_TYPES = [
        ('NGO', 'NGO'),
        ('GO', 'GO'),
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # ОСНОВНОЕ
    # =====================================================

    number = models.CharField(
        max_length=50,
        unique=True,
        db_index=True,
        verbose_name="Номер рулона"
    )

    steel_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=10,
        choices=STEEL_TYPES,
        default='NGO',
        db_index=True,
        verbose_name="Тип стали"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # СВЯЗИ
    # =====================================================

    order = models.ForeignKey(
        'Order',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='rolls'
    )

    session = models.ForeignKey(
        'SimulationSession',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='rolls'
    )

    target_grade = models.ForeignKey(
        'Grade',
        on_delete=models.PROTECT,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='target_rolls'
    )

    grade = models.ForeignKey(
        'Grade',
        on_delete=models.PROTECT,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='actual_rolls'
    )

    predicted_grade = models.ForeignKey(
        'Grade',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='predicted_rolls'
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ХИМИЯ
    # =====================================================

    si_content = models.FloatField(
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(5.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Si %"
    )

    c_content = models.FloatField(
        default=0.005,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0001),
            MaxValueValidator(0.1)
        ],
        verbose_name="C %"
    )

    h2_content = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0005,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(0.02)
        ],
        verbose_name="H₂"
    )

    n2_content = models.FloatField(
        default=0.006,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(0.05)
        ],
        verbose_name="N₂"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ГЕОМЕТРИЯ
    # =====================================================

    weight = models.FloatField(
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(1.0),
            MaxValueValidator(50.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Масса, т"
    )

    width = models.FloatField(
        default=1250,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(500),
            MaxValueValidator(2500)
        ],
        verbose_name="Ширина, мм"
    )

    thickness = models.FloatField(
        default=0.35,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.15),
            MaxValueValidator(1.5)
        ],
        db_index=True,
        verbose_name="Толщина, мм"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # МЕТАЛЛУРГИЯ
    # =====================================================

    grain_size = models.FloatField(
        default=18.0,
        verbose_name="Размер зерна"
    )

    texture_factor = models.FloatField(
        default=1.0,
        verbose_name="Texture factor"
    )

    orientation_factor = models.FloatField(
        default=1.0,
        verbose_name="Orientation factor"
    )

    cold_reduction = models.FloatField(
        default=65.0,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(100.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Степень ХП %"
    )

    inhibitor_level = models.FloatField(
        default=1.0,
        verbose_name="Уровень ингибиторов"
    )

    domain_refinement = models.FloatField(
        default=1.0,
        verbose_name="Domain refinement"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # СОСТОЯНИЕ
    # =====================================================

    incoming_state = models.CharField(
        max_length=30,
        choices=INCOMING_STATE_CHOICES,
        default='hot_rolled'
    )

    status = models.CharField(
        max_length=20,
        choices=STATUS_CHOICES,
        default='queue',
        db_index=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ПРОИЗВОДСТВО
    # =====================================================

    has_normalized = models.BooleanField(default=False)

    has_skin_pass = models.BooleanField(default=False)

    current_route_step = models.ForeignKey(
        'RouteStep',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='current_rolls'
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ПРЕДСКАЗАНИЯ
    # =====================================================

    predicted_losses = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_induction = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    simulation_notes = models.TextField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ОТК
    # =====================================================

    is_predicted = models.BooleanField(default=False)

    is_certified = models.BooleanField(default=False)

    certified_at = models.DateTimeField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ДАТЫ
    # =====================================================

    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True)

    # =====================================================
    # META
    # =====================================================

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Рулон"
        verbose_name_plural = "Рулоны"

        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=['number']),
            models.Index(fields=['status']),
            models.Index(fields=['steel_type']),
            models.Index(fields=['thickness']),
            models.Index(fields=['created_at']),
        ]

    # =====================================================
    # METHODS
    # =====================================================

    def __str__(self):

        grade = self.grade.name if self.grade else '-'
        pred = self.predicted_grade.name if self.predicted_grade else '-'

        return (
            f"{self.number} | "
            f"{self.steel_type} | "
            f"h={self.thickness} | "
            f"grade={grade} | "
            f"pred={pred}"
        )

    @property
    def is_go(self):
        return self.steel_type == 'GO'

    @property
    def is_ngo(self):
        return self.steel_type == 'NGO'

    def find_historical_prototype(self):

        return Roll.objects.filter(
            status='completed',
            steel_type=self.steel_type,
            thickness__range=(
                self.thickness - 0.03,
                self.thickness + 0.03
            ),
            si_content__range=(
                self.si_content - 0.10,
                self.si_content + 0.10
            ),
        ).exclude(
            id=self.id
        ).order_by(
            '-created_at'
        ).first()

    def clean(self):

        if self.is_go and self.si_content < 2.8:
            raise ValidationError(
                "GO сталь требует Si >= 2.8%"
            )

        if self.thickness <= 0:
            raise ValidationError(
                "Толщина должна быть > 0"
            )
        
class ProcessMode(models.Model):
    name = models.CharField("Название режима", max_length=100)
    temperature = models.IntegerField("Температура отжига, °C")
    speed = models.FloatField("Скорость линии, м/мин")
    
    duration = models.IntegerField(help_text="Длительность в часах")
    h2_content = models.FloatField("Содержание H2, %", default=75.0)
    n2_content = models.FloatField("Содержание N2, %", default=25.0)

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Режим обработки"
        verbose_name_plural = "Режимы обработки"

    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.name} ({self.temperature}°C, v={self.speed})"

# =========================================================
# SIMULATION RESULT
# =========================================================

class SimulationResult(models.Model):
    """
    Результат симуляции металлургического процесса.

    Поддержка:
    - NGO
    - GO
    - ГОСТ / IEC / EN / ASTM
    - расширенные магнитные свойства
    - контроль ОТК
    - KPI
    - дефекты
    """

    # =====================================================
    # СВЯЗИ
    # =====================================================

    roll = models.ForeignKey(
        'Roll',
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name="simulation_results"
    )

    order = models.ForeignKey(
        'Order',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name="simulation_results"
    )

    mode = models.ForeignKey(
        'ProcessMode',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_grade = models.ForeignKey(
        'Grade',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name="predicted_simulation_results"
    )

    grade = models.ForeignKey(
        'Grade',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name="approved_simulation_results"
    )

    standard = models.ForeignKey(
        'SteelStandard',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='simulation_results'
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ТИП СТАЛИ
    # =====================================================

    steel_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=10,
        choices=[
            ('NGO', 'NGO'),
            ('GO', 'GO'),
        ],
        default='NGO',
        db_index=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # МАРШРУТ
    # =====================================================

    route = models.CharField(
        max_length=50,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        db_index=True
    )

    annealing_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=30,
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ФАКТИЧЕСКИЕ ПАРАМЕТРЫ ПРОЦЕССА
    # =====================================================

    actual_temp = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_h2 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_n2 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    cooling_rate = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    dew_point = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    grain_size = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    texture_factor = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_annealing_quality = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    final_temperature = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ОБЕЗУГЛЕРОЖИВАНИЕ
    # =====================================================

    decarburization_efficiency = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0
    )

    final_c_content = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ПРОГНОЗИРУЕМЫЕ СВОЙСТВА
    # =====================================================

    predicted_p15_50 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_b2500 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_p10_400 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_b5000 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_b10000 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    predicted_anisotropy = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ФАКТИЧЕСКИЕ СВОЙСТВА
    # =====================================================

    actual_p15_50 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_b2500 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_p10_400 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_b5000 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_b10000 = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    actual_anisotropy = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # KPI
    # =====================================================

    final_weight = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    yield_percent = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    energy_consumption = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    process_duration = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    downtime_probability = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0
    )

    defect_probability = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0
    )

    cumulative_risk = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0
    )

    # =====================================================
    # КОНТРОЛЬ КАЧЕСТВА
    # =====================================================

    is_ok = models.BooleanField(
        default=False,
        db_index=True
    )

    gost_ok = models.BooleanField(
        default=False,
        db_index=True
    )

    inspection_status = models.CharField(
        max_length=10,
        choices=[
            ('pending', 'Ожидает проверки'),
            ('approve', 'Одобрено'),
            ('reject', 'Брак'),
            ('retest', 'Повторная проверка'),
        ],
        default='pending',
        db_index=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ДЕФЕКТЫ
    # =====================================================

    is_defect = models.BooleanField(
        default=False,
        db_index=True
    )

    defect_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=100,
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    defect_reason = models.TextField(
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ВРЕМЯ
    # =====================================================

    simulation_time = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now_add=True,
        db_index=True
    )

    processed_at = models.DateTimeField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # СЛУЖЕБНОЕ
    # =====================================================

    notes = models.TextField(
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    inspector_comment = models.TextField(
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # META
    # =====================================================

    class Meta:

        verbose_name = "Результат симуляции"

        verbose_name_plural = (
            "Результаты симуляции"
        )

        ordering = ['-simulation_time']

        indexes = [

            # -----------------------------
            # время
            # -----------------------------

            models.Index(
                fields=['-simulation_time']
            ),

            # -----------------------------
            # статус
            # -----------------------------

            models.Index(
                fields=['inspection_status']
            ),

            models.Index(
                fields=['is_ok']
            ),

            models.Index(
                fields=['gost_ok']
            ),

            models.Index(
                fields=['is_defect']
            ),

            # -----------------------------
            # маршрут
            # -----------------------------

            models.Index(
                fields=['route']
            ),

            models.Index(
                fields=['steel_type']
            ),

            # -----------------------------
            # свойства
            # -----------------------------

            models.Index(
                fields=['actual_p15_50']
            ),

            models.Index(
                fields=['actual_b2500']
            ),
        ]

    # =====================================================
    # STRING
    # =====================================================

    def __str__(self):

        roll_number = (
            self.roll.number
            if self.roll
            else 'UNKNOWN'
        )

        return (
            f"Simulation #{self.pk} | "
            f"{roll_number}"
        )

    # =====================================================
    # FULL OK
    # =====================================================

    @property
    def is_fully_ok(self):

        return (

            self.is_ok

            and self.gost_ok

            and not self.is_defect

            and self.inspection_status
            == 'approve'
        )

    # =====================================================
    # DEFECT STATUS
    # =====================================================

    @property
    def has_critical_defect(self):

        critical_defects = [

            'crack',

            'lamination',

            'overheat',

            'magnetic_failure',

            'surface_defect',
        ]

        return (
            self.is_defect
            and self.defect_type
            in critical_defects
        )

    # =====================================================
    # AUTO SAVE LOGIC
    # =====================================================

    def save(self, *args, **kwargs):
        # -------------------------------------------------
        # STEEL TYPE
        # -------------------------------------------------
        if self.roll:
            self.steel_type = self.roll.steel_type

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # YIELD
        # -------------------------------------------------
        if (
            self.final_weight is not None
            and self.roll
            and self.roll.weight
            and self.roll.weight > 0
        ):
            self.yield_percent = round(
                (self.final_weight / self.roll.weight) * 100,
                2
            )

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # DEFECT LOGIC
        # -------------------------------------------------
        if self.is_defect:
            note = " | Обнаружен технологический риск"
            self.notes = (self.notes or "") + note

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # APPROVE LOGIC (ИСПРАВЛЕНО)
        # -------------------------------------------------
        # Ранее здесь стояло: self.inspection_status = 'approve'
        # Это автоматически одобряло рулоны ДО проверки ОТК.
        # Теперь мы только вычисляем флаг is_ok. Статус остаётся 'pending',
        # пока инспектор или завершённая Celery-задача явно его не изменит.
        if (
            self.gost_ok
            and not self.is_defect
            and self.actual_p15_50 is not None
            and self.actual_b2500 is not None
        ):
            self.is_ok = True
            # inspection_status НЕ ТРОГАЕМ. Он должен оставаться 'pending'.

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # NORMALIZATION
        # -------------------------------------------------
        if self.route:
            self.route = str(self.route).strip().upper()
        if self.annealing_type:
            self.annealing_type = str(self.annealing_type).strip().lower()

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # SAFE LIMITS
        # -------------------------------------------------
        numeric_fields = [
            'actual_p15_50', 'actual_b2500', 'actual_p10_400',
            'actual_b5000', 'actual_b10000', 'predicted_p15_50',
            'predicted_b2500', 'predicted_p10_400', 'predicted_b5000',
            'predicted_b10000', 'actual_anisotropy', 'predicted_anisotropy',
            'yield_percent', 'decarburization_efficiency',
        ]
        for field_name in numeric_fields:
            value = getattr(self, field_name, None)
            if value is not None:
                try:
                    setattr(self, field_name, round(float(value), 4))
                except Exception:
                    setattr(self, field_name, None)

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # FINAL SAVE
        # -------------------------------------------------
        super().save(*args, **kwargs)

class Route(models.Model):
    """
    Технологический маршрут производства
    электротехнической (динамной) стали.

    Используется:
    - для автоматического подбора маршрута,
    - для имитационного моделирования,
    - для digital twin / MES логики.
    """

    ROUTE_TYPES = [
        ('NGO', 'Non Grain Oriented'),
        ('GO', 'Grain Oriented'),
    ]

    ROUTE_CATEGORY = [
        ('standard', 'Стандартный'),
        ('thin', 'Тонкий материал'),
        ('high_si', 'Высококремнистый'),
        ('high_perm', 'Высокая магнитная проницаемость'),
        ('experimental', 'Экспериментальный'),
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # ОСНОВНЫЕ ДАННЫЕ
    # =====================================================

    name = models.CharField(
        "Код маршрута",
        max_length=100,
        unique=True
    )

    title = models.CharField(
        "Название маршрута",
        max_length=255
    )

    description = models.TextField(
        "Описание маршрута",
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    steel_type = models.CharField(
        "Тип электротехнической стали",
        max_length=10,
        choices=ROUTE_TYPES,
        default='NGO'
    )

    category = models.CharField(
        "Категория маршрута",
        max_length=30,
        choices=ROUTE_CATEGORY,
        default='standard'
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ТЕХНОЛОГИЧЕСКИЕ ОГРАНИЧЕНИЯ
    # =====================================================

    min_thickness = models.FloatField(
        "Минимальная толщина (мм)",
        help_text="Включительно"
    )

    max_thickness = models.FloatField(
        "Максимальная толщина (мм)",
        help_text="Включительно"
    )

    min_si = models.FloatField(
        "Минимальное содержание Si (%)",
        default=2.4
    )

    max_si = models.FloatField(
        "Максимальное содержание Si (%)",
        default=3.8
    )

    target_temperature = models.FloatField(
        "Целевая температура отжига (°C)",
        default=850
    )

    target_h2 = models.FloatField(
        "Целевое содержание H₂ (%)",
        default=5.0
    )

    target_n2 = models.FloatField(
        "Целевое содержание N₂ (%)",
        default=95.0
    )

    target_reduction = models.FloatField(
        "Целевая степень обжатия (%)",
        default=65.0
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ПРОИЗВОДСТВЕННЫЕ KPI
    # =====================================================

    expected_yield = models.FloatField(
        "Ожидаемый yield (%)",
        default=96.0
    )

    expected_oee = models.FloatField(
        "Ожидаемый OEE (%)",
        default=85.0
    )

    expected_scrap_rate = models.FloatField(
        "Ожидаемый уровень брака (%)",
        default=2.5
    )

    expected_energy = models.FloatField(
        "Ожидаемое энергопотребление (кВт⋅ч)",
        default=1200
    )

    # =====================================================
    # СИСТЕМНЫЕ ПАРАМЕТРЫ
    # =====================================================

    is_active = models.BooleanField(
        "Активен",
        default=True
    )

    created_at = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now_add=True
    )

    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # META
    # =====================================================

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Технологический маршрут"
        verbose_name_plural = "Технологические маршруты"

        ordering = [
            'steel_type',
            'category',
            'min_thickness'
        ]

    # =====================================================
    # STRING
    # =====================================================
    def get_steps(self):
        """Безопасный способ получения шагов маршрута"""
        try:
            return self.route_steps.all().order_by('order')
        except AttributeError:
            # Fallback, если related_name не сработал
            from .models import RouteStep
            return RouteStep.objects.filter(route=self).order_by('order')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Маршрут"
        verbose_name_plural = "Маршруты"
        
    def __str__(self):

        return (
            f"{self.name} | "
            f"{self.steel_type} | "
            f"{self.min_thickness}–{self.max_thickness} мм"
        )

    # =====================================================
    # HELPERS
    # =====================================================

    @property
    def route_steps_count(self):
        return self.route_steps.count()

    @property
    def average_duration(self):

        total = self.route_steps.aggregate(
            total=models.Sum('planned_duration')
        )['total']

        return total or 0

    @property
    def is_go(self):
        return self.steel_type == 'GO'

    @property
    def is_ngo(self):
        return self.steel_type == 'NGO'
    
class SteelGradeReference(models.Model):
    """
    Эталонные (нормативные) значения для марок динамной стали по ГОСТ.
    Одна запись = одна комбинация "марка + толщина".
    """

    grade_name = models.CharField(
        "Марка стали", 
        max_length=50,
        help_text="Например: 2412, 2413, 3408 и т.д."
    )

    thickness = models.FloatField(
        "Толщина, мм",
        help_text="Толщина рулона, для которой действуют данные нормативы"
    )

    # === Основные магнитные характеристики ===
    p15_50_max = models.FloatField(
        "P1.5/50 максимум, Вт/кг",
        help_text="Максимально допустимые магнитные потери"
    )
    b2500_min = models.FloatField(
        "B2500 минимум, Тл",
        help_text="Минимально допустимая магнитная индукция"
    )

    # === Расширенные магнитные характеристики ===
    p10_400_max = models.FloatField(
        "P1.0/400 максимум, Вт/кг",
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text="Максимальные потери на высоких частотах"
    )
    b5000_min = models.FloatField(
        "B5000 минимум, Тл",
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )
    b10000_min = models.FloatField(
        "B10000 минимум, Тл",
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )
    max_anisotropy = models.FloatField(
        "Максимальная анизотропия, %",
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text="Допустимый уровень анизотропии"
    )

    # === Дополнительная информация ===
    class_type = models.CharField(
        "Класс стали",
        max_length=10,
        choices=[('1', '1 класс'), ('2', '2 класс')],
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text="Класс по ГОСТ (1 - высший, 2 - первый)"
    )

    standard = models.CharField(
        "Стандарт",
        max_length=50,
        default="ГОСТ 21427.2-83",
        help_text="Нормативный документ"
    )

    description = models.TextField(
        "Описание / примечание",
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    # === Технические поля ===
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
