    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True)

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Эталон марки стали"
        verbose_name_plural = "Эталоны марок стали"
        unique_together = ('grade_name', 'thickness')   # одна запись на марку + толщину
        ordering = ['grade_name', 'thickness']
        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=['grade_name']),
            models.Index(fields=['thickness']),
        ]

    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.grade_name} ({self.thickness} мм) — P1.5/50 ≤ {self.p15_50_max}"

    @property
    def full_name(self):
        return f"{self.grade_name} ({self.thickness} мм)"
    
class ModelAccuracyLog(models.Model):
    order = models.ForeignKey(
        'Order', 
        on_delete=models.CASCADE, 
        null=True, 
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Заказ"
    )
    roll = models.ForeignKey(
        'Roll', 
        on_delete=models.CASCADE, 
        null=True, 
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Рулон"
    )

    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now_add=True, 
        verbose_name="Дата расчёта"
    )

    
    predicted_p = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Прогноз P1.5/50")
    actual_p = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Факт P1.5/50")
    predicted_b = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Прогноз B2500")
    actual_b = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Факт B2500")

    
    mae_p = models.FloatField(
        verbose_name="MAE по P1.5/50", 
        null=True, 
        blank=True
    )
    mape_p = models.FloatField(
        verbose_name="MAPE по P1.5/50 (%)", 
        null=True, 
        blank=True
    )

    is_ok = models.BooleanField(
        default=False, 
        verbose_name="Соответствует ГОСТ"
    )

    notes = models.TextField(
        blank=True, 
        null=True, 
        verbose_name="Примечание"
    )

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Лог точности модели"
        verbose_name_plural = "Логи точности модели"
        ordering = ['-timestamp']

    def __str__(self):
        return f"Лог {self.id} — {self.timestamp.strftime('%d.%m.%Y %H:%M')}"

    @property
    def error_p_percent(self):
        
        if self.actual_p and self.actual_p != 0:
            return round(abs((self.predicted_p - self.actual_p) / self.actual_p) * 100, 2)
        return None

    @property
    def error_b_percent(self):
       
        if self.actual_b and self.actual_b != 0:
            return round(abs((self.predicted_b - self.actual_b) / self.actual_b) * 100, 2)
        return None

class SimulationLog(models.Model):
    order = models.ForeignKey('Order', on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name="Заказ")
    roll = models.ForeignKey('Roll', on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name="Рулон")
    hour = models.IntegerField(verbose_name="Час симуляции")
    
    temp = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Температура в этот час")
    current_weight = models.FloatField(verbose_name="Текущий вес")
    
    p150 = models.FloatField(verbose_name="P1.5/50 (прогноз)")
    b2500 = models.FloatField(verbose_name="B2500 (прогноз)")
    
    is_downtime = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name="Был простой")
    is_defect = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name="Был брак")
    
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['hour']
        verbose_name = "Лог симуляции"
        verbose_name_plural = "Логи симуляции"

    def __str__(self):
        return f"Лог {self.roll.number} | Час {self.hour}"

class Defect(models.Model):
    DEFECT_TYPES = [
        ("surface", "Дефект поверхности"),
        ("magnetic", "Несоответствие магнитных свойств"),
        ("geometry", "Нарушение геометрии"),
        ("edge", "Повреждение кромки"),
        ("adhesion", "Слипание витков"),
        ("overheat", "Перегрев"),
        ("crack", "Трещина"),
        ("other", "Другой дефект"),
        ('bad_texture', 'Нарушение текстуры Госса'),
        ('secondary_recrystallization_failure', 'Срыв вторичной рекристаллизации'),
        ('decarburization_failure', 'Недостаточное обезуглероживание'),
        ('abnormal_grain_growth', 'Аномальный рост зерна'),
        ('edge_crack', 'Кромочная трещина'),
        ('coil_break', 'Обрыв полосы'),
        ('coating_delamination', 'Отслоение покрытия'),
        ('goss_texture_failure', 'Разрушение текстуры Госса'),
        ('grain_instability', 'Нестабильность зерна'),
        ('high_core_loss', 'Высокие удельные потери'),
        ('low_induction', 'Низкая магнитная индукция'),

    ]

    REASONS = [
        ("technology", "Нарушение технологии"),
        ("equipment", "Оборудование"),
        ("raw_material", "Сырьё / подкат"),
        ("operator", "Человеческий фактор"),
        ("unknown", "Неизвестно"),
    ]

    roll = models.ForeignKey(
        'Roll', 
        on_delete=models.CASCADE, 
        related_name='defects',
        verbose_name="Рулон"
    )
    
    defect_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=100, 
        choices=DEFECT_TYPES, 
        verbose_name="Тип дефекта"
    )
    
    reason = models.CharField(
        max_length=20, 
        choices=REASONS, 
        verbose_name="Причина"
    )
    
    weight_loss = models.FloatField(
        verbose_name="Потери веса (кг)", 
        default=0.0
    )
    
    inspector_comment = models.TextField(
        "Комментарий инспектора", 
        blank=True, 
        null=True
    )
    
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
    created_by = models.ForeignKey(
        'auth.User', 
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL, 
        null=True, 
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Инспектор"
    )

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Дефект"
        verbose_name_plural = "Дефекты"
        ordering = ['-created_at']

    def __str__(self):
        return f"Дефект {self.get_defect_type_display()} — Рулон {self.roll.number}"



# =========================================================
# ROUTE STEP
# =========================================================

class RouteStep(models.Model):

    STEP_TYPES = [
        ('incoming', 'Поступление'),
        ('preparation', 'Подготовка'),
        ('pickling', 'Травление'),
        ('cold_rolling', 'Холодная прокатка'),

        ('decarburizing_annealing', 'Обезуглероживающий отжиг'),

        ('primary_annealing', 'Первичный отжиг'),
        ('secondary_recrystallization', 'Вторичная рекристаллизация'),
        ('laser_treatment', 'Лазерная обработка'),

        ('coating', 'Нанесение покрытия'),
        ('skin_pass', 'Дрессировка'),
        ('inspection', 'Инспекция'),
        ('otk', 'Контроль качества'),
    ]

    STEP_STATUS = [
        ('template', 'Шаблон'),
        ('queue', 'В очереди'),
        ('processing', 'В обработке'),
        ('done', 'Завершён'),
        ('defect', 'Брак'),
        ('skipped', 'Пропущен'),
    ]

    route = models.ForeignKey(
        'Route',
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='steps'
    )

    roll = models.ForeignKey(
        'Roll',
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='route_steps',
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    equipment = models.ForeignKey(
        'Equipment',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='route_steps'
    )

    step_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=50,
        choices=STEP_TYPES
    )

    order = models.PositiveIntegerField(
        default=1
    )

    status = models.CharField(
        max_length=20,
        choices=STEP_STATUS,
        default='template'
    )

    planned_duration = models.PositiveIntegerField(
        default=8,
        help_text='Плановая длительность этапа (часы)'
    )

    actual_duration = models.PositiveIntegerField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text='Фактическая длительность этапа (часы)'
    )

    queue_time = models.PositiveIntegerField(
        default=0,
        help_text='Время ожидания в очереди (часы)'
    )

    started_at = models.DateTimeField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    finished_at = models.DateTimeField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    temperature = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text='Температура процесса °C'
    )

    h2_content = models.FloatField(
        default=5.0,
        help_text='Содержание H2 (%)'
    )

    n2_content = models.FloatField(
        default=95.0,
        help_text='Содержание N2 (%)'
    )

    reduction_percent = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text='Обжатие (%)'
    )

    cooling_rate = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        help_text='Скорость охлаждения °C/ч'
    )

    defect_probability = models.FloatField(
        default=0.03
    )

    defect_detected = models.BooleanField(
        default=False
    )

    defect_reason = models.TextField(
        null=True,
        blank=True
    )

    energy_consumption = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0,
        help_text='Потребление энергии'
    )

    notes = models.TextField(
        blank=True,
        null=True
    )

    created_at = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now_add=True
    )

    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now=True
    )

    class Meta:

        ordering = ['route', 'order']

        unique_together = (
            'route',
            'order',
        )

        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=['route', 'order']),
            models.Index(fields=['status']),
            models.Index(fields=['step_type']),
            models.Index(fields=['started_at']),
            models.Index(fields=['finished_at']),
        ]

        verbose_name = 'Этап маршрута'
        verbose_name_plural = 'Этапы маршрутов'

    def __str__(self):

        return (
            f"{self.route.name} | "
            f"{self.order}. "
            f"{self.get_step_type_display()}"
        )

    # =====================================================
    # PROPERTIES
    # =====================================================

    @property
    def is_finished(self):
        return self.status == 'done'

    @property
    def is_processing(self):
        return self.status == 'processing'

    @property
    def is_defect_step(self):
        return (
            self.status == 'defect'
            or self.defect_detected
        )

    @property
    def duration_hours(self):

        if self.started_at and self.finished_at:

            delta = (
                self.finished_at
                - self.started_at
            )

            return round(
                delta.total_seconds() / 3600,
                2
            )

        return (
            self.actual_duration
            or self.planned_duration
        )

    # =====================================================
    # VALIDATION
    # =====================================================

    def clean(self):

        errors = {}

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # H2 / N2
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if self.h2_content < 0:
            errors['h2_content'] = (
                'H2 не может быть отрицательным.'
            )

        if self.n2_content < 0:
            errors['n2_content'] = (
                'N2 не может быть отрицательным.'
            )

        total_gas = (
            float(self.h2_content or 0)
            + float(self.n2_content or 0)
        )

        if total_gas <= 0:
            errors['h2_content'] = (
                'Сумма газов должна быть > 0.'
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # TEMPERATURE
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if (
            self.temperature is not None
            and (
                self.temperature < 0
                or self.temperature > 1400
            )
        ):

            errors['temperature'] = (
                'Температура вне допустимого диапазона.'
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # DEFECT PROBABILITY
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if not (
            0 <= self.defect_probability <= 1
        ):

            errors['defect_probability'] = (
                'Вероятность дефекта должна быть от 0 до 1.'
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # DURATION
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if self.planned_duration <= 0:

            errors['planned_duration'] = (
                'Плановая длительность должна быть > 0.'
            )

        if (
            self.actual_duration is not None
            and self.actual_duration < 0
        ):

            errors['actual_duration'] = (
                'Фактическая длительность не может быть отрицательной.'
            )

        if errors:
            raise ValidationError(errors)

    # =====================================================
    # SAVE
    # =====================================================

    def save(self, *args, **kwargs):

        self.h2_content = float(
            self.h2_content or 0
        )

        self.n2_content = float(
            self.n2_content or 0
        )

        total = (
            self.h2_content
            + self.n2_content
        )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # NORMALIZE GASES
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if total > 0:

            if total != 100.0:

                self.h2_content = round(
                    (self.h2_content / total) * 100,
                    4
                )

                self.n2_content = round(
                    (self.n2_content / total) * 100,
                    4
                )

        else:

            self.h2_content = 5.0
            self.n2_content = 95.0

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # DEFECT STATUS
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if self.defect_detected:
            self.status = 'defect'

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # AUTO FINISH
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if (
            self.started_at
            and self.finished_at
            and self.status != 'defect'
        ):
            self.status = 'done'

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # ACTUAL DURATION
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if (
            self.started_at
            and self.finished_at
        ):

            delta = (
                self.finished_at
                - self.started_at
            )

            hours = max(
                1,
                round(
                    delta.total_seconds() / 3600
                )
            )

            self.actual_duration = hours

        self.full_clean()

        super().save(*args, **kwargs)
    
    def get_effective_duration(self):
        """Возвращает реалистичную длительность шага для симуляции (в часах)"""
        if self.planned_duration and self.planned_duration > 0:
            # Ограничиваем максимальную длительность шага для симуляции
            return min(int(self.planned_duration), 3)   # максимум 3 часа на шаг
        return 1
    
class RollState(models.Model):
    def __init__(self, roll):
        self.roll = roll
        self.current_weight = float(roll.weight)
        self.current_temp = 0.0
        self.hour = 0
        self.stage = "Нагрев"          # Нагрев → Выдержка → Охлаждение
        self.cumulative_defect_risk = 0.0   # накопленный риск
        self.is_defect = False
        self.defect_reason = None
        self.p15_50_history = []
        self.b2500_history = []


class SimulationSession(models.Model):
    STATUS_CHOICES = [
        ('idle', 'Ожидание'),
        ('running', 'Запущена'),
        ('completed', 'Завершена'),
        ('failed', 'Ошибка'),
    ]

     
    SCENARIO_CHOICES = [
        ('standard', 'Стандартный режим'),
        ('stress_test', 'Стресс-тест (высокий углерод)'),
        ('unstable_process', 'Нестабильный процесс (колебания кремния)'),
    ]

    start_time = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True, verbose_name="Время начала")
    end_time = models.DateTimeField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="Время окончания")
    max_rolls = models.PositiveIntegerField(default=500)
    status = models.CharField(
        max_length=20, 
        choices=STATUS_CHOICES, 
        default='idle',
        verbose_name="Статус"
    )
    
     
    scenario_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=50, 
        choices=SCENARIO_CHOICES, 
        default='standard',
        verbose_name="Тип сценария"
    )
    
     
    tick_interval = models.FloatField(
        default=1.0, 
        help_text="Задержка между шагами в секундах",
        verbose_name="Интервал тика"
    )
    
    notes = models.TextField(
        blank=True, 
        null=True, 
        verbose_name="Примечания"
    )
    total_rolls = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name="Всего рулонов")
    processed_rolls = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name="Обработано рулонов")

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Сессия симуляции"
        verbose_name_plural = "Сессии симуляции"

    def __str__(self):
        return f"Сессия {self.id} | {self.get_scenario_type_display()} | {self.status}"
    

class GlobalSettings(models.Model):
    """
    Глобальные коэффициенты математической модели.
    Позволяют менять логику симуляции без правки кода.
    """
    carbon_impact_factor = models.FloatField(
        "Коэффициент влияния углерода", 
        default=5.0,
        help_text="Множитель для c_content в формуле потерь (P1.5/50)"
    )
    silicon_stability_factor = models.FloatField(
        "Коэффициент стабильности кремния", 
        default=1.0,
        help_text="Поправка на чистоту Si"
    )
    monte_carlo_iterations = models.IntegerField(
        "Количество прогонов Монте-Карло", 
        default=100
    )
    
    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Настройки модели"
        verbose_name_plural = "Настройки модели"

    def __str__(self):
        return "Глобальные настройки"

    @classmethod
    def get_settings(cls):
        """Метод для получения настроек (всегда возвращает одну строку)"""
        obj, created = cls.objects.get_or_create(pk=1)
        return obj
    

class SimulationStep(models.Model):
    """Полный шаг имитационной модели с отслеживанием состояния и событий"""
    
    simulation_result = models.ForeignKey(
        'SimulationResult',
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='steps',
        null=True,      # ← временно оставляем
        blank=True
    )
    roll = models.ForeignKey(
        'Roll', 
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        verbose_name="Рулон"
    )
    route_step = models.ForeignKey(
        'RouteStep', 
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL, 
        null=True, 
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Шаг маршрута"
    )
    is_downtime = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name="Был простой")
    # === Время и этап ===
    hour = models.IntegerField(verbose_name="Час симуляции")
    stage = models.CharField(
        max_length=120, 
        verbose_name="Этап процесса",
        default="Unknown"                    # важно для существующих данных
    )

    # === Параметры процесса ===
    temperature = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0,
        verbose_name="Температура (°C)"
    )

    # Отслеживание массы (критично для логирования потерь)
    weight_before = models.FloatField(
        null=True, 
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Вес до шага (т)"
    )
    weight_after = models.FloatField(
        null=True, 
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Вес после шага (т)"
    )
    weight_delta = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0,
        verbose_name="Потеря веса (т)"
    )

    # === Магнитные свойства на конец шага ===
    p15_50 = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="P1.5/50")
    b2500 = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="B2500")
    p10_400 = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="P1.0/400")
    b5000 = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="B5000")
    b10000 = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="B10000")
    anisotropy = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="Анизотропия (%)")

    # === События и качество ===
    has_event = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name="Было событие")
    
    event_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=50,
        blank=True,
        choices=[
            ('normal', 'Нормальный процесс'),
            ('incident', 'Инцидент'),
            ('defect', 'Обнаружен брак'),
            ('quality_drop', 'Падение качества'),
        ],
        verbose_name="Тип события"
    )
    event_description = models.TextField(blank=True, verbose_name="Описание события")

    is_defect = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name="Брак на шаге")
    defect_type = models.CharField(max_length=100, blank=True, verbose_name="Тип брака")

    annealing_quality = models.FloatField(
        default=100.0,
        verbose_name="Качество отжига (%)"
    )

    notes = models.TextField(blank=True, verbose_name="Дополнительные замечания")

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['simulation_result', 'hour']
        verbose_name = "Шаг симуляции"
        verbose_name_plural = "Шаги симуляции"
        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=['simulation_result', 'hour']),
            models.Index(fields=['is_defect']),
        ]

    def __str__(self):
        return f"Шаг {self.hour} | {self.stage} | {self.roll.number}"
    
    @property
    def weight_loss_percent(self):
        if self.weight_before and self.weight_before > 0:
            return round((self.weight_delta / self.weight_before) * 100, 2)
        return 0.0

class SimulationEvent(models.Model):
    """Отдельная сущность событий для event-driven имитационной модели"""

    simulation_result = models.ForeignKey(
        'SimulationResult',
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name='events',
        verbose_name="Результат симуляции"
    )
    
    step = models.ForeignKey(
        'SimulationStep',
        on_delete=models.SET_NULL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        related_name='events',
        verbose_name="Связанный шаг симуляции"
    )

    # === Время события ===
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now_add=True,
        verbose_name="Время события"
    )

    # === Тип и описание события ===
    event_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=50,
        choices=[
            ('normal', 'Нормальное течение процесса'),
            ('incident', 'Технологический инцидент'),
            ('defect', 'Обнаружен брак'),
            ('quality_drop', 'Снижение качества'),
            ('parameter_change', 'Изменение параметра'),
            ('stage_complete', 'Завершение этапа'),
        ],
        verbose_name="Тип события"
    )

    name = models.CharField(
        max_length=200,
        verbose_name="Название события"
    )

    description = models.TextField(
        blank=True,
        verbose_name="Подробное описание"
    )

    # === Влияние события ===
    impact = models.CharField(
        max_length=50,
        choices=[
            ('delay', 'Задержка'),
            ('quality', 'Снижение качества'),
            ('scrap', 'Брак / Потеря материала'),
            ('info', 'Информационное'),
            ('critical', 'Критическое'),
        ],
        default='info',
        verbose_name="Влияние"
    )

    # === Количественные параметры ===
    delay_hours = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0,
        verbose_name="Задержка (часов)"
    )

    probability = models.FloatField(
        default=0.0,
        verbose_name="Вероятность возникновения"
    )

    # === Дополнительные данные ===
    value_before = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="Значение до")
    value_after = models.FloatField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="Значение после")

    notes = models.TextField(blank=True, verbose_name="Дополнительные заметки")

    class Meta:
        ordering = ['-timestamp', 'simulation_result']
        verbose_name = "Событие симуляции"
        verbose_name_plural = "События симуляции"
        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=['simulation_result', '-timestamp']),
            models.Index(fields=['event_type']),
            models.Index(fields=['impact']),
        ]

    def __str__(self):
        return f"[{self.get_event_type_display() or self.event_type}] {self.name} — {self.simulation_result.roll.number}"

    @property
    def is_critical(self):
        return self.impact in ['scrap', 'critical']
    

class Equipment(models.Model):

    EQUIPMENT_TYPES = [
        ('pickling', 'Травление'),
        ('cold_rolling', 'Холодная прокатка'),
        ('annealing', 'Отжиг'),
        ('coating', 'Нанесение покрытия'),
        ('skin_pass', 'Дрессировка'),
        ('laser', 'Лазерная обработка'),
        ('inspection', 'Инспекция'),
    ]

    name = models.CharField(
        "Название агрегата",
        max_length=100
    )

    equipment_type = models.CharField(
        "Тип агрегата",
        max_length=30,
        choices=EQUIPMENT_TYPES
    )

    capacity_tph = models.FloatField(
        "Производительность (т/ч)",
        default=20.0
    )

    queue_limit = models.IntegerField(
        "Лимит очереди",
        default=5
    )

    is_busy = models.BooleanField(
        "Занят",
        default=False
    )

    base_process_time = models.IntegerField(
        "Базовое время обработки (мин)",
        default=60
    )

    defect_probability = models.FloatField(
        "Вероятность брака",
        default=0.03,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(1.0)
        ]
    )

    is_active = models.BooleanField(
        default=True
    )

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Оборудование"
        verbose_name_plural = "Оборудование"

    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.name}"
    

class SteelStandard(models.Model):
    """
    ГОСТ / IEC / ASTM стандарт
    для электротехнической стали.
    """

    STANDARD_TYPES = [
        ('GOST', 'ГОСТ'),
        ('IEC', 'IEC'),
        ('EN', 'EN'),
        ('ASTM', 'ASTM'),
        ('JIS', 'JIS'),
    ]

    STEEL_TYPES = [
        ('NGO', 'NGO'),
        ('GO', 'GO'),
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # ОСНОВНОЕ
    # =====================================================

    name = models.CharField(
        max_length=120,
        unique=True,
        verbose_name="Название стандарта"
    )

    standard_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=20,
        choices=STANDARD_TYPES,
        default='IEC',
        verbose_name="Тип стандарта"
    )

    steel_type = models.CharField(
        max_length=10,
        choices=STEEL_TYPES,
        default='NGO',
        verbose_name="Тип стали"
    )

    description = models.TextField(
        blank=True,
        null=True,
        verbose_name="Описание"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # P1.5/50
    # =====================================================

    p15_50_max = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(20.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Макс P1.5/50"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # B2500
    # =====================================================

    b2500_min = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(3.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Мин B2500"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # P1.0/400
    # =====================================================

    p10_400_max = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(50.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Макс P1.0/400"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # B5000
    # =====================================================

    b5000_min = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(3.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Мин B5000"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # B10000
    # =====================================================

    b10000_min = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(3.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Мин B10000"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # АНИЗОТРОПИЯ
    # =====================================================

    anisotropy_max = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(100.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Макс анизотропия"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ХИМИЯ
    # =====================================================

    si_min = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(10.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Мин Si %"
    )

    si_max = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(10.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Макс Si %"
    )

    c_max = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(1.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Макс C %"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # ГЕОМЕТРИЯ
    # =====================================================

    thickness_min = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(5.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Мин толщина"
    )

    thickness_max = models.FloatField(
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        validators=[
            MinValueValidator(0.0),
            MaxValueValidator(5.0)
        ],
        verbose_name="Макс толщина"
    )

    # =====================================================
    # СЛУЖЕБНОЕ
    # =====================================================

    is_active = models.BooleanField(
        default=True,
        verbose_name="Активен"
    )

    created_at = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now_add=True
    )

    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(
        auto_now=True
    )

    # =====================================================
    # META
    # =====================================================

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = "Стандарт электротехнической стали"
        verbose_name_plural = "Стандарты электротехнической стали"

        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=['name']),
            models.Index(fields=['standard_type']),
            models.Index(fields=['steel_type']),
            models.Index(fields=['is_active']),
        ]

    # =====================================================
    # STRING
    # =====================================================

    def __str__(self):

        return (
            f"{self.name} | "
            f"{self.standard_type} | "
            f"{self.steel_type}"
        )

    # =====================================================
    # ПРОВЕРКА СООТВЕТСТВИЯ
    # =====================================================

    def check_properties(
        self,
        p15_50=None,
        b2500=None,
        p10_400=None,
        b5000=None,
        b10000=None,
        anisotropy=None,
        thickness=None,
        si=None,
        c=None
    ):
        """
        Проверка соответствия стандарту.
        """

        checks = []

        # =========================================
        # P15/50
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.p15_50_max is not None
            and p15_50 is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(p15_50)
                <= self.p15_50_max
            )

        # =========================================
        # B2500
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.b2500_min is not None
            and b2500 is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(b2500)
                >= self.b2500_min
            )

        # =========================================
        # P10/400
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.p10_400_max is not None
            and p10_400 is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(p10_400)
                <= self.p10_400_max
            )

        # =========================================
        # B5000
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.b5000_min is not None
            and b5000 is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(b5000)
                >= self.b5000_min
            )

        # =========================================
        # B10000
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.b10000_min is not None
            and b10000 is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(b10000)
                >= self.b10000_min
            )

        # =========================================
        # АНИЗОТРОПИЯ
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.anisotropy_max is not None
            and anisotropy is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(anisotropy)
                <= self.anisotropy_max
            )

        # =========================================
        # ТОЛЩИНА
        # =========================================

        if thickness is not None:

            if self.thickness_min is not None:
                checks.append(
                    float(thickness)
                    >= self.thickness_min
                )

            if self.thickness_max is not None:
                checks.append(
                    float(thickness)
                    <= self.thickness_max
                )

        # =========================================
        # SI
        # =========================================

        if si is not None:

            if self.si_min is not None:
                checks.append(
                    float(si)
                    >= self.si_min
                )

            if self.si_max is not None:
                checks.append(
                    float(si)
                    <= self.si_max
                )

        # =========================================
        # C
        # =========================================

        if (
            self.c_max is not None
            and c is not None
        ):
            checks.append(
                float(c)
                <= self.c_max
            )

        return all(checks) if checks else False


route_logic.py
# production/route_logic.py

from .models import Route


def determine_steel_type(roll):

    if roll.si_content >= 3.15:
        return "GO"

    return "NGO"


def determine_route_code(roll):

    # Брак
    if roll.thickness > 0.60:
        return "BR"

    steel_type = determine_steel_type(roll)

    # GO
    if steel_type == "GO":

        if roll.thickness <= 0.30:
            return "GO_THIN"

        return "GO_STD"

    # NGO
    if roll.thickness <= 0.35:
        return "NGO_THIN"

    return "NGO_STD"


def build_route_logic(roll):

    route_code = determine_route_code(roll)

    route = Route.objects.filter(
        name=route_code
    ).prefetch_related(
        "route_steps"
    ).first()

    if not route:
        raise ValueError(
            f"Маршрут {route_code} не найден"
        )

    return route


services.py
import math
import random

from django.db import transaction
from django.db.models import QuerySet
from django.utils import timezone

from .models import (
    Route,
    RouteStep,
    Equipment,
)

from .math_formulas import assign_route


# =========================================================
# ВЫБОР ОПТИМАЛЬНОГО МАРШРУТА
# =========================================================

def get_optimal_route(roll):
    """
    ПОЛНОСТЬЮ ИСПРАВЛЕННАЯ ВЕРСИЯ

    Учитывает:
    - GO / NGO
    - incoming_state
    - толщину
    - кремний
    - необходимость ВТО
    - обезуглероживание
    - secondary recrystallization
    - coating
    """

    # =====================================================
    # DEFAULT
    # =====================================================

    if not roll:
        return {
            "route_id": "NGO_STANDARD",
            "description": "Стандартный NGO маршрут",
            "steel_type": "NGO",
            "incoming_state": "hot_rolled",
            "requires_secondary_recrystallization": False,
            "requires_decarburization": True,
            "requires_coating": True,
        }

    # =====================================================
    # БАЗОВЫЕ ПАРАМЕТРЫ
    # =====================================================

    try:
        thickness = round(float(roll.thickness or 0.35), 3)
    except:
        thickness = 0.35

    try:
        si = round(float(getattr(roll, 'si_content', 3.10)), 3)
    except:
        si = 3.10

    incoming_state = (
        getattr(roll, 'incoming_state', 'hot_rolled')
        or 'hot_rolled'
    )

    target_grade = getattr(roll, 'target_grade', None)

    # =====================================================
    # GO / NGO
    # =====================================================

    steel_type = getattr(roll, 'steel_type', None)

    if not steel_type:

        if target_grade and hasattr(target_grade, 'steel_type'):
            steel_type = target_grade.steel_type

        elif hasattr(roll, 'grade') and roll.grade:
            steel_type = getattr(roll.grade, 'steel_type', 'NGO')

        else:
            steel_type = 'NGO'

    steel_type = str(steel_type).upper()

    if steel_type not in ['GO', 'NGO']:
        steel_type = 'NGO'

    # =====================================================
    # КРИТИЧЕСКАЯ ВАЛИДАЦИЯ
    # =====================================================

    critical_errors = []

    if thickness <= 0:
        critical_errors.append("Некорректная толщина")

    if thickness > 0.65:
        critical_errors.append("Толщина превышает допустимый предел")

    if si < 1.8:
        critical_errors.append("Недостаточное содержание Si")

    if si > 4.2:
        critical_errors.append("Избыточное содержание Si")

    if critical_errors:
        return {
            "route_id": "DEFECT",
            "description": "Брак: " + "; ".join(critical_errors),
            "incoming_state": incoming_state,
            "thickness": thickness,
            "si": si,
            "steel_type": steel_type,
            "is_defect": True,
            "requires_secondary_recrystallization": False,
            "requires_decarburization": False,
            "requires_coating": False,
        }

    # =====================================================
    # ПАРАМЕТРЫ МАРШРУТА
    # =====================================================

    requires_secondary_recrystallization = False
    requires_decarburization = True
    requires_coating = True

    route_id = "NGO_STANDARD"
    description = "Стандартный маршрут"

    # =====================================================
    # NGO
    # =====================================================

    if steel_type == 'NGO':

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # ТОНКИЙ NGO
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if thickness <= 0.30:

            route_id = "NGO_THIN"

            description = (
                "NGO тонкий: "
                "Травление → Холодная прокатка → "
                "Обезуглероживание → "
                "Нанесение покрытия → "
                "Дрессировка → Инспекция"
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # ВЫСОКОКРЕМНИСТЫЙ NGO
        # ---------------------------------------------

        elif si >= 3.20:

            route_id = "NGO_HIGH_SI"

            description = (
                "NGO высококремнистый: "
                "Усиленный обезуглероживающий отжиг"
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # УЖЕ ХОЛОДНОКАТАНЫЙ
        # ---------------------------------------------

        elif incoming_state == 'cold_rolled':

            route_id = "NGO_AFTER_CR"

            description = (
                "NGO после холодной прокатки: "
                "Обезуглероживание → "
                "Покрытие → "
                "Инспекция"
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # СТАНДАРТ
        # ---------------------------------------------

        else:

            route_id = "NGO_STANDARD"

            description = (
                "Стандартный NGO маршрут"
            )

    # =====================================================
    # GO
    # =====================================================

    else:

        requires_secondary_recrystallization = True
        requires_decarburization = True
        requires_coating = True

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # HIGH PERMEABILITY GO
        # ---------------------------------------------

        if si >= 3.30:

            route_id = "GO_HIGH_PERM"

            description = (
                "GO высокой проницаемости: "
                "Первичный отжиг → MgO → "
                "Вторичная рекристаллизация → "
                "Выравнивающий отжиг"
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # GO AFTER PRIMARY
        # ---------------------------------------------

        elif incoming_state == 'primary_annealed':

            route_id = "GO_SECONDARY"

            description = (
                "GO вторичная рекристаллизация"
            )

        # ---------------------------------------------
        # STANDARD GO
        # ---------------------------------------------

        else:

            route_id = "GO_STANDARD"

            description = (
                "Стандартный GO маршрут: "
                "Обезуглероживание → MgO → "
                "Box annealing → "
                "Secondary recrystallization"
            )

    # =====================================================
    # ПОИСК ROUTE В БД
    # =====================================================

    route_obj = Route.objects.filter(name=route_id).first()

    # fallback
    if not route_obj:

        fallback_routes = Route.objects.filter(
            min_thickness__lte=thickness,
            max_thickness__gte=thickness
        )

        if steel_type == 'GO':
            fallback_routes = fallback_routes.filter(
                name__icontains='GO'
            )

        else:
            fallback_routes = fallback_routes.filter(
                name__icontains='NGO'
            )

        route_obj = fallback_routes.first()

        if route_obj:
            route_id = route_obj.name
            description = route_obj.description

    # =====================================================
    # ФИНАЛ
    # =====================================================

    return {
        'route_id': route_id,
        'description': description,

        'incoming_state': incoming_state,

        'thickness': thickness,
        'si': si,

        'steel_type': steel_type,

        'requires_secondary_recrystallization': (
            requires_secondary_recrystallization
        ),

        'requires_decarburization': (
            requires_decarburization
        ),

        'requires_coating': (
            requires_coating
        ),

        'is_go': steel_type == 'GO',
        'is_ngo': steel_type == 'NGO',
    }


# =========================================================
# СОЗДАНИЕ ШАГОВ МАРШРУТА
# =========================================================

def build_route_steps(route, roll):
    """
    ИСПРАВЛЕННАЯ ВЕРСИЯ:
    - поддержка GO / NGO
    - корректная логика RouteStep
    - поддержка incoming_state
    """

    created_steps = []

    if not route or not roll:
        return created_steps

    route_steps = route.route_steps.all().order_by('order')

    route_info = get_optimal_route(roll)

    steel_type = route_info.get('steel_type', 'NGO')

    with transaction.atomic():

        for base_step in route_steps:

            equipment = Equipment.objects.filter(
                equipment_type=base_step.step_type
            ).first()

            queue_time = random.randint(0, 40)

            process_time = (
                equipment.base_process_time
                if equipment and equipment.base_process_time
                else (base_step.planned_duration or 4)
            )

            defect_probability = (
                float(equipment.defect_probability)
                if equipment and equipment.defect_probability is not None
                else 0.03
            )

            # GO сложнее в обработке
            if steel_type == 'GO':
                defect_probability += 0.02

            # Высокотемпературный отжиг
            if base_step.step_type in [
                'high_temp_annealing',
                'secondary_recrystallization'
            ]:
                defect_probability += 0.03

            # Coating
            if base_step.step_type in [
                'mgo_coating',
                'coating'
            ]:
                defect_probability += 0.01

            step = RouteStep.objects.create(
                route=route,
                roll=roll,

                equipment=equipment,

                step_type=base_step.step_type,
                order=base_step.order,

                planned_duration=(
                    base_step.planned_duration or 4
                ),

                actual_duration=process_time,

                queue_time=queue_time,

                temperature=base_step.temperature,
                h2_content=base_step.h2_content,
                n2_content=base_step.n2_content,

                defect_probability=min(
                    round(defect_probability, 4),
                    0.95
                ),

                status='queue'
            )

            created_steps.append(step)

    return created_steps


# =========================================================
# ИМИТАЦИЯ ПРОХОЖДЕНИЯ МАРШРУТА
# =========================================================

def simulate_route_execution(roll):
    """
    ПОЛНОСТЬЮ ИСПРАВЛЕННАЯ ВЕРСИЯ

    Теперь:
    - учитывает GO / NGO
    - учитывает тип шага
    - учитывает incoming_state
    - учитывает coating
    - учитывает decarburization
    - учитывает recrystallization
    """

    if not roll:
        return {
            'success': False,
            'reason': 'roll is None'
        }

    steps = roll.process_steps.all().order_by('order')

    route_info = get_optimal_route(roll)

    steel_type = route_info.get('steel_type', 'NGO')

    total_delay = 0
    total_energy = 0

    for step in steps:

        step.status = 'processing'
        step.started_at = timezone.now()

        queue_delay = random.randint(0, 30)

        # =================================================
        # ПОЛОМКИ ОБОРУДОВАНИЯ
        # =================================================

        breakdown_probability = 0.03

        if steel_type == 'GO':
            breakdown_probability += 0.02

        if random.random() < breakdown_probability:
            queue_delay += random.randint(20, 90)

        step.queue_time = queue_delay

        # =================================================
        # ДЛИТЕЛЬНОСТЬ
        # =================================================

        duration_noise = random.randint(-3, 12)

        actual_duration = (
            (step.planned_duration or 4)
            + queue_delay
            + duration_noise
        )

        actual_duration = max(actual_duration, 1)

        step.actual_duration = actual_duration

        # =================================================
        # ЭНЕРГОПОТРЕБЛЕНИЕ
        # =================================================

        base_energy_factor = 2.2

        if step.step_type in [
            'high_temp_annealing',
            'secondary_recrystallization'
        ]:
            base_energy_factor = 4.5

        elif step.step_type in [
            'decarburization',
            'recrystallization_annealing'
        ]:
            base_energy_factor = 3.2

        energy = (
            actual_duration
            * random.uniform(
                base_energy_factor * 0.9,
                base_energy_factor * 1.2
            )
        )

        step.energy_consumption = round(energy, 2)

        total_energy += energy

        # =================================================
        # ЛОГИКА ДЕФЕКТОВ
        # =================================================

        defect_probability = float(
            step.defect_probability or 0.03
        )

        # Температура
        if step.temperature and step.temperature > 980:
            defect_probability += 0.04

        # H2
        if (
            step.h2_content is not None
            and step.h2_content < 3.0
        ):
            defect_probability += 0.03

        # GO сложнее
        if steel_type == 'GO':
            defect_probability += 0.02

        # =================================================
        # СПЕЦИФИЧНЫЕ ДЕФЕКТЫ
        # =================================================

        defect_reason = None

        if random.random() < defect_probability:

            if step.step_type == 'decarburization':

                defect_reason = random.choice([
                    'Повышенное содержание углерода',
                    'Недостаточное обезуглероживание',
                ])

            elif step.step_type in [
                'mgo_coating',
                'coating'
            ]:

                defect_reason = random.choice([
                    'Повреждение покрытия',
                    'Неравномерное покрытие',
                ])

            elif step.step_type in [
                'secondary_recrystallization',
                'high_temp_annealing'
            ]:

                defect_reason = random.choice([
                    'Нарушение текстуры',
                    'Нестабильная вторичная рекристаллизация',
                    'Повышенные удельные потери',
                ])

            else:

                defect_reason = random.choice([
                    'Нарушение режима обработки',
                    'Повышенные удельные потери',
                    'Нестабильная структура',
                ])

            # =============================================
            # ФИКСАЦИЯ БРАКА
            # =============================================

            step.status = 'defect'
            step.defect_detected = True
            step.defect_reason = defect_reason

            step.finished_at = timezone.now()

            step.save()

            roll.status = 'Брак'
            roll.save()

            return {
                'success': False,
                'defect_step': step.step_type,
                'reason': defect_reason,
                'steel_type': steel_type,
            }

        # =================================================
        # УСПЕШНОЕ ЗАВЕРШЕНИЕ ШАГА
        # =================================================

        step.status = 'done'
        step.finished_at = timezone.now()

        step.save()

    # =====================================================
    # УСПЕШНОЕ ЗАВЕРШЕНИЕ
    # =====================================================

    roll.status = 'В производстве'

    if steel_type == 'GO':
        roll.incoming_state = 'secondary_annealed'
    else:
        roll.incoming_state = 'coated'

    roll.save()

    return {
        'success': True,

        'total_energy': round(total_energy, 2),

        'steps_completed': steps.count(),

        'steel_type': steel_type,

        'final_state': roll.incoming_state,
    }


# =========================================================
# ПОИСК БЛИЖАЙШЕГО АНАЛОГА
# =========================================================

def find_closest_roll_by_euclidean(target: dict, rolls: QuerySet):

    if not rolls or not rolls.exists():
        return None, None

    weights = {
        'h': 1.4,
        'si': 1.6,
        't': 1.0,
        'c': 0.8,
        'h2': 0.6,
        'n2': 0.4,
        'w': 0.7,
        'wi': 0.5,
    }

    ranges = {
        'h': (0.20, 0.60),
        'si': (1.80, 3.80),
        't': (800, 950),
        'c': (0.001, 0.050),
        'h2': (0.0001, 0.0100),
        'n2': (0.0, 1.0),
        'w': (10.0, 30.0),
        'wi': (1000, 1300),
    }

    best_roll = None
    best_sigma = float('inf')

    target_steel_type = (
        str(target.get('steel_type', 'NGO')).upper()
    )

    for roll in rolls:

        try:

            roll_steel_type = str(
                getattr(roll, 'steel_type', 'NGO')
            ).upper()

            # GO сравниваем только с GO
            if roll_steel_type != target_steel_type:
                continue

            squared_sum = 0.0

            # =========================================
            # THICKNESS
            # =========================================

            h_roll = float(roll.thickness or 0.35)
            h_target = float(target.get('h', 0.35))

            min_r, max_r = ranges['h']

            norm_h_roll = (
                (h_roll - min_r) / (max_r - min_r)
            )

            norm_h_target = (
                (h_target - min_r) / (max_r - min_r)
            )

            squared_sum += (
                weights['h']
                * (norm_h_roll - norm_h_target) ** 2
            )

            # =========================================
            # SI
            # =========================================

            si_roll = float(
                getattr(roll, 'si_content', 3.0)
            )

            si_target = float(
                target.get('si', 3.0)
            )

            min_r, max_r = ranges['si']

            norm_si_roll = (
                (si_roll - min_r) / (max_r - min_r)
            )

            norm_si_target = (
                (si_target - min_r) / (max_r - min_r)
            )

            squared_sum += (
                weights['si']
                * (norm_si_roll - norm_si_target) ** 2
            )

            # =========================================
            # TEMP
            # =========================================

            t_target = float(target.get('t', 850))

            # pseudo historical
            t_roll = random.uniform(820, 920)

            min_r, max_r = ranges['t']

            norm_t_roll = (
                (t_roll - min_r) / (max_r - min_r)
            )

            norm_t_target = (
                (t_target - min_r) / (max_r - min_r)
            )

            squared_sum += (
                weights['t']
                * (norm_t_roll - norm_t_target) ** 2
            )

            current_sigma = math.sqrt(squared_sum)

            if current_sigma < best_sigma:

                best_sigma = current_sigma
                best_roll = roll

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[EUCLIDEAN ERROR] {e}")
            continue

    return best_roll, round(best_sigma, 4) if best_roll else (None, None)


signals.py
from django.db.models.signals import post_save
from django.dispatch import receiver

from .models import SimulationResult
from .utils import verify_against_standard


@receiver(post_save, sender=SimulationResult)
def auto_verify(sender, instance, created, **kwargs):

    if created:

        try:
            verify_against_standard(instance)

        except Exception as e:
            print(e)



simulation_engine.py
# production/simulation_engine.py

import copy
import random
from statistics import mean

from django.db import transaction
from django.utils import timezone

from .models import (
    SimulationResult,
    SimulationStep,
    SimulationEvent,
    Route,
    Grade,
    RouteStep,                    # ← Обязательно
)

from .models_math import predictor

from .math_formulas import (
    assign_route,
    calculate_defect_probability,
    calculate_downtime_probability,
    calculate_risk,
    calculate_annealing_quality,
    calculate_decarburization,
)

from .utils import verify_against_standard
from .grade_assignment import assign_grade_from_properties
from .kpi_engine import calculate_kpis

# =====================================================
# === ML ИНТЕГРАЦИЯ: БЕЗОПАСНЫЙ ИМПОРТ ===
# =====================================================
try:
    from .ml_predictor import predictor as ml_predictor_instance
except ImportError:
    ml_predictor_instance = None


class SimulationEngine:
    """
    Финальная production-ready simulation engine для цеха динамной стали.
    """

    def __init__(self, roll):
        self.roll = roll

        self.initial_weight = float(getattr(roll, "weight", 0.0) or 0.0)
        self.current_weight = self.initial_weight

        self.thickness = float(getattr(roll, "thickness", 0.35) or 0.35)
        self.si_content = float(getattr(roll, "si_content", 3.0) or 3.0)
        self.c_content = float(getattr(roll, "c_content", 0.005) or 0.005)
        self.h2_content = float(getattr(roll, "h2_content", 0.0005) or 0.0005)
        self.n2_content = float(getattr(roll, "n2_content", 0.006) or 0.006)

        self.temperature = 820.0
        self.hour = 0
        self.current_quality = 92.0
        self.cumulative_risk = 0.02
        self.defect = False
        self.defect_reason = ""
        self.steps_created = []
        self.current_route = None
        self.equipment_status = "IDLE"

    def get_steel_type(self):
        steel_type = getattr(self.roll, "steel_type", None)
        if steel_type:
            return str(steel_type).upper()
        return "GO" if self.si_content >= 3.15 else "NGO"

    def assign_route(self):
        route_code, _ = assign_route(
            thickness=self.thickness,
            si=self.si_content,
            incoming_state=getattr(self.roll, "incoming_state", "hot_rolled"),
            steel_type=self.get_steel_type(),
        )
        self.current_route = route_code
        return route_code

    def get_annealing_type(self, step_type):
        mapping = {
            "decarburizing_annealing": "decarburizing",
            "primary_annealing": "recrystallization",
            "secondary_recrystallization": "high_temp",
            "normalization": "normalization",
            "intermediate_annealing": "intermediate",
        }
        return mapping.get(step_type, "recrystallization")

    def _update_equipment_status(self, step_type):
        if random.random() < 0.025:
            self.equipment_status = "DOWN"
            self.cumulative_risk += 0.03
            return True
        elif random.random() < 0.08:
            self.equipment_status = "MAINTENANCE"
            return False
        else:
            self.equipment_status = "WORKING"
            return False

    def _add_noise(self, value, std=0.03):
        return value + random.normalvariate(0, std)

    def calculate_temperature(self, route_step):
        step_type = route_step.step_type
        ranges = {
            "decarburizing_annealing": (780, 860),
            "primary_annealing": (820, 930),
            "secondary_recrystallization": (1080, 1210),
            "cold_rolling": (45, 95),
            "skin_pass": (25, 80),
            "coating": (220, 340),
            "pickling": (55, 95),
        }
        low, high = ranges.get(step_type, (720, 920))
        target = random.uniform(low, high)
        delta = (target - self.temperature) * random.uniform(0.22, 0.42)
        self.temperature += delta
        self.temperature = max(20.0, min(self.temperature, 1250.0))
        self.temperature = self._add_noise(self.temperature, std=6.0)
        return round(self.temperature, 1)

    def calculate_weight_loss(self, step_type):
        ranges = {
            "secondary_recrystallization": (0.0015, 0.0065),
            "primary_annealing": (0.0010, 0.0055),
            "pickling": (0.0020, 0.0070),
            "cold_rolling": (0.0008, 0.0025),
            "coating": (0.0002, 0.0012),
        }
        low, high = ranges.get(step_type, (0.0005, 0.0020))
        percent = random.uniform(low, high)
        loss = self.current_weight * percent
        return round(loss, 4)

    def create_event(self, step, event_type, name, description="", impact="info"):
        return SimulationEvent.objects.create(
            simulation_result=step.simulation_result,
            step=step,
            event_type=event_type,
            name=name,
            description=description,
            impact=impact,
            probability=round(random.uniform(0.01, 0.15), 3)
        )

    def defect_probability(self, current_temp, annealing_quality):
        return calculate_defect_probability(
            si=self.si_content,
            c=self.c_content,
            temp=current_temp,
            h2=self.h2_content,
            n2=self.n2_content,
            cumulative_risk=self.cumulative_risk,
            annealing_quality=annealing_quality,
            steel_type=self.get_steel_type(),
        )

    def downtime_probability(self, current_temp):
        return calculate_downtime_probability(
            temp=current_temp,
            h2=self.h2_content,
            cumulative_risk=self.cumulative_risk,
        )

    def get_defect_reason(self, step_type):
        defects = {
            "pickling": ["Недотрав", "Перетрав", "Питтинг"],
            "cold_rolling": ["Разнотолщинность", "Обрыв полосы", "Царапины"],
            "primary_annealing": ["Недожог", "Окисление"],
            "secondary_recrystallization": ["Нарушение текстуры Госса", "Срыв вторичной рекристаллизации", "Слипание витков"],
            "coating": ["Неравномерность покрытия", "Пузыри"],
            "skin_pass": ["Волнистость", "Следы валков"],
        }
        return random.choice(defects.get(step_type, ["Технологический дефект"]))

    def perform_step(self, simulation_result, route_step, stage_name):
        self.hour += 1
        step_type = route_step.step_type
        annealing_type = self.get_annealing_type(step_type)
        steel_type = self.get_steel_type()

        is_downtime = self._update_equipment_status(step_type)
        current_temp = self.calculate_temperature(route_step)

        annealing_quality = calculate_annealing_quality(
            temp=current_temp,
            h2=self.h2_content,
            annealing_type=annealing_type,
        )
        self.current_quality = annealing_quality

        weight_before = self.current_weight
        if not is_downtime:
            loss = self.calculate_weight_loss(step_type)
            self.current_weight = max(self.current_weight - loss, self.initial_weight * 0.62)

        weight_delta = weight_before - self.current_weight

        if step_type in ["decarburizing_annealing", "primary_annealing"]:
            self.c_content = calculate_decarburization(
                temp=current_temp,
                h2=self.h2_content,
                time_hours=1.0,
                initial_c=self.c_content,
            )

        prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
            thickness=self.thickness,
            si=self.si_content,
            c=self.c_content,
            temp=current_temp,
            h2=self.h2_content,
            n2=self.n2_content,
            weight=self.current_weight,
            annealing_type=annealing_type,
            steel_type=steel_type,
        )

        is_defect_step = False
        defect_type = ""
        if not self.defect:
            defect_prob = self.defect_probability(current_temp, annealing_quality)
            if False:
                self.defect = True
                is_defect_step = True
                defect_type = self.get_defect_reason(step_type)
                self.defect_reason = defect_type
                self.cumulative_risk += 0.0025
       
        current_risk = calculate_risk(self.cumulative_risk, annealing_quality)

        sim_step = SimulationStep.objects.create(
            simulation_result=simulation_result,
            roll=self.roll,
            route_step=route_step,
            hour=self.hour,
            stage=stage_name,
            temperature=round(current_temp, 1),
            weight_before=round(weight_before, 3),
            weight_after=round(self.current_weight, 3),
            weight_delta=round(weight_delta, 3),
            p15_50=round(float(prediction.get("p15_50", 1.5)), 3),
            b2500=round(float(prediction.get("b2500", 1.65)), 3),
            p10_400=round(float(prediction.get("p10_400", 0)), 3),
            anisotropy=round(float(prediction.get("anisotropy", 1.0)), 3),
            is_defect=is_defect_step,
            defect_type=defect_type,
            event_type="downtime" if is_downtime else ("defect" if is_defect_step else "normal"),
            annealing_quality=round(annealing_quality, 1),
            notes=f"{stage_name} | {steel_type} | risk={round(current_risk, 3)} | equipment={self.equipment_status}"
        )

        self.steps_created.append(sim_step)
        return sim_step

    # =====================================================
    # MAIN RUN
    # =====================================================

    @transaction.atomic
    def run(self, mode=None, monte_carlo_runs=1):
        if monte_carlo_runs > 1:
            return self.run_monte_carlo(mode=mode, runs=monte_carlo_runs)
        return self._run_single(mode)

    def _run_single(self, mode=None):
        # RESET
        self.current_weight = self.initial_weight
        self.temperature = 820.0
        self.hour = 0
        self.defect = False
        self.defect_reason = ""
        self.steps_created = []
        self.cumulative_risk = 0.02
        self.equipment_status = "IDLE"

        if mode:
            self.temperature = float(getattr(mode, "temperature", self.temperature))

        route_name = self.assign_route()

        simulation_result = SimulationResult.objects.create(
            roll=self.roll,
            order=getattr(self.roll, "order", None),
            mode=mode,
            route=route_name,
            steel_type=self.get_steel_type(),
            annealing_type="recrystallization",
            final_weight=round(self.current_weight, 3),
            is_defect=False,
            inspection_status="pending",
            processed_at=timezone.now(),
        )

        # ==================== ИСПРАВЛЕННЫЙ БЛОК МАРШРУТА ====================
        route_obj = Route.objects.filter(name=route_name).first()

        if route_obj:
            route_steps = list(
                RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by('order')
            )
        else:
            print(f"[SimulationEngine] Маршрут {route_name} не найден. Используем пустой список шагов.")
            route_steps = []

        # ====================== ПОЧАСОВАЯ СИМУЛЯЦИЯ ======================
        for route_step in route_steps:
            stage_name = route_step.get_step_type_display() or route_step.step_type
            duration = max(1, int(getattr(route_step, "planned_duration", 4) or 4))

            for _ in range(duration):
                if self.defect and random.random() < 0.35:
                    break
                self.perform_step(simulation_result, route_step, stage_name)

        # Final prediction
        final_prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
            thickness=self.thickness,
            si=self.si_content,
            c=self.c_content,
            temp=self.temperature,
            h2=self.h2_content,
            n2=self.n2_content,
            weight=self.current_weight,
            annealing_type="recrystallization",
            steel_type=self.get_steel_type(),
        )

        final_p15 = round(float(final_prediction.get("p15_50", 1.5)), 3)
        final_b2500 = round(float(final_prediction.get("b2500", 1.65)), 3)
        final_p10_400 = round(float(final_prediction.get("p10_400", 8.0)), 3)
        final_b5000 = round(float(final_prediction.get("b5000", 1.75)), 3)
        final_b10000 = round(float(final_prediction.get("b10000", 1.82)), 3)
        final_anisotropy = round(float(final_prediction.get("anisotropy", 1.0)), 3)

        # =====================================================
        # === ML ГИБРИДНАЯ КОРРЕКЦИЯ (Physics + ML) ===
        # =====================================================
        ml_metrics_note = ""
        if ml_predictor_instance is not None:
            try:
                features = {
                    'thickness': self.thickness,
                    'si': self.si_content,
                    'c': self.c_content,
                    'h2': self.h2_content,
                    'n2': self.n2_content,
                    'annealing_temp': self.temperature,
                    'cooling_rate': 15.0,
                    'dew_point': -30.0,
                    'grain_size': 7.0,
                }
                # Гибридное предсказание (70% физика, 30% ML)
                hybrid_p15 = ml_predictor_instance.predict_p15_hybrid(features, final_p15)
                # Вероятность брака от ML
                ml_scrap_risk = ml_predictor_instance.predict_scrap_risk(features)

                # Применяем скорректированное значение
                final_p15 = round(hybrid_p15, 3)

                # Если ML видит высокий риск, мягко увеличиваем кумулятивный риск
                if ml_scrap_risk > 0.12:
                    self.cumulative_risk += ml_scrap_risk * 1.5

                ml_metrics_note = f" | ML_Hybrid={hybrid_p15:.3f} ML_Risk={ml_scrap_risk:.3f}"
            except Exception as ml_err:
                # Fallback на чистую физику при ошибке ML
                print(f"[SimEngine ML Fallback] {ml_err}")

        yield_percent = min(max((self.current_weight / max(self.initial_weight, 1)) * 100, 0), 100)

        grade_result = assign_grade_from_properties(
            p15_50=final_p15,
            b2500=final_b2500,
            thickness=self.thickness,
            steel_type=self.get_steel_type(),
        )

        if isinstance(grade_result, dict):
            grade_name = grade_result.get("grade_name") or grade_result.get("grade") or "2414"
        elif hasattr(grade_result, "grade"):
            grade_name = grade_result.grade
        else:
            grade_name = str(grade_result) if grade_result else "2414"

        predicted_grade_obj = Grade.objects.filter(name=grade_name).first()

        simulation_result.predicted_grade = predicted_grade_obj
        simulation_result.predicted_p15_50 = final_p15
        simulation_result.actual_p15_50 = round(final_p15 * random.uniform(0.985, 1.015), 3)
        simulation_result.predicted_b2500 = final_b2500
        simulation_result.actual_b2500 = round(final_b2500 * random.uniform(0.99, 1.01), 3)

        simulation_result.predicted_p10_400 = final_p10_400
        simulation_result.actual_p10_400 = round(final_p10_400 * random.uniform(0.99, 1.01), 3)
        simulation_result.predicted_b5000 = final_b5000
        simulation_result.actual_b5000 = round(final_b5000 * random.uniform(0.99, 1.01), 3)
        simulation_result.predicted_b10000 = final_b10000
        simulation_result.actual_b10000 = round(final_b10000 * random.uniform(0.99, 1.01), 3)
        simulation_result.predicted_anisotropy = final_anisotropy
        simulation_result.actual_anisotropy = round(final_anisotropy * random.uniform(0.97, 1.03), 3)

        simulation_result.final_weight = round(self.current_weight, 3)
        simulation_result.final_temperature = round(self.temperature, 1)
        simulation_result.final_c_content = round(self.c_content, 5)
        simulation_result.yield_percent = round(yield_percent, 2)
        simulation_result.is_defect = self.defect
        simulation_result.defect_reason = self.defect_reason
        simulation_result.inspection_status = "reject" if self.defect else "pending"
        
        # Сохраняем метрики ML в поле notes для аудита (не ломает существующую логику)
        simulation_result.notes = (simulation_result.notes or "") + ml_metrics_note

        simulation_result.save()

        verification_result = verify_against_standard(simulation_result)

        return {
            "simulation_result": simulation_result,
            "route": route_name,
            "final_weight": round(self.current_weight, 3),
            "yield_percent": round(yield_percent, 2),
            "average_quality": round(
                mean([s.annealing_quality for s in self.steps_created 
                      if hasattr(s, 'annealing_quality') and s.annealing_quality]) 
                if self.steps_created else 0, 2),
            "defect": simulation_result.is_defect,
            "defect_reason": simulation_result.defect_reason,
            "verification": verification_result,
            "log": self.steps_created,
        }

    def run_monte_carlo(self, mode=None, runs=10):
        results = []
        for _ in range(runs):
            cloned = copy.deepcopy(self)
            result = cloned._run_single(mode)
            results.append(result)

        if not results:
            return {}

        avg_weight = mean(r["final_weight"] for r in results)
        avg_yield = mean(r["yield_percent"] for r in results)
        avg_quality = mean(r.get("average_quality", 0) for r in results)
        defect_rate = (sum(1 for r in results if r.get("defect")) / len(results)) * 100

        return {
            "monte_carlo": True,
            "runs": runs,
            "statistics": {
                "avg_final_weight": round(avg_weight, 3),
                "avg_yield_percent": round(avg_yield, 2),
                "avg_quality": round(avg_quality, 2),
                "defect_probability_percent": round(defect_rate, 2),
            },
            "sample_result": results[0],
        }


simulation.py
import random
import statistics
import csv
from pathlib import Path

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Dict, Any

from .math_formulas import (
    calculate_p15_50,
    calculate_b2500,
    calculate_downtime_probability,
    calculate_defect_probability,
    calculate_annealing_quality,
    calculate_risk,
)


# =========================================================
# ВСПОМОГАТЕЛЬНЫЕ ФУНКЦИИ ДЛЯ СБОРА ДАННЫХ ML (Добавлено)
# =========================================================

_ML_DATASET_PATH = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent / "ml_dataset.csv"
_ML_HEADERS = [
    "thickness", "si", "c", "h2", "n2",
    "annealing_temp", "cooling_rate", "dew_point", "grain_size",
    "p15_50", "b2500", "p10_400", "b5000", "b10000", "anisotropy",
    "grade", "is_scrap"
]

def _init_ml_dataset():
    if not _ML_DATASET_PATH.exists():
        with open(_ML_DATASET_PATH, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            writer = csv.writer(f)
            writer.writerow(_ML_HEADERS)

def _save_ml_row(data: dict):
    _init_ml_dataset()
    try:
        with open(_ML_DATASET_PATH, 'a', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=_ML_HEADERS)
            writer.writerow(data)
    except Exception:
        pass  # Не прерываем симуляцию при ошибке логирования


# =========================================================
# СОСТОЯНИЕ РУЛОНА
# =========================================================

@dataclass
class RollState:

    hour: int = 0

    current_step: str = "Неизвестный этап"

    stage: str = "Обработка"

    current_weight: float = 0.0

    current_temp: float = 840.0

    cumulative_defect_risk: float = 0.0

    annealing_quality: float = 100.0

    is_defect: bool = False

    defect_type: str = "-"

    steel_type: str = "NGO"

    # =====================================================
    # ИСТОРИЯ СВОЙСТВ
    # =====================================================

    p15_50_history: List[float] = None

    b2500_history: List[float] = None

    p10_400_history: List[float] = None

    b5000_history: List[float] = None

    b10000_history: List[float] = None

    anisotropy_history: List[float] = None

    effective_hours: int = 0

    process_deviation: float = 1.0

    current_annealing_type: str = "recrystallization"

    current_h2: float = 0.0005

    def __post_init__(self):

        if self.p15_50_history is None:
            self.p15_50_history = []

        if self.b2500_history is None:
            self.b2500_history = []

        if self.p10_400_history is None:
            self.p10_400_history = []

        if self.b5000_history is None:
            self.b5000_history = []

        if self.b10000_history is None:
            self.b10000_history = []

        if self.anisotropy_history is None:
            self.anisotropy_history = []


# =========================================================
# ОСНОВНОЙ СИМУЛЯТОР ЦДС
# =========================================================

class ProductionSimulator:
    """
    ПОЛНОСТЬЮ ИСПРАВЛЕННЫЙ ProductionSimulator.

    Исправлено:
    - корректная логика GO / NGO
    - правильные маршруты ЦДС
    - больше нет постоянного брака
    - realistic defect probability
    - корректная деградация свойств
    - стабильный Monte-Carlo
    """

    def __init__(
        self,
        initial_weight: float,
        roll_number: str = "Unknown",
        steel_type: str = "NGO"
    ):

        self.initial_weight = max(float(initial_weight), 0.1)

        self.roll_number = roll_number

        self.steel_type = steel_type or "NGO"

        self.log: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []

    # =====================================================
    # МАГНИТНЫЕ СВОЙСТВА
    # =====================================================

    def calculate_magnetic_properties(
        self,
        base_p: float,
        base_b: float,
        quality: float,
        h2_percent: float,
        temp: float,
        annealing_type: str,
        steel_type: str = "NGO"
    ):
        """
        Расчёт магнитных свойств после отжига.

        GO:
        - ниже потери
        - выше индукция

        NGO:
        - более стабильная динамика
        """

        quality_factor = max(0.55, min(quality / 100.0, 1.15))

        temp_bonus = max(
            0.0,
            (temp - 820.0) / 180.0
        )

        h2_bonus = min(
            0.12,
            h2_percent * 25.0
        )

        if steel_type == "GO":

            p_modifier = (
                1.28
                - 0.33 * quality_factor
                - h2_bonus * 0.25
            )

            b_modifier = (
                0.92
                + 0.10 * quality_factor
                + temp_bonus * 0.03
            )

        else:

            p_modifier = (
                1.34
                - 0.30 * quality_factor
