                - h2_bonus * 0.15
            )

            b_modifier = (
                0.90
                + 0.09 * quality_factor
                + temp_bonus * 0.02
            )

        p_loss = base_p * p_modifier

        b_induction = base_b * b_modifier

        p_loss = max(0.75, min(p_loss, 5.5))

        b_induction = max(1.35, min(b_induction, 2.15))

        return (
            round(p_loss, 3),
            round(b_induction, 3)
        )

    # =====================================================
    # ОСНОВНОЙ RUN
    # =====================================================

    def run(
        self,
        route_steps,
        p_predicted: float,
        b_predicted: float,
        si: float = 3.0,
        c: float = 0.005,
        h2: float = 0.0005,
        n2: float = 0.006,
        base_temp: float = 840,
        monte_carlo_runs: int = 1,
        thickness: float = 0.35,
        steel_type: str = "NGO"
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        steel_type = steel_type or self.steel_type

        if monte_carlo_runs <= 1:

            simulation_log = self._single_run(
                route_steps=route_steps,
                p_predicted=p_predicted,
                b_predicted=b_predicted,
                si=si,
                c=c,
                h2=h2,
                n2=n2,
                base_temp=base_temp,
                thickness=thickness,
                steel_type=steel_type
            )

            final_entry = next(
                (
                    item
                    for item in reversed(simulation_log)
                    if item.get("hour") == "ИТОГ"
                ),
                None
            )

            # === ML: Сохранение результатов симуляции в датасет ===
            if final_entry:
                _save_ml_row({
                    "thickness": thickness,
                    "si": si,
                    "c": c,
                    "h2": h2,
                    "n2": n2,
                    "annealing_temp": final_entry.get("actual_temp", base_temp),
                    "cooling_rate": 15.0,
                    "dew_point": -30.0,
                    "grain_size": 7.0,
                    "p15_50": final_entry.get("final_p15_50", p_predicted),
                    "b2500": final_entry.get("final_b2500", b_predicted),
                    "p10_400": final_entry.get("final_p10_400", 0),
                    "b5000": final_entry.get("final_b5000", 0),
                    "b10000": final_entry.get("final_b10000", 0),
                    "anisotropy": final_entry.get("final_anisotropy", 0),
                    "grade": "2412" if final_entry.get("final_p15_50", 99) < 2.4 else "2414",
                    "is_scrap": 1 if final_entry.get("is_defect", False) else 0
                })

            return {
                "success": True,
                "log": simulation_log,
                "final": final_entry,
                "monte_carlo": False,
            }

        # =================================================
        # MONTE-CARLO
        # =================================================

        results = []

        for _ in range(monte_carlo_runs):

            log = self._single_run(
                route_steps,
                p_predicted,
                b_predicted,
                si,
                c,
                h2,
                n2,
                base_temp,
                thickness,
                steel_type
            )

            final = next(
                (
                    item
                    for item in reversed(log)
                    if item.get("hour") == "ИТОГ"
                ),
                None
            )

            if final:

                results.append({
                    "final_weight": final.get(
                        "final_weight",
                        self.initial_weight
                    ),
                    "total_hours": final.get(
                        "total_hours",
                        0
                    ),
                    "has_defect": final.get(
                        "is_defect",
                        False
                    ),
                    "risk": final.get(
                        "risk",
                        2.5
                    ),
                    "p15_50": final.get(
                        "final_p15_50",
                        p_predicted
                    ),
                })

        if not results:

            return {
                "success": False,
                "error": "Monte-Carlo не вернул результатов"
            }

        avg_weight = statistics.mean(
            r["final_weight"]
            for r in results
        )

        avg_hours = statistics.mean(
            r["total_hours"]
            for r in results
        )

        defect_rate = (
            sum(
                1
                for r in results
                if r["has_defect"]
            )
            / len(results)
        ) * 100

        avg_risk = statistics.mean(
            r["risk"]
            for r in results
        )

        return {
            "success": True,
            "monte_carlo": True,
            "runs": monte_carlo_runs,
            "statistics": {
                "avg_final_weight": round(avg_weight, 2),
                "avg_total_hours": round(avg_hours, 1),
                "defect_probability_percent": round(defect_rate, 1),
                "avg_risk": round(avg_risk, 2),
                "yield_percent": round(
                    (avg_weight / self.initial_weight) * 100,
                    2
                )
            }
        }

    # =====================================================
    # ОДИН ПРОГОН
    # =====================================================

    def _single_run(
        self,
        route_steps,
        p_predicted,
        b_predicted,
        si,
        c,
        h2,
        n2,
        base_temp,
        thickness,
        steel_type
    ):

        self.log = []

        state = RollState(
            current_weight=self.initial_weight,
            current_temp=base_temp,
            current_h2=h2,
            steel_type=steel_type
        )

        total_planned_hours = sum(
            getattr(step, 'planned_duration', 4)
            for step in route_steps
        ) if route_steps else 0

        for step in route_steps:

            if state.is_defect:
                break

            step_type = getattr(
                step,
                'step_type',
                str(step)
            )

            step_name = getattr(
                step,
                'get_step_type_display',
                lambda: step_type
            )()

            state.current_step = step_name

            hours_in_step = max(
                int(getattr(step, 'planned_duration', 4)),
                1
            )

            target_temp = (
                getattr(step, 'temperature', base_temp)
                or base_temp
            )

            annealing_type = self._resolve_annealing_type(
                step_type
            )

            state.current_annealing_type = annealing_type

            for _ in range(hours_in_step):

                if state.is_defect:
                    break

                state.hour += 1

                state.effective_hours += 1

                state.stage = self._get_substage(
                    step_type
                )

                state.current_temp = (
                    self._calculate_temperature(
                        step_type,
                        target_temp
                    )
                )

                # =========================================
                # ПРОСТОЙ
                # =========================================

                downtime_probability = (
                    calculate_downtime_probability(
                        state.current_temp,
                        h2,
                        state.cumulative_defect_risk
                    )
                )

                downtime_probability *= 0.45

                if random.random() < downtime_probability:

                    reason = random.choice([
                        "Сбой датчика",
                        "Колебание температуры",
                        "Проблема привода",
                        "Смена рулона",
                    ])

                    self.log.append({
                        "hour": state.hour,
                        "step": state.current_step,
                        "stage": state.stage,
                        "status": "ПРОСТОЙ",
                        "reason": reason,
                        "temp": round(
                            state.current_temp,
                            1
                        ),
                        "weight": round(
                            state.current_weight,
                            4
                        ),
                        "defect": False,
                        "annealing_quality": round(
                            state.annealing_quality,
                            1
                        ),
                    })

                    state.cumulative_defect_risk += 0.004

                    continue

                # =========================================
                # ВЕРОЯТНОСТЬ БРАКА
                # =========================================

                defect_probability = (
                    calculate_defect_probability(
                        si,
                        c,
                        state.current_temp,
                        h2,
                        n2,
                        state.cumulative_defect_risk,
                        state.annealing_quality
                    )
                )

                # ГЛАВНОЕ ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ:
                defect_probability *= 0.18

                if steel_type == "GO":
                    defect_probability *= 1.25

                if random.random() < defect_probability:

                    defect_type = self._get_defect_type(
                        step_type,
                        state.current_temp,
                        h2,
                        si,
                        steel_type
                    )

                    state.is_defect = True

                    state.defect_type = defect_type

                    self.log.append({
                        "hour": state.hour,
                        "step": state.current_step,
                        "stage": state.stage,
                        "status": "БРАК",
                        "reason": "Обнаружен дефект",
                        "temp": round(
                            state.current_temp,
                            1
                        ),
                        "weight": round(
                            state.current_weight,
                            4
                        ),
                        "defect": True,
                        "defect_type": defect_type,
                        "annealing_quality": round(
                            state.annealing_quality,
                            1
                        ),
                    })

                    break

                # =========================================
                # НОРМАЛЬНЫЙ ЧАС
                # =========================================

                self._process_normal_hour(
                    state=state,
                    base_p=p_predicted,
                    base_b=b_predicted,
                    h2=h2,
                    step_type=step_type,
                    annealing_type=annealing_type,
                    si=si,
                    thickness=thickness,
                    steel_type=steel_type
                )

                self.log.append({
                    "hour": state.hour,
                    "step": state.current_step,
                    "stage": state.stage,
                    "status": "РАБОТА",
                    "temp": round(state.current_temp, 1),

                    "p15_50": state.p15_50_history[-1],
                    "b2500": state.b2500_history[-1],

                    "p10_400": state.p10_400_history[-1],
                    "b5000": state.b5000_history[-1],
                    "b10000": state.b10000_history[-1],

                    "anisotropy": state.anisotropy_history[-1],

                    "weight": round(
                        state.current_weight,
                        4
                    ),

                    "defect": False,

                    "annealing_quality": round(
                        state.annealing_quality,
                        1
                    ),

                    "annealing_type": annealing_type,

                    "steel_type": steel_type,

                    "actual_temp": round(
                        state.current_temp,
                        1
                    ),

                    "actual_h2": round(
                        state.current_h2,
                        4
                    ),

                    "dev": round(
                        state.process_deviation,
                        4
                    )
                })

                state.cumulative_defect_risk += 0.0018

        # =================================================
        # ИТОГ
        # =================================================

        final_risk = calculate_risk(
            state.cumulative_defect_risk,
            state.annealing_quality
        )

        last_p = (
            state.p15_50_history[-1]
            if state.p15_50_history
            else p_predicted
        )

        last_b = (
            state.b2500_history[-1]
            if state.b2500_history
            else b_predicted
        )

        self.log.append({

            "hour": "ИТОГ",

            "step": "Завершение производства",

            "status": "ФИНАЛ",

            "risk": round(final_risk, 2),

            "final_weight": round(
                state.current_weight,
                3
            ),

            "total_hours": state.effective_hours,

            "planned_hours": total_planned_hours,

            "is_defect": state.is_defect,

            "defect_type": state.defect_type,

            "steel_type": steel_type,

            "final_p15_50": round(last_p, 3),

            "final_b2500": round(last_b, 3),

            "final_p10_400": round(
                state.p10_400_history[-1],
                2
            ) if state.p10_400_history else None,

            "final_b5000": round(
                state.b5000_history[-1],
                3
            ) if state.b5000_history else None,

            "final_b10000": round(
                state.b10000_history[-1],
                3
            ) if state.b10000_history else None,

            "final_anisotropy": round(
                state.anisotropy_history[-1],
                1
            ) if state.anisotropy_history else None,

            "process_deviation": round(
                state.process_deviation,
                4
            ),

            "annealing_quality": round(
                state.annealing_quality,
                1
            ),

            "annealing_type": (
                state.current_annealing_type
            ),

            "actual_temp": round(
                state.current_temp,
                1
            ),

            "actual_h2": round(
                state.current_h2,
                4
            ),
        })

        return self.log

    # =====================================================
    # ВСПОМОГАТЕЛЬНЫЕ
    # =====================================================

    def _resolve_annealing_type(self, step_type):

        if step_type == 'high_temp_annealing':
            return 'high_temp'

        if step_type == 'recrystallization_annealing':
            return 'recrystallization'

        if step_type == 'decarburizing':
            return 'decarburizing'

        return 'recrystallization'

    def _get_substage(self, step_type: str):

        mapping = {

            "incoming":
                "Поступление подката",

            "preparation":
                "Подготовка рулона",

            "normalization":
                "Нормализация",

            "pickling":
                "Травление",

            "cold_rolling":
                "Холодная прокатка",

            "skin_pass":
                "Дрессировка",

            "recrystallization_annealing":
                "Рекристаллизационный отжиг",

            "high_temp_annealing":
                "Высокотемпературный отжиг",

            "coating":
                "Нанесение покрытия",

            "otk":
                "Контроль качества",
        }

        return mapping.get(
            step_type,
            step_type.replace('_', ' ').capitalize()
        )

    def _calculate_temperature(
        self,
        step_type,
        base_temp
    ):

        if step_type == "high_temp_annealing":
            return random.uniform(930, 1080)

        if step_type == "recrystallization_annealing":
            return random.uniform(780, 920)

        if step_type == "normalization":
            return random.uniform(980, 1080)

        if step_type == "cold_rolling":
            return random.uniform(35, 85)

        if step_type == "skin_pass":
            return random.uniform(25, 70)

        if step_type == "pickling":
            return random.uniform(55, 90)

        if step_type == "coating":
            return random.uniform(180, 320)

        if step_type == "otk":
            return random.uniform(18, 28)

        return base_temp + random.uniform(-10, 10)

    def _get_defect_type(
        self,
        step_type,
        temp,
        h2,
        si,
        steel_type
    ):

        ngo_defects = {
            "cold_rolling": [
                "Разнотолщинность",
                "Царапины",
                "Вмятины",
            ],

            "coating": [
                "Неравномерность покрытия",
                "Отслоение покрытия",
            ],

            "recrystallization_annealing": [
                "Недожог",
                "Окисление поверхности",
            ],
        }

        go_defects = {
            "high_temp_annealing": [
                "Нарушение текстуры GO",
                "Крупное зерно",
                "Потеря ориентировки",
            ],

            "coating": [
                "Повреждение MgO",
                "Неравномерное покрытие",
            ],
        }

        defects_map = (
            go_defects
            if steel_type == "GO"
            else ngo_defects
        )

        return random.choice(
            defects_map.get(
                step_type,
                ["Локальный дефект поверхности"]
            )
        )

    # =====================================================
    # НОРМАЛЬНЫЙ ЧАС
    # =====================================================

    def _process_normal_hour(
        self,
        state: RollState,
        base_p: float,
        base_b: float,
        h2: float,
        step_type: str,
        annealing_type: str,
        si: float,
        thickness: float,
        steel_type: str
    ):

        # =========================================
        # ПОТЕРЯ МАССЫ
        # =========================================

        loss = random.uniform(
            0.00002,
            0.00025
        )

        state.current_weight = max(
            0.01,
            state.current_weight * (1 - loss)
        )

        model_error = random.uniform(
            0.992,
            1.008
        )

        # =========================================
        # ОТЖИГ
        # =========================================

        if step_type in [
            "recrystallization_annealing",
            "high_temp_annealing"
        ]:

            state.annealing_quality = (
                calculate_annealing_quality(
                    state.current_temp,
                    h2,
                    annealing_type
                )
            )

            state.annealing_quality = max(
                65.0,
                min(state.annealing_quality, 99.0)
            )

            p_value, b_value = (
                self.calculate_magnetic_properties(
                    base_p=base_p,
                    base_b=base_b,
                    quality=state.annealing_quality,
                    h2_percent=h2,
                    temp=state.current_temp,
                    annealing_type=annealing_type,
                    steel_type=steel_type
                )
            )

        else:

            p_value = (
                base_p
                * model_error
                * state.process_deviation
            )

            b_value = (
                base_b
                * model_error
                / state.process_deviation
            )

            state.annealing_quality = max(
                70.0,
                state.annealing_quality
                - random.uniform(0.02, 0.15)
            )

        # =========================================
        # ДОПОЛНИТЕЛЬНЫЕ ПАРАМЕТРЫ
        # =========================================

        p10_400_value = (
            p_value
            * random.uniform(5.4, 6.4)
        )

        b5000_value = (
            b_value
            * random.uniform(1.03, 1.08)
        )

        b10000_value = (
            b5000_value
            * random.uniform(1.04, 1.09)
        )

        if steel_type == "GO":

            anisotropy_value = random.uniform(
                1.5,
                5.0
            )

        else:

            anisotropy_value = random.uniform(
                3.0,
                8.5
            )

        # =========================================
        # СОХРАНЕНИЕ
        # =========================================

        state.p15_50_history.append(
            round(p_value, 3)
        )

        state.b2500_history.append(
            round(b_value, 3)
        )

        state.p10_400_history.append(
            round(p10_400_value, 2)
        )

        state.b5000_history.append(
            round(b5000_value, 3)
        )

        state.b10000_history.append(
            round(b10000_value, 3)
        )

        state.anisotropy_history.append(
            round(anisotropy_value, 1)
        )

        # =========================================
        # H2
        # =========================================

        state.current_h2 = (
            h2
            + random.uniform(-0.00005, 0.00008)
        )



tasks.py
# production/tasks.py

import time
import logging
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional

from celery import shared_task
from django.utils import timezone
from django.db import transaction
from django.core.cache import cache

from .models import (
    SimulationResult,
    Roll,
    SimulationSession,
    ProcessMode,
    Grade,
    Route,
    RouteStep,
)

from .simulation_engine import SimulationEngine
from .utils import verify_against_standard
from .services import get_optimal_route as get_optimal_route_service
from .models_math import predictor

from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# =========================================================
# GradeResult — структура данных для результата определения марки
# =========================================================
@dataclass
class GradeResult:
    """
    Результат определения марки стали.
    
    Attributes:
        grade: Название марки (например, "2412", "3408")
        gost_ok: Соответствует ли параметрам ГОСТ
        magnetic_ok: Соответствует ли магнитным требованиям
        grade_name: Альтернативное имя марки (для совместимости)
        steel_type: Тип стали (GO/NGO)
    """
    grade: str
    gost_ok: bool = False
    magnetic_ok: bool = False
    grade_name: Optional[str] = None
    steel_type: str = "NGO"


# =========================================================
# ОПРЕДЕЛЕНИЕ МАРКИ СТАЛИ
# =========================================================
def determine_grade(
    thickness: float,
    si: float,
    p_val: float,
    b_val: float,
    **kwargs
) -> GradeResult:
    
    print(">>> USING determine_grade FROM TASKS.PY")
    """
    Определение марки электротехнической стали по параметрам.
    
    Логика основана на требованиях ГОСТ 21427.2-83 и внутренних стандартах НЛМК.
    
    Параметры:
        thickness: Толщина рулона, мм
        si: Содержание кремния, %
        p_val: Магнитные потери P1.5/50, Вт/кг
        b_val: Магнитная индукция B2500, Тл
        
    Возвращает:
        GradeResult с определённой маркой и флагами соответствия
    """
    try:
        thickness = round(float(thickness or 0.35), 2)
        p = round(float(p_val or 2.5), 3)
        b = round(float(b_val or 1.7), 3)
        si = round(float(si or 3.0), 3)
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        return GradeResult(grade="2414", gost_ok=False)

    # Валидация диапазона параметров
    if not (0.20 <= thickness <= 2.00) or not (0.50 <= p <= 6.00) or \
       not (1.00 <= b <= 2.30) or not (0.50 <= si <= 4.50):
        return GradeResult(grade="2414", gost_ok=False)

    # Логика для наиболее распространённой толщины 0.35 мм (±0.03)
    if abs(thickness - 0.35) <= 0.03:
        if p <= 3.10 and b >= 1.82 and 2.90 <= si <= 3.40:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="M400-50A",
                grade_name="M400-50A",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )
        elif p <= 3.50 and b >= 1.78 and si >= 2.85:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2412",
                grade_name="2412",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )
        elif p <= 3.80 and b >= 1.72:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2413",
                grade_name="2413",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )
    
    # Толстые листы (≥0.40 мм)
    elif thickness >= 0.40:
        if p <= 3.65 and b >= 1.75 and si >= 2.80:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2413",
                grade_name="2413",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )
    
    # Тонкие листы (<0.32 мм)
    elif thickness < 0.32:
        if p <= 2.40 and b >= 1.85 and si >= 3.0:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2412",
                grade_name="2412",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )

    # Fallback — марка присваивается, но ГОСТ не проходит
    fallback_grade = "2414" if p > 3.8 or b < 1.65 else "2413"
    return GradeResult(
        grade=fallback_grade,
        grade_name=fallback_grade,
        gost_ok=False,
        magnetic_ok=False,
        steel_type="NGO"
    )


# =========================================================
# ВСПОМОГАТЕЛЬНЫЕ ФУНКЦИИ ДЛЯ ИНТЕРАКТИВНОЙ СИМУЛЯЦИИ
# =========================================================

def _update_interactive_progress(
    session_id: str,
    status: str = 'running',
    progress: float = 0.0,
    current_step: Optional[str] = None,
    steps_total: int = 0,
    steps_done: int = 0,
    result: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    error: Optional[str] = None
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Обновление прогресса интерактивной симуляции в Redis cache.
    
    Параметры:
        session_id: Уникальный идентификатор сессии
        status: Текущий статус выполнения
        progress: Процент выполнения (0-100)
        current_step: Название текущего этапа
        steps_total: Общее количество шагов
        steps_done: Количество выполненных шагов
        result: Результат симуляции (при завершении)
        error: Сообщение об ошибке (при сбое)
        
    Возвращает:
        Обновлённые данные прогресса
    """
    cache_key = f'sim_interactive_{session_id}'
    current_data = cache.get(cache_key) or {}
    
    updated_data = {
        **current_data,
        'status': status,
        'progress': progress,
        'current_step': current_step,
        'steps_total': steps_total,
        'steps_done': steps_done,
        'updated_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),
    }
    
    if result is not None:
        updated_data['result'] = result
    if error is not None:
        updated_data['error'] = error
        updated_data['status'] = 'failed'
    
    # TTL: 1 час
    cache.set(cache_key, updated_data, timeout=3600)
    return updated_data


def _run_interactive_single_roll(
    roll_id: int,
    mode_id: int,
    session_id: str
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Выполнение симуляции одного рулона с пошаговым обновлением прогресса.
    
    Параметры:
        roll_id: ID рулона для симуляции
        mode_id: ID режима термической обработки
        session_id: Уникальный идентификатор сессии
        
    Возвращает:
        Словарь с результатами симуляции
    """
    # Загрузка данных
    roll = Roll.objects.select_related('order', 'target_grade').get(id=roll_id)
    mode = ProcessMode.objects.get(id=mode_id)
    
    # 1. Инициализация (5%)
    _update_interactive_progress(
        session_id=session_id,
        status='initializing',
        progress=5,
        current_step='Загрузка данных рулона',
        steps_total=10,
        steps_done=1
    )
    
    # 2. Расчёт маршрута (15%)
    _update_interactive_progress(
        session_id=session_id,
        status='calculating_route',
        progress=15,
        current_step='Расчёт технологического маршрута',
        steps_total=10,
        steps_done=2
    )
    
    route_info = get_optimal_route_service(roll)
    route_id = route_info.get('route_id', 'R2') if isinstance(route_info, dict) else route_info
    route_obj = Route.objects.filter(name=route_id).first()
    route_steps = list(
        RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by('order')
    ) if route_obj else []
    
    # 3. Предварительный прогноз (25%)
    _update_interactive_progress(
        session_id=session_id,
        status='predicting',
        progress=25,
        current_step='Предварительный прогноз свойств',
        steps_total=10,
        steps_done=3
    )
    
    prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
        thickness=roll.thickness,
        si=roll.si_content,
        c=getattr(roll, 'c_content', 0.005),
        temp=float(mode.temperature),
        h2=getattr(roll, 'h2_content', 0.0005),
        n2=getattr(roll, 'n2_content', 0.006),
        weight=roll.weight,
        annealing_type='recrystallization'
    )
    
    # 4. Запуск симуляции (40%)
    _update_interactive_progress(
        session_id=session_id,
        status='simulating',
        progress=40,
        current_step='Запуск имитационной модели',
        steps_total=10,
        steps_done=4
    )
    
    engine = SimulationEngine(roll=roll)
    
    # Локальные переменные для отслеживания состояния
    final_weight = roll.weight
    has_defect = False
    defect_reason = ""
    log_items = []
    
    # Оценка общего количества шагов для прогресс-бара
    total_steps = len(route_steps) * 4
    
    # Почасовая симуляция по этапам маршрута
    for route_step in route_steps:
        if has_defect:
            break
            
        stage_name = route_step.get_step_type_display() or route_step.step_type
        duration = max(1, int(getattr(route_step, "planned_duration", 4) or 4))
        
        for _ in range(duration):
            if has_defect:
                break
                
            # Выполнение одного часа симуляции
            engine.hour += 1
            current_temp = engine.calculate_temperature(route_step)
            annealing_quality = engine.calculate_annealing_quality(
                temp=current_temp,
                h2=engine.h2_content,
                annealing_type=engine.get_annealing_type(route_step.step_type)
            )
            
            # Обновление прогресса каждые 2 часа симуляции
            if engine.hour % 2 == 0:
                progress_pct = min(40 + (engine.hour / max(total_steps, 1)) * 40, 80)
                _update_interactive_progress(
                    session_id=session_id,
                    status='simulating',
                    progress=progress_pct,
                    current_step=f'{stage_name}: час {engine.hour}',
                    steps_total=total_steps,
                    steps_done=engine.hour
                )
                # Небольшая задержка для плавного обновления в UI
                time.sleep(0.1)
            
            # Проверка вероятности дефекта
            defect_prob = engine.defect_probability(current_temp, annealing_quality)
            if not has_defect and time.time() % 100 < defect_prob * 10:
                has_defect = True
                defect_reason = engine.get_defect_reason(route_step.step_type)
                break
            
            # Логирование текущего состояния
            log_items.append({
                'hour': engine.hour,
                'stage': stage_name,
                'temp': round(current_temp, 1),
                'quality': round(annealing_quality, 1),
                'weight': round(engine.current_weight, 3)
            })
    
    # 9. Финальный расчёт (85%)
    _update_interactive_progress(
        session_id=session_id,
        status='finalizing',
        progress=85,
        current_step='Финальный расчёт показателей',
        steps_total=10,
        steps_done=9
    )
    
    final_prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
        thickness=roll.thickness,
        si=roll.si_content,
        c=engine.c_content,
        temp=engine.temperature,
        h2=engine.h2_content,
        n2=engine.n2_content,
        weight=engine.current_weight,
        annealing_type='recrystallization'
    )
    
    final_weight = round(engine.current_weight, 2)
    yield_percent = round((final_weight / max(roll.weight, 0.01)) * 100, 2)
    
    # Определение марки по итоговым параметрам
    grade_result = determine_grade(
        thickness=roll.thickness,
        si=roll.si_content,
        p_val=final_prediction.get('p15_50', 2.5),
        b_val=final_prediction.get('b2500', 1.8)
    )
    
    predicted_grade = Grade.objects.filter(name=grade_result.grade).first()
    
    # Формирование результата
    result = {
        'roll_id': roll.id,
        'roll_number': roll.number,
        'final_weight': final_weight,
        'yield_percent': yield_percent,
        'has_defect': has_defect,
        'defect_reason': defect_reason if has_defect else None,
        'predicted_grade': grade_result.grade,
        'gost_ok': grade_result.gost_ok,
        'predicted': {
            'p15_50': final_prediction.get('p15_50'),
            'b2500': final_prediction.get('b2500'),
            'p10_400': final_prediction.get('p10_400'),
            'b5000': final_prediction.get('b5000'),
            'anisotropy': final_prediction.get('anisotropy'),
        },
        'route': route_id,
        'log_summary': {
            'total_hours': engine.hour,
            'steps_count': len(log_items),
            'avg_quality': round(
                sum(item['quality'] for item in log_items) / len(log_items), 1
            ) if log_items else 0
        }
    }
    
    # 10. Завершение (100%)
    _update_interactive_progress(
        session_id=session_id,
        status='completed',
        progress=100,
        current_step='Симуляция завершена',
        steps_total=10,
        steps_done=10,
        result=result
    )
    
    return result


# =========================================================
# ЗАДАЧА: ИНТЕРАКТИВНАЯ СИМУЛЯЦИЯ (Real-time)
# =========================================================

@shared_task(bind=True, max_retries=3, default_retry_delay=30)
def run_interactive_simulation(
    self,
    session_id: str,
    roll_id: int,
    mode_id: int
):
    """
    Интерактивная симуляция одного рулона с отслеживанием прогресса в реальном времени.
    
    Прогресс сохраняется в Redis cache по ключу: sim_interactive_{session_id}
    Клиент может опрашивать эндпоинт /api/simulation-progress/{session_id}/ 
    для получения актуального статуса.
    
    Параметры:
        session_id: Уникальный идентификатор сессии (для polling)
        roll_id: ID рулона для симуляции
        mode_id: ID режима термической обработки
    """
    try:
        # Инициализация: ожидание запуска
        _update_interactive_progress(
            session_id=session_id,
            status='queued',
            progress=0,
            current_step='Ожидание запуска',
            steps_total=10,
            steps_done=0
        )
        
        # Валидация входных данных
        if not Roll.objects.filter(id=roll_id).exists():
            raise ValueError(f"Рулон с id={roll_id} не найден")
        if not ProcessMode.objects.filter(id=mode_id).exists():
            raise ValueError(f"Режим с id={mode_id} не найден")
        
        # Запуск симуляции
        result = _run_interactive_single_roll(
            roll_id=roll_id,
            mode_id=mode_id,
            session_id=session_id
        )
        
        logger.info(f'[INTERACTIVE] Сессия {session_id}: рулон {roll_id} обработан')
        return {'success': True, 'session_id': session_id, 'result': result}
        
    except Roll.DoesNotExist:
        error_msg = f"Рулон {roll_id} не найден"
        logger.error(f'[INTERACTIVE ERROR] {error_msg}')
        _update_interactive_progress(
            session_id=session_id,
            status='failed',
            progress=0,
            current_step=None,
            error=error_msg
        )
        return {'success': False, 'error': error_msg}
        
    except ProcessMode.DoesNotExist:
        error_msg = f"Режим {mode_id} не найден"
        logger.error(f'[INTERACTIVE ERROR] {error_msg}')
        _update_interactive_progress(
            session_id=session_id,
            status='failed',
            progress=0,
            current_step=None,
            error=error_msg
        )
        return {'success': False, 'error': error_msg}
        
    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"Ошибка симуляции: {str(e)}"
        logger.error(f'[INTERACTIVE CRITICAL] Сессия {session_id}: {error_msg}', exc_info=True)
        _update_interactive_progress(
            session_id=session_id,
            status='failed',
            progress=0,
            current_step=None,
            error=error_msg
        )
        # Повторная попытка через 30 секунд
        raise self.retry(exc=e, countdown=30)


# =========================================================
# ЗАДАЧА: ПАКЕТНАЯ СИМУЛЯЦИЯ (Производственная очередь)
# =========================================================

@shared_task(bind=True, max_retries=3, default_retry_delay=60)
def run_production_simulation(self, session_id):
    """
    Пакетная обработка рулонов в рамках сессии симуляции.
    
    Обрабатывает все рулоны, привязанные к сессии, с обновлением их статуса
    и созданием записей SimulationResult. Поддерживает retry при временных ошибках.
    
    Параметры:
        session_id: ID сессии симуляции из таблицы SimulationSession
    """
    session = None

    try:
        # Загрузка сессии
        session = SimulationSession.objects.get(id=session_id)
        session.status = 'running'
        session.start_time = timezone.now()
        session.save(update_fields=['status', 'start_time'])

        # Получение очереди рулонов
        rolls = Roll.objects.filter(
            session=session,
            status__in=['В очереди', 'В обработке (пакет)']
        ).select_related('target_grade', 'order')

        total_rolls = rolls.count()

        if total_rolls == 0:
            session.status = 'completed'
            session.end_time = timezone.now()
            session.notes = 'Нет рулонов для обработки'
            session.save()
            return 'Нет рулонов'

        session.total_rolls = total_rolls
        session.processed_rolls = 0
        session.save(update_fields=['total_rolls', 'processed_rolls'])

        logger.info(f'[SESSION {session_id}] Запуск обработки {total_rolls} рулонов')

        processed = 0
        default_mode = ProcessMode.objects.first()

        # Обработка каждого рулона
        for idx, roll in enumerate(rolls, start=1):
            try:
                with transaction.atomic():
                    roll.refresh_from_db()

                    if roll.session != session:
                        continue

                    # Блокировка рулона
                    roll.status = 'На проверке'
                    roll.save(update_fields=['status'])

                    # Определение маршрута
                    route_data = get_optimal_route_service(roll)
                    route_id = (
                        route_data.get('route_id') 
                        if isinstance(route_data, dict) 
                        else route_data
                    )
                    route = (
                        Route.objects.filter(name=route_id).first() or 
                        Route.objects.filter(name='R2').first()
                    )

                    # Запуск симуляции
                    engine = SimulationEngine(roll=roll)
                    engine_result = engine.run(mode=default_mode, monte_carlo_runs=1)

                    # Создание записи результата
                    sim_result_obj = SimulationResult.objects.create(
                        roll=roll,
                        order=roll.order,
                        mode=default_mode,
                        route=route.name if route else 'R2',
                        final_weight=round(
                            engine_result.get('final_weight', roll.weight), 2
                        ),
                        is_defect=bool(
                            engine_result.get('defect') or 
                            engine_result.get('is_defect')
                        ),
                        defect_reason=engine_result.get('defect_reason', ''),
                         inspection_status='pending',
                        notes=f'Session {session_id}'
                    )

                    # Определение марки и проверка ГОСТ
                    actual_p = (
                        engine_result.get('actual_p15_50') or 
                        getattr(sim_result_obj, 'actual_p15_50', 3.2)
                    )
                    actual_b = (
                        engine_result.get('actual_b2500') or 
                        getattr(sim_result_obj, 'actual_b2500', 1.82)
                    )

                    grade_result = determine_grade(
                        thickness=roll.thickness or 0.35,
                        si=roll.si_content or 3.15,
                        p_val=actual_p,
                        b_val=actual_b
                    )

                    predicted_grade = Grade.objects.filter(
                        name=grade_result.grade
                    ).first()

                    # Обновление результата симуляции
                    sim_result_obj.predicted_grade = predicted_grade
                    sim_result_obj.gost_ok = grade_result.gost_ok
                    sim_result_obj.is_ok = (
                        grade_result.gost_ok and not sim_result_obj.is_defect
                    )
                    sim_result_obj.inspection_status = (
                        "approve" if sim_result_obj.is_ok else "reject"
                    )
                    sim_result_obj.save()

                    # Обновление рулона
                    roll.predicted_grade = predicted_grade
                    roll.status = 'Обработан' if sim_result_obj.is_ok else 'Брак'
                    roll.weight = round(
                        engine_result.get('final_weight', roll.weight), 2
                    )
                    roll.save(update_fields=['predicted_grade', 'status', 'weight'])

                # Обновление прогресса сессии
                processed += 1
                session.processed_rolls = processed
                session.save(update_fields=['processed_rolls'])

                logger.info(f'[{idx}/{total_rolls}] {roll.number} → {roll.status}')

                # Задержка для имитации реального времени обработки
                time.sleep(getattr(session, 'tick_interval', 0.4))

            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f'[ERROR] Рулон {roll.number}: {str(e)}', exc_info=True)
                try:
                    roll.status = 'Ошибка'
                    roll.simulation_notes = str(e)[:200]
                    roll.save(update_fields=['status', 'simulation_notes'])
                except:
                    pass
                continue

        # Финализация сессии
        session.status = 'completed'
        session.end_time = timezone.now()
        session.notes = f'Обработано {processed} из {total_rolls}'
        session.save()

        logger.info(f'[SESSION {session_id}] Завершена успешно')
        return f'Сессия {session_id}: {processed}/{total_rolls}'

    except SimulationSession.DoesNotExist:
        logger.error(f'Сессия {session_id} не найдена')
        return f'Сессия {session_id} не найдена'

    except Exception as e:
        if session:
            session.status = 'failed'
            session.end_time = timezone.now()
            session.notes = str(e)[:500]
            session.save()
        logger.critical(f'[CRITICAL] Сессия {session_id}: {str(e)}', exc_info=True)
        raise self.retry(exc=e, countdown=30)

utils.py
# production/verification.py

from django.db import transaction

from .models import (
    SimulationResult,
    SteelStandard,
)


# =========================================================
# SAFE FLOAT
# =========================================================

def _safe_float(value, default=0.0):
    try:
        if value is None:
            return float(default)
        return float(value)
    except Exception:
        return float(default)


# =========================================================
# GET GRADE NAME
# =========================================================

def _extract_grade_name(grade_obj):
    if not grade_obj:
        return None
    try:
        if hasattr(grade_obj, 'name'):
            value = str(grade_obj.name).strip()
        else:
            value = str(grade_obj).strip()
        return value if value else None
    except Exception:
        return None


# =========================================================
# FIND STANDARD (УЛУЧШЕНАЯ ВЕРСИЯ)
# =========================================================

def _find_standard(simulation_result, roll, steel_type):
    # 1. Из целевой марки рулона
    try:
        if roll and getattr(roll, 'target_grade', None):
            std = roll.target_grade.standard
            if std and getattr(std, 'is_active', True):
                return std
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 2. Из предсказанной марки
    try:
        predicted_grade = getattr(simulation_result, 'predicted_grade', None)
        if predicted_grade and hasattr(predicted_grade, 'standard'):
            std = predicted_grade.standard
            if std and getattr(std, 'is_active', True):
                return std
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 3. Поиск по имени марки
    grade_name = None
    try:
        predicted_grade = getattr(simulation_result, 'predicted_grade', None)
        grade_name = _extract_grade_name(predicted_grade)
    except Exception:
        pass

    if not grade_name and roll:
        try:
            grade_name = _extract_grade_name(roll.target_grade)
        except Exception:
            pass

    if grade_name:
        try:
            standard = SteelStandard.objects.filter(
                steel_type=steel_type,
                is_active=True,
                name__iexact=grade_name
            ).first()
            if standard:
                return standard
        except Exception:
            pass

    # ====================== FALLBACK ======================
    # 4. Любой активный стандарт для данного типа стали
    try:
        standard = SteelStandard.objects.filter(
            steel_type=steel_type,
            is_active=True
        ).first()
        if standard:
            return standard
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 5. Любой активный стандарт (самый последний fallback)
    try:
        standard = SteelStandard.objects.filter(is_active=True).first()
        if standard:
            return standard
    except Exception:
        pass

    return None


# =========================================================
# VERIFY AGAINST STANDARD (ГЛАВНАЯ ФУНКЦИЯ)
# =========================================================

def verify_against_standard(simulation_result):
    if simulation_result is None:
        return {
            'gost_ok': False,
            'is_defect': True,
            'reason': 'SimulationResult отсутствует',
        }

    roll = getattr(simulation_result, 'roll', None)

    # ====================== STEEL TYPE ======================
    steel_type = getattr(simulation_result, 'steel_type', None)
    if not steel_type and roll:
        steel_type = getattr(roll, 'steel_type', 'NGO')

    steel_type = str(steel_type or 'NGO').upper().strip()
    if steel_type not in ['GO', 'NGO']:
        steel_type = 'NGO'

    # ====================== PROPERTIES ======================
    actual_p15_50 = _safe_float(getattr(simulation_result, 'actual_p15_50', 0.0))
    actual_b2500 = _safe_float(getattr(simulation_result, 'actual_b2500', 0.0))
    actual_p10_400 = _safe_float(getattr(simulation_result, 'actual_p10_400', 0.0))
    actual_b5000 = _safe_float(getattr(simulation_result, 'actual_b5000', 0.0))
    actual_b10000 = _safe_float(getattr(simulation_result, 'actual_b10000', 0.0))
    actual_anisotropy = _safe_float(getattr(simulation_result, 'actual_anisotropy', 0.0))

    # ====================== CHEMISTRY & GEOMETRY ======================
    thickness = _safe_float(getattr(roll, 'thickness', 0.35), 0.35) if roll else 0.35
    si = _safe_float(getattr(roll, 'si_content', 3.0), 3.0) if roll else 3.0
    c = _safe_float(getattr(roll, 'c_content', 0.005), 0.005) if roll else 0.005

    thickness = max(0.01, thickness)
    si = max(0.0, si)
    c = max(0.0, c)

    # ====================== FIND STANDARD ======================
    standard = _find_standard(simulation_result, roll, steel_type)

    # ====================== DEFAULT FLAGS ======================
    p_ok = b_ok = p10_400_ok = b5000_ok = b10000_ok = anisotropy_ok = True
    chemistry_ok = thickness_ok = True
    gost_ok = False
    reason = 'Undefined'

    # ====================== ANOMALY CHECK ======================
    anomaly_reason = None
    if actual_p15_50 <= 0 or actual_p15_50 > 15:
        anomaly_reason = 'Аномальное значение P15/50'
    elif actual_b2500 <= 0 or actual_b2500 > 2.6:
        anomaly_reason = 'Аномальное значение B2500'
    elif thickness <= 0 or thickness > 2.0:
        anomaly_reason = 'Аномальная толщина'

    if anomaly_reason:
        try:
            with transaction.atomic():
                simulation_result.gost_ok = False
                simulation_result.is_defect = True
                simulation_result.is_ok = False
                simulation_result.defect_reason = anomaly_reason
                simulation_result.inspection_status = 'reject'
                simulation_result.save(update_fields=['gost_ok', 'is_defect', 'is_ok', 'defect_reason', 'inspection_status'])
        except Exception:
            pass
        return {'gost_ok': False, 'is_defect': True, 'reason': anomaly_reason}

    # ====================== STANDARD CHECK ======================
    if standard:
        # P15/50
        if standard.p15_50_max is not None:
            p_ok = actual_p15_50 <= float(standard.p15_50_max)

        # B2500
        if standard.b2500_min is not None:
            b_ok = actual_b2500 >= float(standard.b2500_min)

        # Дополнительные параметры
        if standard.p10_400_max is not None and actual_p10_400 > 0:
            p10_400_ok = actual_p10_400 <= float(standard.p10_400_max)
        if standard.b5000_min is not None and actual_b5000 > 0:
            b5000_ok = actual_b5000 >= float(standard.b5000_min)
        if standard.b10000_min is not None and actual_b10000 > 0:
            b10000_ok = actual_b10000 >= float(standard.b10000_min)
        if standard.anisotropy_max is not None and actual_anisotropy > 0:
            anisotropy_ok = actual_anisotropy <= float(standard.anisotropy_max)

        # Химия и геометрия
        if standard.si_min is not None and si < float(standard.si_min):
            chemistry_ok = False
        if standard.si_max is not None and si > float(standard.si_max):
            chemistry_ok = False
        if standard.c_max is not None and c > float(standard.c_max):
            chemistry_ok = False
        if standard.thickness_min is not None and thickness < float(standard.thickness_min):
            thickness_ok = False
        if standard.thickness_max is not None and thickness > float(standard.thickness_max):
            thickness_ok = False

        checks = [p_ok, b_ok, chemistry_ok, thickness_ok]

        if standard.p10_400_max is not None and actual_p10_400 > 0:
            checks.append(p10_400_ok)
        if standard.b5000_min is not None and actual_b5000 > 0:
            checks.append(b5000_ok)
        if standard.b10000_min is not None and actual_b10000 > 0:
            checks.append(b10000_ok)
        if standard.anisotropy_max is not None and actual_anisotropy > 0:
            checks.append(anisotropy_ok)

        gost_ok = all(checks)
        reason = f'Проверка по стандарту {standard.name}'

    else:
        # ====================== NO STANDARD FALLBACK ======================
        reason = 'Стандарт не найден → используются дефолтные лимиты'
        # Дефолтные разумные пределы
        p_ok = 0.8 <= actual_p15_50 <= 4.5
        b_ok = actual_b2500 >= 1.4
        gost_ok = p_ok and b_ok

    # ====================== SAVE RESULT ======================
    try:
        with transaction.atomic():
            simulation_result.gost_ok = gost_ok
            simulation_result.is_ok = gost_ok
            simulation_result.inspection_status = 'pending'

            if not gost_ok and standard:
                simulation_result.defect_reason = f'Несоответствие требованиям стандарта {standard.name}'
            elif not gost_ok:
                simulation_result.defect_reason = 'Несоответствие требованиям стандарта'
            else:
                simulation_result.defect_reason = ''

            simulation_result.save(update_fields=[
                 'gost_ok', 'is_defect', 'is_ok', 'inspection_status', 'defect_reason'
            ])
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'[VERIFY SAVE ERROR] {e}')

    # ====================== RETURN ======================
    return {
        'gost_ok': gost_ok,
        'is_defect': simulation_result.is_defect,
        'reason': reason,
        'p_ok': p_ok,
        'b_ok': b_ok,
        'p10_400_ok': p10_400_ok,
        'b5000_ok': b5000_ok,
        'b10000_ok': b10000_ok,
        'anisotropy_ok': anisotropy_ok,
        'chemistry_ok': chemistry_ok,
        'thickness_ok': thickness_ok,
        'steel_type': steel_type,
        'standard': standard.name if standard else None,
        'actual_p15_50': round(actual_p15_50, 3),
        'actual_b2500': round(actual_b2500, 3),
        'actual_p10_400': round(actual_p10_400, 3),
        'actual_b5000': round(actual_b5000, 3),
        'actual_b10000': round(actual_b10000, 3),
        'actual_anisotropy': round(actual_anisotropy, 3),
        'si': round(si, 3),
        'c': round(c, 5),
        'thickness': round(thickness, 3),
    }

def is_planning(user):
    return user.groups.filter(name='Planning').exists() or user.is_superuser

def is_qc(user):
    return user.groups.filter(name='QC').exists() or user.is_superuser

def is_management(user):
    return user.groups.filter(name='Management').exists() or user.is_superuser



from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional


@dataclass
class GradeResult:
    grade: str
    quality_class: Optional[str] = None
    gost_ok: bool = False
    magnetic_ok: bool = False
    grade_name: Optional[str] = None          # для совместимости
    steel_type: str = "NGO"
    matched: bool = False

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional


@dataclass
class GradeResult:
    grade: str
    gost_ok: bool = False
    magnetic_ok: bool = False
    grade_name: Optional[str] = None
    steel_type: str = "NGO"


def determine_grade(
    thickness: float,
    si: float,
    p_val: float,
    b_val: float,
    **kwargs
) -> GradeResult:
    
    print(">>> USING determine_grade FROM VIEWS.PY <<<")
    # =========================================================
    # SAFE CONVERT
    # =========================================================
    try:
        thickness = round(float(thickness or 0.35), 2)
        p = round(float(p_val or 2.5), 3)
        b = round(float(b_val or 1.7), 3)
        si = round(float(si or 3.0), 3)
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        return GradeResult(grade="2414", gost_ok=False, magnetic_ok=False)

    # =========================================================
    # ЗАЩИТА ОТ АНОМАЛИЙ
    # =========================================================
    if not (0.20 <= thickness <= 2.00) or not (0.50 <= p <= 6.00) or \
       not (1.00 <= b <= 2.30) or not (0.50 <= si <= 4.50):
        return GradeResult(grade="2414", gost_ok=False, magnetic_ok=False)

    # =========================================================
    # ОСНОВНАЯ ЛОГИКА ДЛЯ ЦДС НЛМК
    # =========================================================

    # 1. Самая распространённая группа 0.35 мм
    if abs(thickness - 0.35) <= 0.03:          # 0.32 – 0.38 мм
        if p <= 3.10 and b >= 1.82 and 2.90 <= si <= 3.40:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="M400-50A",
                grade_name="M400-50A",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )
        elif p <= 3.50 and b >= 1.78 and si >= 2.85:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2412",
                grade_name="2412",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )
        elif p <= 3.80 and b >= 1.72:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2413",
                grade_name="2413",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )

    # 2. Толстые листы (>0.40 мм)
    elif thickness >= 0.40:
        if p <= 3.65 and b >= 1.75 and si >= 2.80:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2413",
                grade_name="2413",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )

    # 3. Тонкие листы (<0.32 мм)
    elif thickness < 0.32:
        if p <= 2.40 and b >= 1.85 and si >= 3.0:
            return GradeResult(
                grade="2412",
                grade_name="2412",
                gost_ok=True,
                magnetic_ok=True,
                steel_type="NGO"
            )

    # =========================================================
    # FALLBACK — марка присваивается, но ГОСТ не проходит
    # =========================================================
    fallback_grade = "2414" if p > 3.8 or b < 1.65 else "2413"
    
    return GradeResult(
        grade=fallback_grade,
        grade_name=fallback_grade,
        gost_ok=False,           # Важно: здесь явно False
        magnetic_ok=False,
        steel_type="NGO"
    )


@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_planning)
def plan_view(request):
    rolls = Roll.objects.filter(status='В очереди').select_related(
        'target_grade',
        'predicted_grade',
        'session'
    )
    modes = ProcessMode.objects.all()
    orders = Order.objects.filter(is_active=True)

    # =====================================================================
    # ОТОБРАЖЕНИЕ РЕЗУЛЬТАТОВ
    # =====================================================================
    show_result = False
    last_single_roll = None
    simulation_result = None
    simulation_log = []
    final_grade = None          # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 2: ЕДИНЫЙ ИСТОЧНИК ИСТИНЫ (вместо assigned_grade)
    has_defect = False
    final_status = ""
    gost_ok = False

    # 1. Последняя одиночная симуляция (приоритет)
    last_single_session = SimulationSession.objects.filter(
        status='completed',
        total_rolls=1
    ).order_by('-end_time').first()

    if (
        last_single_session
        and last_single_session.end_time
        and (timezone.now() - last_single_session.end_time).total_seconds() < 1800
    ):
        show_result = True
        last_single_roll = Roll.objects.filter(
            session=last_single_session
        ).first()

        if last_single_roll:
            simulation_result = SimulationResult.objects.filter(
                roll=last_single_roll
            ).order_by('-simulation_time').first()

            if simulation_result:
                simulation_log = list(simulation_result.steps.all().order_by('hour')) if hasattr(simulation_result, 'steps') else []

    # =====================================================================
    # БАЗОВЫЙ КОНТЕКСТ
    # =====================================================================
    context = {
        'rolls': rolls,
        'modes': modes,
        'orders': orders,
        'show_result': show_result,
        'roll_source': 'db',
        'now': timezone.now(),
        'MAX_ROLLS_PER_SESSION': getattr(settings, 'MAX_ROLLS_PER_SESSION', 500),
        'MAX_ROLLS_IN_QUEUE': getattr(settings, 'MAX_ROLLS_IN_QUEUE', 2000),
        'last_single_roll': last_single_roll,
        'simulation_result': simulation_result,
        'simulation_log': simulation_log,
        'has_defect': has_defect,
        'final_status': final_status,
        'gost_ok': gost_ok,
        
        # Дефолтные значения для рендеринга шаблона
        'opt': {'p': None, 'b': None, 'yield': 0, 'time': 0, 'mode_name': '', 'p_clean': None, 'b_clean': None},
        'prediction': {'p10_400': None, 'b5000': None, 'b10000': None, 'anisotropy': None},
        'thickness': 0, 'si': 0, 'c': 0, 'h2': 0, 'n2': 0,
        'weight_initial': 0, 'weight_final': 0,
        'avg_annealing': 0, 'min_annealing': 0,
        'risk': 0,
        'total_steps': 0,               # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 1: Для таблицы "Шаг"
        'total_process_hours': 0.0,     # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 1: Реальное время цикла (~2.6 ч)
        'final_grade': None,            # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 2
        'assigned_grade': None,         # Оставлен для обратной совместимости с шаблоном
        'is_ok': False,
        'roll_label': 'Не выбран',
        'applied_route': None,
        'main_annealing_type': '',
        'actual_p15_50': 0, 'actual_b2500': 0,
        'monte_carlo_stats': None,
        'batch_results': [],
        'batch_session_id': None,
    }

    # =====================================================================
    # POST — ОБРАБОТКА ЗАПРОСОВ
    # =====================================================================
    if request.method == 'POST':
        # =================================================================
        # ПАКЕТНЫЙ РЕЖИМ
        # =================================================================
        if request.POST.get('batch_mode') == 'true':
            roll_ids = request.POST.getlist('roll_ids')
            if not roll_ids or len(roll_ids) < 2:
                context['error'] = "Для пакетного режима выберите минимум 2 рулона"
                return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
            
            max_limit = getattr(settings, 'MAX_ROLLS_PER_SESSION', 500)
            if len(roll_ids) > max_limit:
                context['error'] = f"Превышен лимит на сессию: {len(roll_ids)} > {max_limit}"
                return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
            
            try:
                with transaction.atomic():
                    session = SimulationSession.objects.create(
                        status='running',
                        tick_interval=0.4,
                        total_rolls=len(roll_ids),
                        processed_rolls=0,
                        notes=f"Пакетная обработка запущена пользователем {request.user.username}"
                    )
                    
                    updated_count = Roll.objects.filter(
                        id__in=roll_ids,
                        status='В очереди'
                    ).update(
                        session=session,
                        status='В обработке (пакет)'
                    )
                    
                    if updated_count != len(roll_ids):
                        raise Exception(f"Не удалось обновить все рулоны. Обновлено: {updated_count} из {len(roll_ids)}")
                    
                run_production_simulation.delay(session.id)
                messages.success(request, f" Пакетная симуляция запущена: {len(roll_ids)} рулонов.")
                return redirect('plan')
                
            except Exception as e:
                context['error'] = f"Ошибка запуска пакетной симуляции: {str(e)}"
                print(f"[BATCH ERROR] {e}")
                return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        # =================================================================
        # ОДИНОЧНЫЙ РЕЖИМ
        # =================================================================
        roll_source = request.POST.get('roll_source', 'db')
        mode_id = request.POST.get('mode_id')
        order_id = request.POST.get('order_id')
        
        monte_carlo_enabled = request.POST.get('monte_carlo') == 'on'
        
        try:
            monte_carlo_runs = int(request.POST.get('monte_carlo_runs', 30)) if monte_carlo_enabled else 1
        except (TypeError, ValueError):
            monte_carlo_runs = 1
            
        monte_carlo_runs = max(1, min(monte_carlo_runs, 100))
        
        context.update({
            'roll_source': roll_source,
            'selected_order_id': order_id,
            'selected_mode_id': mode_id
        })
        
        # =================================================================
        # ИНИЦИАЛИЗАЦИЯ
        # =================================================================
        thickness = 0.35
        si = 3.15
        c = 0.005
        weight = 18.5
        h2 = 0.0005
        n2 = 0.006
        
        roll_label = "Неизвестный рулон"
        roll_obj = None
        incoming_state = 'hot_rolled'
        
        # =================================================================
        # ПОЛУЧЕНИЕ ДАННЫХ
        # =================================================================
        try:
            if roll_source == 'manual':
                si = float(request.POST.get('manual_si') or 3.15)
                c = float(request.POST.get('manual_c') or 0.005)
                thickness = float(request.POST.get('manual_thickness') or 0.35)
                weight = float(request.POST.get('manual_weight') or 18.5)
                h2 = float(request.POST.get('manual_h2') or 0.0005)
                n2 = float(request.POST.get('manual_n2') or 0.006)
                roll_label = "Экспериментальный ввод"
            else:
                roll_id = request.POST.get('roll_id')
                if not roll_id:
                    context['error'] = "Необходимо выбрать ровно 1 рулон"
                    return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
                
                roll_obj = get_object_or_404(Roll, id=roll_id)
                
                si = float(roll_obj.si_content or 3.15)
                c = float(getattr(roll_obj, 'c_content', 0.005) or 0.005)
                thickness = float(roll_obj.thickness or 0.35)
                weight = float(roll_obj.weight or 18.5)
                h2 = float(getattr(roll_obj, 'h2_content', 0.0005) or 0.0005)
                n2 = float(getattr(roll_obj, 'n2_content', 0.006) or 0.006)
                
                roll_label = f"Рулон №{roll_obj.number}"
                context['selected_roll_id'] = roll_id
                incoming_state = getattr(roll_obj, 'incoming_state', 'hot_rolled')
                
        except (ValueError, TypeError, AttributeError) as e:
            print(f"[INPUT ERROR] {e}")
            context['error'] = "Ошибка: введены некорректные данные"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        # =================================================================
        # ВАЛИДАЦИЯ
        # =================================================================
        if not order_id:
            context['error'] = "Необходимо выбрать заказ"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        if not mode_id:
            context['error'] = "Необходимо выбрать режим"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        target_order = get_object_or_404(Order, id=order_id)
        selected_mode = get_object_or_404(ProcessMode, id=mode_id)
        base_temp = float(selected_mode.temperature or 820)
        
        if thickness <= 0 or thickness > 2.0:
            context['error'] = f"Недопустимая толщина: {thickness} мм"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        if weight <= 0:
            context['error'] = "Ошибка: масса рулона <= 0"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        if not (0.5 <= si <= 4.0):
            context['error'] = f"Si={si}% вне допустимого диапазона"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        # =================================================================
        # МАРШРУТ + ТИП ОТЖИГА
        # =================================================================
        route_info = get_optimal_route(roll_obj)
        
        if isinstance(route_info, tuple):
            route_id = route_info[0]
            route_description = route_info[1] if len(route_info) > 1 else "Маршрут не определён"
        else:
            route_id = route_info.get('route_id', 'R2') if isinstance(route_info, dict) else 'R2'
            route_description = route_info.get('description', 'Стандартный маршрут') if isinstance(route_info, dict) else 'Стандартный маршрут'
        
        route_obj = Route.objects.filter(name=route_id).first()
        route_steps = RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by('order') if route_obj else []
        
        applied_route = {
            "id": route_id,
            "description": route_description,
            "steps_count": len(route_steps),
            "steps": [step.get_step_type_display() for step in route_steps]
        }
        
        annealing_steps = [step for step in route_steps if step.step_type in ['recrystallization_annealing', 'high_temp_annealing']]
        main_annealing_type = 'high_temp' if annealing_steps and annealing_steps[0].step_type == 'high_temp_annealing' else 'recrystallization'
        
        # =================================================================
        # ПРЕДСКАЗАНИЕ
        # =================================================================
        try:
            prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
                thickness=thickness,
                si=si,
                c=c,
                temp=base_temp,
                h2=h2,
                n2=n2,
                weight=weight,
                annealing_type=main_annealing_type
            )
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[PREDICT ERROR] {e}")
            context['error'] = f"Ошибка модели прогнозирования: {str(e)}"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
            
        p_predicted = max(0.5, min(float(prediction.get('p15_50', 2.5)), 6.0))
        b_predicted = max(1.0, min(float(prediction.get('b2500', 1.80)), 2.1))
        
        # =================================================================
        # СИМУЛЯЦИЯ
        # =================================================================
        try:
            from production.simulation_engine import SimulationEngine
            engine = SimulationEngine(roll=roll_obj)
            result = engine.run(
                mode=selected_mode,
                monte_carlo_runs=monte_carlo_runs if monte_carlo_enabled else 1
            )
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[SimulationEngine ERROR] {e}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            context['error'] = f"Ошибка SimulationEngine: {str(e)}"
            return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
        
        # =================================================================
        # РЕЗУЛЬТАТЫ
        # =================================================================
        sim_result_obj = result.get('simulation_result')
        final_weight = round(float(result.get('final_weight', weight)), 2)
        
        has_defect = bool(
            result.get('defect') or 
            result.get('is_defect') or 
            (sim_result_obj.is_defect if sim_result_obj else False)
        )
        
        defect_reason = result.get('defect_reason') or getattr(sim_result_obj, 'defect_reason', "")
        log_items = result.get('log', [])
        
        actual_p15_50 = max(0.8, min(
            float(result.get("actual_p15_50") or 
                  getattr(sim_result_obj, 'actual_p15_50', p_predicted) or p_predicted),
            5.5
        ))
        
        actual_b2500 = max(1.0, min(
            float(result.get("actual_b2500") or 
                  getattr(sim_result_obj, 'actual_b2500', b_predicted) or b_predicted),
            2.1
        ))
        
        # ====================== ОПРЕДЕЛЕНИЕ МАРКИ И ГОСТ (НЕЗАВИСИМО ОТ has_defect) ======================
        grade_result = determine_grade(
            thickness=thickness,
            si=si,
            p_val=actual_p15_50,
            b_val=actual_b2500
        )

        print("\n===== DETERMINE GRADE DEBUG =====")
        print("thickness =", thickness)
        print("si =", si)
        print("p =", actual_p15_50)
        print("b =", actual_b2500)
        print("grade_result =", grade_result)
        print("grade =", getattr(grade_result, "grade", None))
        print("gost_ok =", getattr(grade_result, "gost_ok", None))
        print("=================================\n")
        
        # Безопасное извлечение данных из GradeResult
        if hasattr(grade_result, 'grade'):
            assigned_grade = grade_result.grade
            gost_ok = getattr(grade_result, 'gost_ok', False)
        else:
            assigned_grade = str(grade_result) if grade_result else None
            gost_ok = False
            
        predicted_grade_obj = Grade.objects.filter(name=assigned_grade).first() if assigned_grade else None
        final_grade = assigned_grade  # Для обратной совместимости с шаблоном
        
        # Статус для Группы Планирования (НИКОГДА НЕ СТАВИТ "БРАК")
        if gost_ok and not has_defect:
            final_status = "ГОДЕН"
        elif gost_ok and has_defect:
            final_status = "ТРЕБУЕТ ПРОВЕРКИ ОТК"
        else:
            final_status = "НЕ СООТВЕТСТВУЕТ ГОСТ"
            
        is_match = gost_ok # is_ok = соответствие ГОСТ
        
        # Обновление рулона
        if roll_obj:
            roll_obj.predicted_grade = predicted_grade_obj
            roll_obj.is_predicted = bool(predicted_grade_obj)
            # ИЗМЕНЕНО: Статус зависит от ГОСТ, а не от случайного флага дефекта
            roll_obj.status = "Обработан" if gost_ok else "Требует проверки"
            roll_obj.weight = final_weight
            roll_obj.save()
            
        # Аналитика
        annealing_qualities = []
        for item in log_items:
            if isinstance(item, dict):
                quality = item.get('annealing_quality')
            elif hasattr(item, 'annealing_quality'):
                quality = item.annealing_quality
            else:
                quality = None
                
            if quality is not None:
                annealing_qualities.append(float(quality))
                
        avg_annealing = round(sum(annealing_qualities) / len(annealing_qualities), 1) if annealing_qualities else 0.0
        
        # ====================== РАСЧЕТ ВРЕМЕНИ ЦИКЛА (ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 1) ======================
        total_steps = len(log_items)
        STEP_MINUTES = 4.5  # Длительность одного цифрового шага симуляции
        total_process_hours = round((total_steps * STEP_MINUTES) / 60, 1)
        
        # Синхронизация с объектом результата (чтобы нигде не было рассинхрона)
        if sim_result_obj:
            sim_result_obj.predicted_grade = predicted_grade_obj
            sim_result_obj.gost_ok = gost_ok
            sim_result_obj.is_ok = is_match
            sim_result_obj.save(update_fields=['predicted_grade', 'gost_ok', 'is_ok'])
            
        # =================================================================
        # ФИНАЛЬНЫЙ КОНТЕКСТ ДЛЯ ОДИНОЧНОЙ СИМУЛЯЦИИ
        # =================================================================
        context.update({
            'show_result': True,
            'roll_label': roll_label,
            'thickness': thickness,
            'si': si,
            'c': c,
            'h2': h2,
            'n2': n2,
            'weight_initial': weight,
            'weight_final': final_weight,
            'avg_annealing': avg_annealing,
            'min_annealing': min(annealing_qualities, default=0),
            'opt': {
                'p': p_predicted,
                'b': b_predicted,
                'time': selected_mode.duration,
                'mode_name': selected_mode.name,
                'yield': round((final_weight / weight) * 100, 2) if weight > 0 else 100.0,
                'p_clean': prediction.get('p15_50_clean'),
                'b_clean': prediction.get('b2500_clean')
            },
            'applied_route': applied_route,
            'simulation_log': log_items,
            'monte_carlo_stats': result.get('monte_carlo_stats') if monte_carlo_enabled else None,
            'is_ok': is_match,
            'gost_ok': gost_ok,
            'final_status': final_status,
            'has_defect': has_defect,
            'simulation_result': sim_result_obj,
            'final_grade': final_grade,           # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 2: ЕДИНАЯ ПЕРЕМЕННАЯ
            'assigned_grade': final_grade,        # ← Дублируем для безопасности старых тегов шаблона
            'prediction': prediction,
            'main_annealing_type': main_annealing_type,
            'actual_p15_50': actual_p15_50,
            'actual_b2500': actual_b2500,
            'risk': calculate_risk(0.02, avg_annealing) if avg_annealing else 2.5,
            'total_steps': total_steps,           # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 1: Кол-во шагов
            'total_process_hours': total_process_hours, # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ 1: Реальное время (~2.6 ч)
        })
        
    # =====================================================================
