    # ЗАГРУЗКА РЕЗУЛЬТАТОВ ПАКЕТНОЙ СЕССИИ (только если нет одиночной)
    # =====================================================================
    if not show_result:
        recent_batch_session = SimulationSession.objects.filter(
            status='completed',
            total_rolls__gte=2
        ).order_by('-end_time').first()
        
        batch_results = []
        batch_session_id = None
        
        if recent_batch_session and recent_batch_session.end_time:
            time_diff = (timezone.now() - recent_batch_session.end_time).total_seconds()
            if time_diff < 1800:  # увеличил до 30 минут
                batch_session_id = recent_batch_session.id
                
                session_rolls = Roll.objects.filter(
                    session=recent_batch_session
                ).select_related('target_grade', 'predicted_grade')
                
                for roll in session_rolls:
                    sim_res = SimulationResult.objects.filter(roll=roll).order_by('-simulation_time').first()
                    if not sim_res:
                        continue
                    
                    # === ИСПРАВЛЕННАЯ ЛОГИКА ОПРЕДЕЛЕНИЯ СТАТУСА ===
                    is_ok = bool(
                        sim_res.is_ok or 
                        sim_res.gost_ok or 
                        getattr(sim_res, 'inspection_status', '') == 'approve' or
                        roll.status in ['Обработан', 'ГОДЕН']
                    )
                    
                    final_status_batch = 'ГОДЕН' if is_ok else 'БРАК'
                    has_defect_flag = not is_ok
                    
                    assigned_grade_name = '—'
                    if roll.predicted_grade and hasattr(roll.predicted_grade, 'name'):
                        assigned_grade_name = roll.predicted_grade.name
                    elif sim_res.predicted_grade and hasattr(sim_res.predicted_grade, 'name'):
                        assigned_grade_name = sim_res.predicted_grade.name
                        
                    steps = sim_res.steps.all().order_by('hour') if hasattr(sim_res, 'steps') else []
                    
                    sim_log = []
                    for s in steps:
                        sim_log.append({
                            'hour': s.hour,
                            'stage': s.stage,
                            'temp': s.temperature,
                            'p15_50': s.p15_50,
                            'b2500': s.b2500,
                            'weight': s.weight_after,
                            'annealing_quality': s.annealing_quality,
                            'defect': s.is_defect,
                            'status': 'Брак' if s.is_defect else 'Норма'
                        })
                        
                    batch_results.append({
                        'roll_id': roll.id,
                        'roll_number': roll.number,
                        'assigned_grade': assigned_grade_name,
                        'final_status': final_status_batch,
                        'has_defect': has_defect_flag,
                        'defect_reason': sim_res.defect_reason or '',
                        'thickness': roll.thickness,
                        'si': roll.si_content,
                        'c': getattr(roll, 'c_content', 0.005),
                        'weight_initial': roll.weight,
                        'h2': getattr(roll, 'h2_content', 0.0005),
                        'n2': getattr(roll, 'n2_content', 0.006),
                        'p_predicted': sim_res.predicted_p15_50,
                        'b_predicted': sim_res.predicted_b2500,
                        'p10_400': getattr(sim_res, 'predicted_p10_400', None),
                        'b5000': getattr(sim_res, 'predicted_b5000', None),
                        'b10000': getattr(sim_res, 'predicted_b10000', None),
                        'anisotropy': getattr(sim_res, 'predicted_anisotropy', None),
                        'simulation_log': sim_log,
                        'weight_final': getattr(sim_res, 'final_weight', roll.weight),
                        'yield_percent': getattr(sim_res, 'yield_percent', 0),
                        'avg_annealing': getattr(sim_res, 'actual_annealing_quality', 0),
                        'risk': 2.5,
                        'is_ok': is_ok
                    })
                    
        context['batch_results'] = batch_results
        context['batch_session_id'] = batch_session_id
        
        print("\n====== PLAN VIEW ======")
        print("final_grade =", final_grade)
        print("gost_ok =", gost_ok)
        print("is_ok =", is_ok)
        print("has_defect =", has_defect)

        sim = context.get("simulation_result")
        if sim:
            print("simulation_result.gost_ok =", sim.gost_ok)
            print("simulation_result.is_ok =", sim.is_ok)
            print("simulation_result.defect_reason =", sim.defect_reason)

        print("=======================\n")

    return render(request, 'production/plan.html', context)
@login_required
def active_session_api(request):
    """Возвращает статус текущей/последней активной сессии для JS-мониторинга"""
    if not request.headers.get('X-Requested-With') == 'XMLHttpRequest':
        return JsonResponse({'session': {'status': 'idle'}})

    session = SimulationSession.objects.filter(
        status__in=['running', 'completed', 'failed']
    ).order_by('-start_time').first()

    if not session:
        return JsonResponse({'session': {'status': 'idle'}})

    rolls_data = []
    status_map = {
        'В очереди': 'Ожидание', 
        'В обработке (пакет)': 'В работе',
        'На проверке': 'На проверке', 
        'Обработан': 'Годен',
        'Брак': 'Брак', 
        'Ошибка': 'Ошибка'
    }
    
    for r in Roll.objects.filter(session=session).only('number', 'status'):
        rolls_data.append({
            'number': r.number, 
            'status': status_map.get(r.status, r.status)
        })

    return JsonResponse({
        'session': {
            'id': session.id,
            'status': session.status,
            'processed_rolls': session.processed_rolls,
            'total_rolls': session.total_rolls,
            'rolls': rolls_data
        }
    })

def quality_view(request):

    simulation_results = SimulationResult.objects.select_related(
        'roll', 
        'roll__grade'
    ).all().order_by('-created_at')

    defects = Defect.objects.select_related('roll').all().order_by('-created_at')

    return render(request, 'production/quality.html', {
        'results': simulation_results,
        'defects': defects,
    })


def dashboard_view(request):
    total = SimulationResult.objects.count()
    good = SimulationResult.objects.filter(gost_ok=True).count()
    
    yield_val = round((good / total * 100), 1) if total > 0 else 0
    
    context = {
        'total': total,
        'good': good,
        'bad': total - good,
        'yield': yield_val,
        'recent_results': SimulationResult.objects.select_related('roll').order_by('-created_at')[:5]
    }
    return render(request, 'production/ruk.html', context)


@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_qc)
def quality_control_view(request):
    """
    Полностью исправленная система ОТК.

    Возможности:
    - approve / reject
    - защита от None
    - синхронизация Roll и SimulationResult
    - корректное присвоение grade
    - ГОСТ / IEC verification
    - отсутствие дублирования дефектов
    - transaction-safe
    """

    # =====================================================
    # POST
    # =====================================================

    if request.method == "POST":

        result_id = (
            request.POST.get("result_id")
            or ""
        ).strip()

        status = (
            request.POST.get("status")
            or ""
        ).strip().lower()

        comment = (
            request.POST.get("comment")
            or ""
        ).strip()

        defect_type = (
            request.POST.get("defect_type")
            or ""
        ).strip()

        reason = (
            request.POST.get("reason")
            or "unknown"
        ).strip()

        # -------------------------------------------------
        # VALIDATION
        # -------------------------------------------------

        if not result_id:

            messages.error(
                request,
                "Не указан результат."
            )

            return redirect("quality")

        if status not in [
            "approve",
            "reject",
        ]:

            messages.error(
                request,
                "Некорректный статус ОТК."
            )

            return redirect("quality")

        try:

            with transaction.atomic():

                res = (
                    SimulationResult.objects
                    .select_for_update()
                    .select_related(
                        "roll",
                        "roll__order",
                        "roll__grade",
                        "roll__predicted_grade",
                        "roll__target_grade",
                        "predicted_grade",
                        "grade",
                    )
                    .get(id=result_id)
                )

                roll = getattr(
                    res,
                    "roll",
                    None
                )

                if not roll:

                    messages.error(
                        request,
                        "У SimulationResult отсутствует Roll."
                    )

                    return redirect("quality")

                # =================================================
                # VERIFY
                # =================================================

                verification = (
                    verify_against_standard(res)
                )

                gost_ok = verification.get(
                    "gost_ok",
                    False
                )

                actual_p = float(
                    getattr(
                        res,
                        "actual_p15_50",
                        0
                    ) or 0
                )

                actual_b = float(
                    getattr(
                        res,
                        "actual_b2500",
                        0
                    ) or 0
                )

                valid_properties = (
                    actual_p > 0
                    and actual_b > 0
                )

                # =================================================
                # UPDATE RESULT
                # =================================================

                res.inspection_status = status

                if hasattr(
                    res,
                    "inspector_comment"
                ):
                    res.inspector_comment = comment

                # =================================================
                # APPROVE
                # =================================================

                if status == "approve":

                    # ---------------------------------------------
                    # FINAL STATUS
                    # ---------------------------------------------

                    res.is_defect = False

                    res.is_ok = (
                        gost_ok
                        and valid_properties
                    )

                    res.gost_ok = gost_ok

                    res.defect_type = None
                    res.defect_reason = None

                    # ---------------------------------------------
                    # FORCE REJECT IF NOT GOST OK
                    # ---------------------------------------------

                    if not gost_ok:

                        res.is_defect = True
                        res.is_ok = False
                        res.inspection_status = "reject"

                        messages.warning(
                            request,
                            (
                                "Результат не прошёл "
                                "проверку стандарта."
                            )
                        )

                    # ---------------------------------------------
                    # UPDATE ROLL
                    # ---------------------------------------------

                    if res.is_ok:

                        roll.status = "Обработан"

                        if hasattr(
                            roll,
                            "is_certified"
                        ):
                            roll.is_certified = True

                        if hasattr(
                            roll,
                            "certified_at"
                        ):
                            roll.certified_at = (
                                timezone.now()
                            )

                        # -----------------------------------------
                        # GRADE
                        # -----------------------------------------

                        grade_obj = None

                        # 1
                        if getattr(
                            roll,
                            "predicted_grade",
                            None
                        ):
                            grade_obj = (
                                roll.predicted_grade
                            )

                        # 2
                        elif getattr(
                            res,
                            "predicted_grade",
                            None
                        ):
                            grade_obj = (
                                res.predicted_grade
                            )

                        # 3 auto
                        else:

                            try:

                                grade_name, steel_type, gost_result, metadata = (
                                    determine_grade(
                                        thickness=float(
                                            getattr(
                                                roll,
                                                "thickness",
                                                0.35
                                            ) or 0.35
                                        ),

                                        si=float(
                                            getattr(
                                                roll,
                                                "si_content",
                                                3.0
                                            ) or 3.0
                                        ),

                                        p_val=actual_p,

                                        b_val=actual_b,
                                    )
                                )

                                if (
                                    grade_name
                                    and gost_result
                                ):

                                    grade_obj, _ = (
                                        Grade.objects.get_or_create(
                                            name=grade_name,
                                            defaults={
                                                "steel_type": steel_type
                                            }
                                        )
                                    )

                            except Exception as grade_error:

                                print(
                                    "[GRADE ERROR]",
                                    grade_error
                                )

                        # -----------------------------------------
                        # SAVE GRADE
                        # -----------------------------------------

                        if grade_obj:

                            if hasattr(
                                roll,
                                "grade"
                            ):
                                roll.grade = grade_obj

                            if hasattr(
                                roll,
                                "predicted_grade"
                            ):
                                roll.predicted_grade = grade_obj

                            res.grade = grade_obj

                    else:

                        roll.status = "Брак"

                        if hasattr(
                            roll,
                            "is_certified"
                        ):
                            roll.is_certified = False

                # =================================================
                # REJECT
                # =================================================

                else:

                    res.is_defect = True
                    res.is_ok = False
                    res.gost_ok = False

                    res.defect_type = (
                        defect_type
                        or "other"
                    )

                    if not res.defect_reason:

                        res.defect_reason = (
                            reason
                        )

                    # ---------------------------------------------
                    # ROLL
                    # ---------------------------------------------

                    roll.status = "Брак"

                    if hasattr(
                        roll,
                        "is_certified"
                    ):
                        roll.is_certified = False

                    if hasattr(
                        roll,
                        "grade"
                    ):
                        roll.grade = None

                    # ---------------------------------------------
                    # DEFECT CREATE
                    # ---------------------------------------------

                    existing_defect = (
                        Defect.objects.filter(
                            roll=roll,
                            defect_type=(
                                defect_type
                                or "other"
                            ),
                            reason=reason,
                        ).exists()
                    )

                    if not existing_defect:

                        Defect.objects.create(

                            roll=roll,

                            defect_type=(
                                defect_type
                                or "other"
                            ),

                            reason=reason,

                            weight_loss=0.0,

                            inspector_comment=comment,

                            created_by=(
                                request.user
                                if request.user.is_authenticated
                                else None
                            )
                        )

                # =================================================
                # SAVE
                # =================================================

                roll.save()

                res.save()

                # =================================================
                # COMPLETE ORDER
                # =================================================

                if (
                    status == "approve"
                    and getattr(
                        roll,
                        "order",
                        None
                    )
                    and res.is_ok
                ):

                    try:

                        check_order_completion(
                            roll.order
                        )

                    except Exception as completion_error:

                        print(
                            "[ORDER COMPLETION ERROR]",
                            completion_error
                        )

            # =====================================================
            # SUCCESS MESSAGE
            # =====================================================

            if (
                status == "approve"
                and res.is_ok
            ):

                messages.success(
                    request,
                    (
                        f"Рулон {roll.number} "
                        f"успешно принят ОТК."
                    )
                )

            else:

                messages.warning(
                    request,
                    (
                        f"Рулон {roll.number} "
                        f"забракован."
                    )
                )

            return redirect("quality")

        # =====================================================
        # GLOBAL ERROR
        # =====================================================

        except SimulationResult.DoesNotExist:

            messages.error(
                request,
                "SimulationResult не найден."
            )

            return redirect("quality")

        except Exception as e:

            print(
                "[QUALITY CONTROL ERROR]",
                e
            )

            messages.error(
                request,
                f"Ошибка ОТК: {str(e)}"
            )

            return redirect("quality")

    # =========================================================
    # GET
    # =========================================================

    results = (
        SimulationResult.objects.filter(

            Q(inspection_status="pending")
            |
            Q(inspection_status__isnull=True)
            |
            Q(inspection_status="")
        )
        .select_related(
            "roll",
            "roll__grade",
            "roll__predicted_grade",
            "roll__target_grade",
            "roll__order",
            "predicted_grade",
            "grade",
            "mode",
        )
        .order_by("-simulation_time")
    )

    # =========================================================
    # VERIFY
    # =========================================================

    for res in results:

        try:

            verification = (
                verify_against_standard(res)
            )

            res.is_gost_ok = verification.get(
                "gost_ok",
                False
            )

            res.standard_name = verification.get(
                "standard",
                "-"
            )

            res.p15_ok = verification.get(
                "p_ok",
                False
            )

            res.b2500_ok = verification.get(
                "b_ok",
                False
            )

            res.p10_400_ok = verification.get(
                "p10_400_ok",
                True
            )

            res.b5000_ok = verification.get(
                "b5000_ok",
                True
            )

            res.b10000_ok = verification.get(
                "b10000_ok",
                True
            )

            res.anisotropy_ok = verification.get(
                "anisotropy_ok",
                True
            )

            res.verify_reason = verification.get(
                "reason",
                ""
            )

            # ---------------------------------------------
            # DELTAS
            # ---------------------------------------------

            predicted_p = float(
                getattr(
                    res,
                    "predicted_p15_50",
                    0
                ) or 0
            )

            actual_p = float(
                getattr(
                    res,
                    "actual_p15_50",
                    0
                ) or 0
            )

            predicted_b = float(
                getattr(
                    res,
                    "predicted_b2500",
                    0
                ) or 0
            )

            actual_b = float(
                getattr(
                    res,
                    "actual_b2500",
                    0
                ) or 0
            )

            res.p_delta = round(
                actual_p - predicted_p,
                3
            )

            res.b_delta = round(
                actual_b - predicted_b,
                3
            )

        except Exception as verify_error:

            print(
                "[VERIFY ERROR]",
                f"SimulationResult #{res.id}",
                verify_error
            )

            res.is_gost_ok = False

            res.standard_name = "-"

            res.p15_ok = False
            res.b2500_ok = False
            res.p10_400_ok = False
            res.b5000_ok = False
            res.b10000_ok = False
            res.anisotropy_ok = False

            res.verify_reason = str(
                verify_error
            )

            res.p_delta = 0
            res.b_delta = 0

    # =========================================================
    # DEFECTS
    # =========================================================

    defects = (
        Defect.objects
        .select_related(
            "roll",
            "created_by",
        )
        .order_by("-created_at")[:20]
    )

    # =========================================================
    # CONTEXT
    # =========================================================

    context = {

        "title":
            "Контроль качества (ОТК)",

        "results":
            results,

        "defects":
            defects,

        "defect_types": (
            Defect.DEFECT_TYPES
            if hasattr(
                Defect,
                "DEFECT_TYPES"
            )
            else []
        ),

        "reasons": (
            Defect.REASONS
            if hasattr(
                Defect,
                "REASONS"
            )
            else []
        ),
    }
    
    context["defect_hints"] = {
        "surface": "Проверьте поверхность на наличие царапин, вмятин, окислов.",
        "magnetic": "Сверьте магнитные свойства с ГОСТ. Возможна ошибка отжига.",
        "geometry": "Измерьте толщину и ширину по всей длине рулона.",
        "edge": "Осмотрите кромки на предмет трещин и заусенцев.",
        "adhesion": "Проверьте на слипание витков после отжига.",
        "overheat": "Проверьте температуру печи и время выдержки.",
        "crack": "Критический дефект. Требуется списание партии.",
        "bad_texture": "Нарушение текстуры. Проверить режим вторичной рекристаллизации.",
        "decarburization_failure": "Недостаточное обезуглероживание. Проверить атмосферу.",
        "low_induction": "Низкая индукция. Возможна проблема с Si или температурой.",
        "high_core_loss": "Высокие потери. Проверить чистоту стали и охлаждение.",
        "other": "Укажите причину в комментарии."
    }
    return render(
        request,
        "production/quality.html",
        context,
    )
def check_order_completion(order):
    """
    Проверка завершения заказа по суммарной массе годной продукции.
    ИСПРАВЛЕНО:
    - защита от повторного закрытия заказа
    - защита от None в required_weight
    - защита от NULL notes
    - корректное обновление только активных заказов
    - безопасный расчёт веса
    """

    if not order:
        return False

    # Если заказ уже закрыт — ничего не делаем
    if getattr(order, 'is_completed', False):
        return True

    required_weight = float(getattr(order, 'required_weight', 0) or 0)

    if required_weight <= 0:
        return False

    # ====================== ПОДСЧЁТ ГОДНОЙ ПРОДУКЦИИ ======================

    ready_rolls = order.rolls.filter(
        models.Q(status='Обработан') |
        models.Q(is_certified=True)
    )

    total_ready_weight = (
        ready_rolls.aggregate(total=Sum('weight')).get('total') or 0.0
    )

    total_ready_weight = round(float(total_ready_weight), 2)

    # ====================== ПРОВЕРКА ВЫПОЛНЕНИЯ ======================

    is_completed_now = total_ready_weight >= required_weight

    if is_completed_now:

        order.is_completed = True
        order.is_active = False

        # Если есть поле completed_at
        if hasattr(order, 'completed_at'):
            from django.utils import timezone
            order.completed_at = timezone.now()

        # Если есть поле completion_percent
        if hasattr(order, 'completion_percent'):
            order.completion_percent = 100.0

        order.save()

        # ====================== ОБНОВЛЕНИЕ SIMULATION RESULT ======================

        simulation_results = SimulationResult.objects.filter(order=order)

        for sim in simulation_results:

            existing_notes = sim.notes or ""

            completion_note = "Заказ завершён по массе"

            if completion_note not in existing_notes:

                if existing_notes.strip():
                    sim.notes = f"{existing_notes} | {completion_note}"
                else:
                    sim.notes = completion_note

                sim.save(update_fields=['notes'])

        print(
            f"[ORDER COMPLETED] "
            f"Заказ {getattr(order, 'order_number', order.id)} завершён. "
            f"Готово: {total_ready_weight} / {required_weight} т"
        )

        return True

    # ====================== ОБНОВЛЕНИЕ ПРОЦЕНТА ВЫПОЛНЕНИЯ ======================

    if hasattr(order, 'completion_percent') and required_weight > 0:

        completion_percent = min(
            round((total_ready_weight / required_weight) * 100, 2),
            100.0
        )

        if order.completion_percent != completion_percent:
            order.completion_percent = completion_percent
            order.save(update_fields=['completion_percent'])

    return False

def register_view(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            user = form.save(commit=False)
            user.set_password(form.cleaned_data['password'])
            user.is_staff = True 
            user.save()
            
            group = form.cleaned_data['role']
            user.groups.add(group)
            
            login(request, user) 
            return redirect('redirect_by_role') 
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'registration/login.html', {'form': form})


def redirect_by_role(request):

    if not request.user.is_authenticated:
        return redirect('register') 
    
    if request.user.is_superuser:
        return redirect('/admin/')
    elif request.user.groups.filter(name='Planning').exists():
        return redirect('plan')
    elif request.user.groups.filter(name='QC').exists():
        return redirect('quality')
    elif request.user.groups.filter(name='Management').exists():
        return redirect('management')
    
    return redirect('register')

def calculate_route(roll):
    """
    Построение визуального маршрута обработки рулона.

    ИСПРАВЛЕНИЯ:
    - защита от None
    - защита от отсутствующего route_id
    - защита от пустых route_steps
    - исправлена ошибка len(queryset) внутри цикла
    - добавлены иконки по типам операций
    - корректный статус шагов
    - fallback при ошибках БД
    - поддержка current_step/current_stage у рулона
    """

    # ====================== FALLBACK БЕЗ РУЛОНА ======================

    if not roll:
        return [
            {
                'name': 'Неизвестный маршрут',
                'icon': '❓',
                'desc': '',
                'status': 'pending'
            }
        ]

    try:

        # ====================== ПОЛУЧЕНИЕ МАРШРУТА ======================

        route_info = get_optimal_route(roll) or {}

        if isinstance(route_info, dict):
            route_id = route_info.get('route_id')
        else:
            route_id = None

        if not route_id:
            route_id = 'R1'

        # ====================== ЗАГРУЗКА ROUTE ======================

        route_obj = (
            Route.objects
            .prefetch_related('route_steps')
            .filter(name=route_id)
            .first()
        )

        # ====================== FALLBACK ПРИ ОТСУТСТВИИ МАРШРУТА ======================

        if not route_obj:

            return [
                {
                    'name': 'АНО (Отжиг)',
                    'icon': '🔥',
                    'desc': 'Термообработка',
                    'status': 'active'
                },
                {
                    'name': 'АП (Покрытие)',
                    'icon': '🧪',
                    'desc': 'Нанесение покрытия',
                    'status': 'pending'
                }
            ]

        # ====================== ШАГИ МАРШРУТА ======================

        route_steps = list(
            RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by('order')
        ) if route_obj else []

        if not route_steps:

            return [
                {
                    'name': 'Маршрут пуст',
                    'icon': '⚠️',
                    'desc': 'Нет шагов обработки',
                    'status': 'pending'
                }
            ]

        # ====================== КАРТА ИКОНОК ======================

        icon_map = {
            'pickling': '🧪',
            'cold_rolling': '🌀',
            'annealing': '🔥',
            'recrystallization_annealing': '🔥',
            'high_temp_annealing': '🔥',
            'coating': '🎨',
            'inspection': '🔍',
            'slitting': '✂️',
            'packing': '📦',
            'quality_control': '✅',
            'tempering': '⚙️',
        }

        # ====================== ТЕКУЩИЙ ШАГ ======================

        current_step = getattr(roll, 'current_step', None)
        current_stage = getattr(roll, 'current_stage', None)

        steps = []

        total_steps = len(route_steps)

        for i, step in enumerate(route_steps):

            step_type = getattr(step, 'step_type', 'unknown')

            # ====================== СТАТУС ШАГА ======================

            if current_step is not None:

                if i < current_step:
                    status = 'complete'
                elif i == current_step:
                    status = 'active'
                else:
                    status = 'pending'

            elif current_stage:

                if current_stage == step_type:
                    status = 'active'
                elif len(steps) == 0:
                    status = 'complete'
                else:
                    status = 'pending'

            else:
                # fallback-логика

                if i == 0:
                    status = 'complete'
                elif i == total_steps - 1:
                    status = 'pending'
                else:
                    status = 'active'

            # ====================== НАЗВАНИЕ ШАГА ======================

            try:
                display_name = step.get_step_type_display()
            except Exception:
                display_name = step_type.replace('_', ' ').title()

            # ====================== ОПИСАНИЕ ======================

            description = getattr(step, 'description', '') or step_type

            # ====================== ДЛИТЕЛЬНОСТЬ ======================

            planned_duration = getattr(step, 'planned_duration', None)

            if planned_duration:
                description += f" ({planned_duration} ч)"

            # ====================== ИКОНКА ======================

            icon = icon_map.get(step_type, '🔄')

            # ====================== ДОБАВЛЕНИЕ ШАГА ======================

            steps.append({
                'name': display_name,
                'icon': icon,
                'desc': description,
                'status': status,
                'step_type': step_type,
                'order': i + 1
            })

        return steps

    except Exception as e:

        print(f"[calculate_route ERROR]: {e}")

        return [
            {
                'name': 'Ошибка маршрута',
                'icon': '❌',
                'desc': str(e),
                'status': 'pending'
            }
        ]

def generate_stochastic_events():
    events = []
    extra_time = 0.0
    risk_multiplier = 1.0

    possible_incidents = [
        {"name": "Сбой датчика натяжения полосы", "prob": 0.07, "delay": 0.3, "impact": "warning"},
        {"name": "Кратковременный перегрев печи АНО", "prob": 0.05, "delay": 0.6, "impact": "warning"},
        {"name": "Задержка подачи краном", "prob": 0.10, "delay": 0.2, "impact": "info"},
        {"name": "Обрыв полосы (критическая остановка)", "prob": 0.01, "delay": 3.5, "impact": "danger"},
    ]

    for incident in possible_incidents:
        if random.random() < incident['prob']:
            events.append({
                "msg": incident['name'],
                "delay": incident['delay'],
                "type": incident['impact']
            })
            extra_time += incident['delay']
            if incident['impact'] == 'danger':
                risk_multiplier = 2.5  

    return events, extra_time, risk_multiplier


def otk_page(request):
    """
    Страница ОТК — проверка ожидающих результатов симуляции по всем параметрам ГОСТ.
    Обновлено: поддержка расширенных магнитных характеристик (P10/400, B5000, B10000, анизотропия).
    """
    results = SimulationResult.objects.filter(
        inspection_status='pending'
    ).select_related('roll', 'roll__target_grade', 'mode').order_by('-simulation_time')

    for res in results:
        verification = verify_against_standard(res)
        
        if "error" not in verification:
            # Основные поля для шаблона
            res.is_gost_ok = verification.get('gost_ok', False)
            res.p_delta = verification.get('p_delta', 0)
            res.b_delta = verification.get('b_delta', 0)
            
            # Дополнительные поля для более детальной информации в шаблоне
            res.p15_ok = verification.get('p_ok', False)
            res.b2500_ok = verification.get('b_ok', False)
            res.p10_400_ok = verification.get('p10_400_ok', True)
            res.b5000_ok = verification.get('b5000_ok', True)
            res.b10000_ok = verification.get('b10000_ok', True)
            res.anisotropy_ok = verification.get('anisotropy_ok', True)
            
            # Можно сохранить полный результат проверки (удобно для отладки)
            res.verification_details = verification.get('all_checks', {})
        else:
            # Если эталон не найден
            res.is_gost_ok = False
            res.p_delta = 0
            res.b_delta = 0
            res.p15_ok = False
            res.b2500_ok = False
            res.p10_400_ok = False
            res.b5000_ok = False
            res.b10000_ok = False
            res.anisotropy_ok = False
            res.verification_details = {}

    return render(request, 'otk.html', {
        'results': results,
        'title': 'Проверка ОТК — Ожидающие результаты'
    })


@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_management)
@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_management)
@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_management)
def management_view(request):
    from django.db.models import Sum, Avg, Count, Q, F
    from django.db.models.functions import TruncDay
    import json
    from datetime import timedelta

    # =====================================================
    # 1. ЗАКАЗЫ И ПЛАН
    # =====================================================
    active_orders = Order.objects.filter(is_active=True).order_by('-created_at')
    total_required = active_orders.aggregate(total=Sum('required_weight'))['total'] or 0
    
    ready_rolls = Roll.objects.filter(
        Q(status__in=['Обработан', 'Готов', 'Completed', 'Certified', 'Ready']) | 
        Q(is_certified=True)
    )
    total_ready = ready_rolls.aggregate(total=Sum('weight'))['total'] or 0
    progress_percent = round((total_ready / total_required * 100), 1) if total_required > 0 else 0

    # =====================================================
    # 2. ОСНОВНЫЕ KPI (YIELD / DEFECT)
    # =====================================================
    results = SimulationResult.objects.select_related('roll', 'mode')
    total_simulations = results.count()
    
    approved_count = results.filter(inspection_status='approve').count()
    rejected_count = results.filter(inspection_status='reject').count()
    
    yield_percent = round(approved_count / total_simulations * 100, 1) if total_simulations > 0 else 0
    defect_percent = round(rejected_count / total_simulations * 100, 1) if total_simulations > 0 else 0

    # =====================================================
    # 3. РАСЧЕТ OEE
    # =====================================================
    availability = 94.5
    performance = 96.2
    quality = yield_percent
    oee = round((availability * performance * quality) / 10000, 1)

    # =====================================================
    # 4. АНАЛИТИКА МОДЕЛИ (ТОЧНОСТЬ)
    # =====================================================
    logs = ModelAccuracyLog.objects.all()
    
    accuracy_stats = logs.aggregate(
        avg_mae=Avg('mae_p'),
        avg_mape=Avg('mape_p')
    )
    
    avg_mae = round(accuracy_stats['avg_mae'] or 0, 3)
    avg_mape = round(accuracy_stats['avg_mape'] or 0, 2)   # ← ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ: всегда инициализируется

    # =====================================================
    # 5. ГЕНЕРАЦИЯ ОПЕРАТИВНЫХ СОБЫТИЙ
    # =====================================================
    events = []
    
    # Риск срыва заказа
    for order in active_orders[:3]:
        if getattr(order, 'get_progress', lambda: 0)() < 50 and order.created_at < timezone.now() - timedelta(days=2):
            events.append({
                'type': 'danger',
                'title': f'Риск срыва заказа {order.order_number}',
                'desc': f'Выполнено только {getattr(order, "get_progress", lambda: 0)()}%. Требуется вмешательство.'
            })

    # Рост брака
    recent_rejects = results.filter(
        inspection_status='reject', 
        simulation_time__gte=timezone.now() - timedelta(hours=4)
    ).count()
    if recent_rejects > 5:
        events.append({
            'type': 'warning',
            'title': 'Аномальный рост брака',
            'desc': f'За последние 4 часа забраковано {recent_rejects} рулонов. Проверьте печь.'
        })

    # Стабильность модели
    if avg_mape > 15:
        events.append({
            'type': 'info',
            'title': 'Снижение точности модели',
            'desc': f'MAPE превысил 15% ({avg_mape}%). Рекомендуется перекалибровка.'
        })
        
    if not events:
        events.append({
            'type': 'success',
            'title': 'Производство в штатном режиме',
            'desc': 'Отклонений от плана не выявлено.'
        })

    # =====================================================
    # 6. СТАТУС ОБОРУДОВАНИЯ
    # =====================================================
    equipment_status = [
        {'name': 'ЛПЦ-2 (Стан холодной прокатки)', 'status': 'online', 'load': '92%'},
        {'name': 'Печь отжига №4', 'status': 'warning', 'load': 'Перегрузка T°'},
        {'name': 'Агрегат нанесения покрытия', 'status': 'online', 'load': '88%'},
        {'name': 'Линия упаковки', 'status': 'maintenance', 'load': 'Плановый ремонт'},
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # 7. ГРАФИКИ
    # =====================================================
    daily_output = results.annotate(day=TruncDay('simulation_time')).values('day').annotate(count=Count('id')).order_by('day')[:14]
    chart_labels = [x['day'].strftime('%d.%m') for x in daily_output]
    chart_data = [x['count'] for x in daily_output]

    mape_daily = logs.annotate(day=TruncDay('timestamp')).values('day').annotate(avg_mape=Avg('mape_p')).order_by('day')[:30]
    mape_labels = [x['day'].strftime('%d.%m') for x in mape_daily]
    mape_values = [round(x['avg_mape'] or 0, 2) for x in mape_daily]

    # Дефекты
    top_defects = Defect.objects.values('defect_type').annotate(total=Count('id')).order_by('-total')[:5]
    defect_weight_loss = Defect.objects.aggregate(total=Sum('weight_loss'))['total'] or 0

    # Сценарии "Что если"
    scenarios = [
        {
            'name': 'Снижение T° отжига на 15°C',
            'impact_bad': 'Рост брака +2.4%',
            'impact_good': 'Экономия энергии -4%',
            'risk': f'Риск для заказа {active_orders.first().order_number if active_orders.exists() else "N/A"}',
            'recommendation': 'Не рекомендуется'
        },
        {
            'name': 'Ускорение линии на 5%',
            'impact_bad': 'Снижение качества покрытия',
            'impact_good': 'Выпуск +12 т/смена',
            'risk': 'Нет критических рисков',
            'recommendation': 'Допустимо при контроле ОТК'
        }
    ]

    # =====================================================
    # ФИНАЛЬНЫЙ CONTEXT
    # =====================================================
    context = {
        # KPI
        'total_ready': round(total_ready, 1),
        'total_required': round(total_required, 1),
        'progress_percent': progress_percent,
        'yield_percent': yield_percent,
        'defect_percent': defect_percent,
        
        # OEE
        'oee': oee,
        'availability': availability,
        'performance': performance,
        'quality_kpi': quality,

        # Events & Equipment
        'events': events,
        'equipment_status': equipment_status,

        # Analytics
        'avg_mae': avg_mae,
        'avg_mape': avg_mape,
        'top_defects': top_defects,
        'defect_weight_loss': round(defect_weight_loss, 2),
        
        # Charts
        'chart_labels_json': json.dumps(chart_labels),
        'chart_data_json': json.dumps(chart_data),
        'mape_labels_json': json.dumps(mape_labels),
        'mape_values_json': json.dumps(mape_values),

        # Orders & Scenarios
        'active_orders': active_orders,
        'scenarios': scenarios,
        
        'now': timezone.now()
    }

    return render(request, 'production/management.html', context)

@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_planning)
@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_planning)
def approve_plan(request, order_id):
    """
    Production-ready версия approve_plan.

    Исправления и улучшения:
    - transaction.atomic + select_for_update
    - надёжная работа с новым SimulationEngine
    - безопасное извлечение данных из результата
    - поддержка GradeResult (dataclass)
    - обновление большего количества полей SimulationResult
    - защита от None и дублирования
    - cleaner и понятный код
    """

    if request.method != "POST":
        return redirect("plan")

    try:

        with transaction.atomic():

            # =====================================================
            # ORDER
            # =====================================================
            order = get_object_or_404(Order, id=order_id)

            roll_id = request.POST.get("roll_id")
            mode_id = request.POST.get("mode_id")

            if not roll_id or not mode_id:
                messages.error(request, "Не выбран рулон или режим обработки.")
                return redirect("plan")

            # =====================================================
            # LOCK ROLL
            # =====================================================
            roll = (
                Roll.objects
                .select_for_update()
                .select_related(
                    "target_grade",
                    "predicted_grade",
                    "order"
                )
                .get(id=roll_id)
            )

            mode = get_object_or_404(ProcessMode, id=mode_id)

            # =====================================================
            # ЗАЩИТА ОТ ПОВТОРНОЙ ОБРАБОТКИ
            # =====================================================
            forbidden_statuses = [
                "В производстве",
                "Обработан",
                "Брак",
            ]

            if roll.status in forbidden_statuses:
                messages.warning(
                    request,
                    f"Рулон {roll.number} уже обработан."
                )
                return redirect("plan")

            # =====================================================
            # ROUTE
            # =====================================================
            route_info = get_optimal_route(roll)

            route_id = route_info.get("route_id", "R1") if isinstance(route_info, dict) else route_info

            route_obj = (
                Route.objects
                .prefetch_related("route_steps")
                .filter(name=route_id)
                .first()
            )

            route_steps = list(
                RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by("order")
            ) if route_obj else []

            # =====================================================
            # MAIN ANNEALING TYPE
            # =====================================================
            annealing_steps = [
                "recrystallization_annealing",
                "high_temp_annealing"
            ]

            main_annealing_step = next(
                (
                    step for step in route_steps
                    if step.step_type in annealing_steps
                ),
                None
            )

            main_annealing_type = (
                "high_temp"
                if (
                    main_annealing_step
                    and main_annealing_step.step_type == "high_temp_annealing"
                )
                else "recrystallization"
            )

            # =====================================================
            # PREDICTION (предварительный прогноз)
            # =====================================================
            prediction = predictor.predict_properties(
                thickness=roll.thickness,
                si=roll.si_content,
                c=getattr(roll, "c_content", 0.005),
                temp=float(mode.temperature),
                h2=getattr(roll, "h2_content", 0.0005),
                n2=getattr(roll, "n2_content", 0.006),
                weight=roll.weight,
                annealing_type=main_annealing_type,
            )

            # =====================================================
            # SIMULATION ENGINE — ОСНОВНАЯ СИМУЛЯЦИЯ
            # =====================================================
            engine = SimulationEngine(roll=roll)

            result = engine.run(
                mode=mode,
                monte_carlo_runs=1
            )

            # =====================================================
            # SAFE EXTRACTION ДАННЫХ ИЗ РЕЗУЛЬТАТА
            # =====================================================
            simulation_result = result.get("simulation_result")

            final_weight = round(
                float(result.get("final_weight", roll.weight)),
                2
            )

            has_defect = bool(
                result.get("defect") or
                result.get("is_defect") or
                False
            )

            defect_reason = result.get("defect_reason") or ""

            # Приоритет: данные из engine → prediction
            actual_p15_50 = float(
                result.get("actual_p15_50") or
                prediction.get("p15_50") or 2.5
            )

            actual_b2500 = float(
                result.get("actual_b2500") or
                prediction.get("b2500") or 1.8
            )

            # =====================================================
            # CLAMP VALUES (ограничение реалистичных значений)
            # =====================================================
            actual_p15_50 = max(0.8, min(actual_p15_50, 5.5))
            actual_b2500 = max(1.0, min(actual_b2500, 2.1))

            # =====================================================
            # DETERMINE GRADE
            # =====================================================
            predicted_grade_obj = None
            assigned_grade = None
            gost_ok = False

            if has_defect:
                assigned_grade = None
                gost_ok = False
            else:
                grade_result = determine_grade(
                    thickness=roll.thickness,
                    si=roll.si_content,
                    p_val=actual_p15_50,
                    b_val=actual_b2500,
                )

                # Поддержка dataclass GradeResult
                if hasattr(grade_result, 'grade'):
                    assigned_grade = grade_result.grade
                    gost_ok = getattr(grade_result, 'gost_ok', False)
                elif isinstance(grade_result, dict):
                    assigned_grade = grade_result.get('grade') or grade_result.get('grade_name')
                    gost_ok = grade_result.get('gost_ok', False)
                else:
                    assigned_grade = str(grade_result)
                    gost_ok = False

                predicted_grade_obj = (
                    Grade.objects
                    .filter(name=assigned_grade)
                    .first()
                )

            # =====================================================
            # FALLBACK CREATE RESULT (если engine не создал)
            # =====================================================
            if not simulation_result:
                simulation_result = SimulationResult.objects.create(
                    roll=roll,
                    order=order,
                    mode=mode,
                    predicted_grade=predicted_grade_obj,
                    route=route_id,

                    predicted_p15_50=prediction.get("p15_50"),
                    predicted_b2500=prediction.get("b2500"),
                    predicted_p10_400=prediction.get("p10_400"),
                    predicted_b5000=prediction.get("b5000"),
                    predicted_b10000=prediction.get("b10000"),
                    predicted_anisotropy=prediction.get("anisotropy"),

                    actual_p15_50=actual_p15_50,
                    actual_b2500=actual_b2500,

                    final_weight=final_weight,
                    yield_percent=round(
                        (final_weight / roll.weight) * 100, 2
                    ) if roll.weight > 0 else 100.0,

                    annealing_type=main_annealing_type,
                    is_ok=gost_ok,
                    gost_ok=gost_ok,
                    is_defect=has_defect,
                    defect_reason=defect_reason,
                    inspection_status="pending",

                    notes=(
                        f"План утверждён. "
                        f"Маршрут: {route_id}. "
                        f"Тип отжига: {main_annealing_type}."
                    )
                )

            # =====================================================
            # UPDATE ROLL
            # =====================================================
            roll.weight = final_weight

            if has_defect:
                roll.status = "Брак"
                roll.predicted_grade = None
            else:
                roll.status = "В производстве"
                if predicted_grade_obj:
                    roll.predicted_grade = predicted_grade_obj

            roll.save(
                update_fields=[
                    "weight",
                    "status",
                    "predicted_grade",
                ]
            )

            # =====================================================
            # USER MESSAGE
            # =====================================================
            if has_defect:
                messages.error(
                    request,
                    f"Для рулона {roll.number} обнаружен брак. {defect_reason}"
                )
            else:
                messages.success(
                    request,
                    f"План успешно утверждён для рулона {roll.number}. "
                    f"Присвоена марка: {assigned_grade}."
                )

            return redirect("plan")

    except Roll.DoesNotExist:
        messages.error(request, "Рулон не найден.")
        return redirect("plan")

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[approve_plan ERROR] {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        messages.error(
            request,
            f"Ошибка при утверждении плана: {str(e)}"
        )
        return redirect("plan")

def build_route_logic(roll):
    """
    Формирует маршрут обработки рулона в legacy-формате:
    [
        {"type": "annealing", "hours": 24},
        {"type": "coating", "hours": 3},
    ]

    ИСПРАВЛЕНИЯ:
    - защита от None
    - защита от отсутствующего route_id
    - защита от пустого маршрута
    - fallback при ошибках БД
    - нормализация step_type
    - защита от None в planned_duration
    - исключение отрицательных длительностей
    - prefetch_related для оптимизации
    - совместимость со старым кодом
    """

    # ====================== FALLBACK БЕЗ РУЛОНА ======================

    if not roll:
        return [
            {
                "type": "unknown",
                "hours": 0
            }
        ]

    try:

        # ====================== ПОЛУЧЕНИЕ МАРШРУТА ======================

        route_info = get_optimal_route(roll) or {}

        if isinstance(route_info, dict):
            route_id = route_info.get('route_id')
        else:
            route_id = None

        if not route_id:
            route_id = 'R1'

        # ====================== ЗАГРУЗКА ROUTE ======================

        route_obj = (
            Route.objects
            .prefetch_related('route_steps')
            .filter(name=route_id)
            .first()
        )

        # ====================== FALLBACK ПРИ ОТСУТСТВИИ ROUTE ======================

        if not route_obj:

            return [
                {"type": "annealing", "hours": 24},
                {"type": "coating", "hours": 3},
                {"type": "quality_control", "hours": 1}
            ]

        # ====================== ПОЛУЧЕНИЕ ШАГОВ ======================

        route_steps = list(
            RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by('order')
        ) if route_obj else []

        if not route_steps:

            return [
                {
                    "type": "empty_route",
                    "hours": 0
                }
            ]

        # ====================== НОРМАЛИЗАЦИЯ ТИПОВ ======================

        step_aliases = {
            'recrystallization_annealing': 'annealing',
            'high_temp_annealing': 'annealing',
            'final_annealing': 'annealing',
            'coating_line': 'coating',
            'inspection': 'quality_control',
            'quality': 'quality_control',
        }

        steps = []

        for step in route_steps:

            raw_step_type = getattr(step, 'step_type', 'unknown')

            # Нормализованный тип
            step_type = step_aliases.get(raw_step_type, raw_step_type)

            # ====================== ДЛИТЕЛЬНОСТЬ ======================

            planned_duration = getattr(step, 'planned_duration', 4)

            try:
                hours = float(planned_duration or 4)
            except (TypeError, ValueError):
                hours = 4

            # Защита от мусорных значений
            if hours < 0:
                hours = 0

            if hours > 240:
                hours = 240

            # ====================== ДОБАВЛЕНИЕ ШАГА ======================

            steps.append({
                "type": str(step_type),
                "hours": int(round(hours))
            })

        # ====================== ЕСЛИ ПОЧЕМУ-ТО ПУСТО ======================

        if not steps:

            return [
                {
                    "type": "unknown",
                    "hours": 0
                }
            ]

        return steps

    except Exception as e:

        print(f"[build_route_logic ERROR]: {e}")

        return [
            {
                "type": "route_error",
                "hours": 0
            }
        ]


def get_best_route(roll):
    """
    Возвращает список этапов оптимального маршрута рулона.

    ИСПРАВЛЕНИЯ:
    - защита от None
    - защита от отсутствующего route_id
    - fallback при ошибках
    - prefetch_related для оптимизации
    - защита от пустых шагов
    - поддержка get_steps_list()
    - fallback если get_steps_list() отсутствует
    - нормализация названий этапов
    - защита от битых step_type
    """

    # ====================== FALLBACK БЕЗ РУЛОНА ======================

    if not roll:
        return [
            "Стандартная обработка",
            "ОТК"
        ]

    try:

        # ====================== ПОЛУЧЕНИЕ МАРШРУТА ======================

        route_info = get_optimal_route(roll) or {}

        if isinstance(route_info, dict):
            route_id = route_info.get('route_id')
        else:
            route_id = None

        if not route_id:
            route_id = 'R1'

        # ====================== ЗАГРУЗКА ROUTE ======================

        route_obj = (
            Route.objects
            .prefetch_related('route_steps')
            .filter(name=route_id)
            .first()
        )

        # ====================== FALLBACK ПРИ ОТСУТСТВИИ ROUTE ======================

        if not route_obj:

            return [
                "Отжиг",
                "Покрытие",
                "Контроль качества"
            ]

        # ====================== ВАРИАНТ С get_steps_list ======================

        if hasattr(route_obj, 'get_steps_list'):

            try:

                steps = route_obj.get_steps_list()

                if isinstance(steps, list) and len(steps) > 0:
                    return [str(step) for step in steps if step]

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[get_steps_list ERROR]: {e}")

        # ====================== FALLBACK НА ROUTE STEP ======================

        route_steps = list(
            RouteStep.objects.filter(route=route_obj).order_by('order')
        ) if route_obj else []

        if not route_steps:

            return [
                "Маршрут пуст"
            ]

        # ====================== КРАСИВЫЕ НАЗВАНИЯ ======================

        display_map = {
            'pickling': 'Травление',
            'cold_rolling': 'Холодная прокатка',
            'recrystallization_annealing': 'Рекристаллизационный отжиг',
            'high_temp_annealing': 'Высокотемпературный отжиг',
            'annealing': 'Отжиг',
            'coating': 'Нанесение покрытия',
            'inspection': 'Контроль качества',
            'quality_control': 'Контроль качества',
            'slitting': 'Продольная резка',
            'packing': 'Упаковка',
            'tempering': 'Дрессировка',
        }

        result = []

        for step in route_steps:

            raw_step_type = getattr(step, 'step_type', None)

            if not raw_step_type:
                continue

            # Пытаемся получить display из Django choices
            try:
                display_name = step.get_step_type_display()

                if display_name:
                    result.append(str(display_name))
                    continue

            except Exception:
                pass

            # fallback через словарь
            result.append(
                display_map.get(
                    raw_step_type,
                    raw_step_type.replace('_', ' ').title()
                )
            )

        # ====================== ЕСЛИ ПОЧЕМУ-ТО ПУСТО ======================

        if not result:

            return [
                "Стандартная обработка",
                "ОТК"
            ]

        return result

    except Exception as e:

        print(f"[get_best_route ERROR]: {e}")

        return [
            "Ошибка маршрута",
            "ОТК"
        ]

def find_best_roll(order_params, available_rolls):
    best_roll = None
    min_diff = float('inf')

    for roll in available_rolls:
        diff = (order_params['thickness'] - roll.thickness)**2 + \
               (order_params['si'] - roll.si_content)**2
        
        if diff < min_diff:
            min_diff = diff
            best_roll = roll
            
    return best_roll


def export_orders_excel(request):
    start_date = request.GET.get('start_date')
    end_date = request.GET.get('end_date')

    logs = ModelAccuracyLog.objects.select_related('order', 'roll').order_by('-timestamp')

    if start_date:
        try:
            start = datetime.strptime(start_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
            logs = logs.filter(timestamp__date__gte=start.date())
        except ValueError:
            pass

    if end_date:
        try:
            end = datetime.strptime(end_date, '%Y-%m-%d')
            logs = logs.filter(timestamp__date__lte=end.date())
        except ValueError:
            pass

    wb = openpyxl.Workbook()
    ws = wb.active
    ws.title = "Отчет по качеству и точности модели"

    headers = [
        'Дата и время',
        '№ Заказа',
        '№ Рулона',
        'Марка стали',
        'Толщина (мм)',
        'Si (%)',
        'Прогноз P1.5/50',
        'Факт P1.5/50',
        'Прогноз B2500',
        'Факт B2500',
        'MAE (P)',
        'MAPE (P, %)',
        'Соответствует ГОСТ',
        'Вердикт',
    ]

    ws.append(headers)

    for log in logs:
        row = [
            log.timestamp.strftime('%d.%m.%Y %H:%M:%S'),
            log.order.order_number if log.order else '-',
            log.roll.number if log.roll else '-',
            getattr(log.roll, 'target_grade_name', '-') if log.roll else '-',
            getattr(log.roll, 'thickness', '-') if log.roll else '-',
            getattr(log.roll, 'si_content', '-') if log.roll else '-',
            log.predicted_p,
            log.actual_p,
            log.predicted_b,
            log.actual_b,
            log.mae_p if hasattr(log, 'mae_p') else '-',
            log.mape_p if hasattr(log, 'mape_p') else '-',
            'Да' if log.is_ok else 'Нет',
            'Соответствует' if log.is_ok else 'Брак / Отклонение'
        ]
        ws.append(row)

    column_widths = [18, 12, 15, 15, 12, 10, 15, 15, 15, 15, 12, 12, 15, 25]
    for i, width in enumerate(column_widths, 1):
        ws.column_dimensions[openpyxl.utils.get_column_letter(i)].width = width

    for cell in ws[1]:
        cell.font = openpyxl.styles.Font(bold=True)
        cell.fill = openpyxl.styles.PatternFill(start_color="DDDDDD", end_color="DDDDDD", fill_type="solid")

    response = HttpResponse(
        content_type='application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet'
    )
    filename = f"NLMK_Quality_Report_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M')}.xlsx"
    response['Content-Disposition'] = f'attachment; filename="{filename}"'

    wb.save(response)
    return response


def render_to_pdf(template_src, context_dict):
    template = get_template(template_src)
    html = template.render(context_dict)
    result = BytesIO()
    pdf = pisa.pisaDocument(BytesIO(html.encode("UTF-8")), result)
    
    if not pdf.err:
        return result.getvalue()
    return None


def export_roll_passport_pdf(request, roll_id):
    roll = get_object_or_404(Roll, id=roll_id)
    
    quality_log = ModelAccuracyLog.objects.filter(roll=roll).order_by('-timestamp').first()
    
    context = {
        'roll': roll,
        'log': quality_log,
        'today': timezone.now(),
        'company_name': 'ПАО НЛМК',
        'department': 'Цех динамной стали (ЦДС)',
    }
    
    pdf = render_to_pdf('pdf/passport_template.html', context)
    
    if pdf:
        response = HttpResponse(pdf, content_type='application/pdf')
        filename = f"Паспорт_качества_рулон_{roll.number}.pdf"
        response['Content-Disposition'] = f'inline; filename="{filename}"'
        return response
    else:
        return HttpResponse("Ошибка при генерации PDF-документа. Попробуйте позже.", status=500)
    

# views.py
def start_simulation_view(request):
    # Создаем сессию с интервалом 2 секунды на рулон
    session = SimulationSession.objects.create(tick_interval=2.0)
    
    # Запускаем фоновую задачу
    run_production_simulation.delay(session.id)
    
    return JsonResponse({"status": "started", "session_id": session.id})

@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_management) 
def sensitivity_view(request):
    """Анализ чувствительности параметров на магнитные свойства"""

    context = {
        'title': 'Анализ чувствительности параметров',
    }

    if request.method == 'POST':
        try:
            # Получаем параметры из формы
            si = float(request.POST.get('si', 3.15))
            temp = float(request.POST.get('temp', 850))
            h2 = float(request.POST.get('h2', 0.0005))
            thickness = float(request.POST.get('thickness', 0.35))
            annealing_type = request.POST.get('annealing_type', 'recrystallization')

            # Валидация базовых значений
            if not (0.1 <= thickness <= 2.0):
                raise ValueError("Недопустимая толщина")
            if not (0.5 <= si <= 4.0):
                raise ValueError("Недопустимое содержание кремния")
            if not (700 <= temp <= 1100):
                raise ValueError("Недопустимая температура отжига")

            # Генерируем диапазоны для анализа чувствительности
            si_values = [round(si - 0.35, 2), si, round(si + 0.35, 2)]
            temp_values = [temp - 50, temp - 25, temp, temp + 25, temp + 50]
            h2_values = [max(0.0001, round(h2 * 0.4, 6)), 
                        h2, 
                        round(h2 * 2.0, 6)]

            results = []

            for s in si_values:
                for t in temp_values:
                    for h in h2_values:
                        pred = predictor.predict_properties(
                            thickness=thickness,
                            si=s,
                            temp=t,
                            h2=h,
                            annealing_type=annealing_type
                        )
                        
                        results.append({
                            'si': round(s, 2),
                            'temp': round(t, 1),
                            'h2': round(h, 6),
                            'p15_50': pred.get('p15_50'),
                            'b2500': pred.get('b2500'),
                            'quality': pred.get('estimated_annealing_quality', pred.get('annealing_quality', '-'))
                        })

            # Сортируем результаты по P1.5/50 (для удобства)
            results.sort(key=lambda x: x['p15_50'])

            context.update({
                'show_result': True,
                'results': results,
                'base_si': si,
                'base_temp': temp,
                'base_h2': h2,
                'thickness': thickness,
                'annealing_type': annealing_type,
            })

            messages.success(request, f"Анализ чувствительности выполнен для {len(results)} комбинаций параметров.")

        except ValueError as ve:
            context['error'] = str(ve)
            messages.error(request, f"Ошибка ввода: {ve}")
        except Exception as e:
            context['error'] = "Произошла ошибка при выполнении анализа чувствительности."
            messages.error(request, f"Ошибка: {e}")
            print(f"[Sensitivity View Error]: {e}")

    return render(request, 'production/sensitivity.html', context)


@login_required
@user_passes_test(is_management)
def model_comparison_view(request):
    """Сравнение разных моделей прогнозирования магнитных свойств"""

    context = {
        'title': 'Сравнение моделей прогнозирования',
    }

    # Используем существующее поле actual_p (это и есть P1.5/50 в старой модели)
    logs = ModelAccuracyLog.objects.select_related('roll').filter(
        actual_p__isnull=False
    ).order_by('-timestamp')[:3000]   # увеличил лимит

    if logs.count() < 80:
        context['error'] = "Недостаточно данных для сравнения моделей. Необходимо минимум 80 записей с фактическими значениями P1.5/50."
        messages.warning(request, context['error'])
        return render(request, 'production/model_comparison.html', context)

    # Подготовка данных
    X = []
    y_p = []   # фактические значения P1.5/50

    for log in logs:
        roll = getattr(log, 'roll', None)
        if not roll:
            continue
        try:
            thickness = float(getattr(roll, 'thickness', 0.35))
            si = float(getattr(roll, 'si_content', 3.10))
            temp = 850.0

            X.append([thickness, si, temp])
            y_p.append(float(log.actual_p))          # ← Здесь было actual_p15_50
        except (TypeError, ValueError, AttributeError, TypeError):
            continue

    if len(X) < 80:
        context['error'] = f"Не удалось собрать достаточно данных (получено только {len(X)} записей)."
        messages.error(request, context['error'])
        return render(request, 'production/model_comparison.html', context)

    X = np.array(X)
    y_p = np.array(y_p)

    # 1. Простая формульная модель
    formula_predictions = []
    for x in X:
        pred = predictor.predict_properties(
            thickness=x[0],
            si=x[1],
            temp=x[2],
            annealing_type='recrystallization'
        )
        formula_predictions.append(pred.get('p15_50', pred.get('p', 0)))

    mape_formula = mean_absolute_percentage_error(y_p, formula_predictions) * 100

    # 2. Ridge Regression
    scaler = StandardScaler()
    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)

    model_ridge = Ridge(alpha=5.0, random_state=42)
    model_ridge.fit(X_scaled, y_p)
    y_pred_ridge = model_ridge.predict(X_scaled)
    mape_ridge = mean_absolute_percentage_error(y_p, y_pred_ridge) * 100

    # 3. Линейная регрессия
    model_lr = LinearRegression()
    model_lr.fit(X_scaled, y_p)
    y_pred_lr = model_lr.predict(X_scaled)
    mape_lr = mean_absolute_percentage_error(y_p, y_pred_lr) * 100

    # Формируем результат
    models_comparison = {
        'formula': {
            'name': 'Простая формульная модель',
            'mape': round(mape_formula, 2)
        },
        'ridge': {
            'name': 'Ridge Regression',
            'mape': round(mape_ridge, 2)
        },
        'linear': {
            'name': 'Линейная регрессия',
            'mape': round(mape_lr, 2)
        }
    }

    sorted_models_list = sorted(models_comparison.items(), key=lambda item: item[1]['mape'])

    context.update({
        'models': models_comparison,
        'sorted_models': sorted_models_list,
        'total_samples': len(X),
        'best_model': sorted_models_list[0][1],
    })

    return render(request, 'production/model_comparison.html', context)
